## 21:1-6 — verses 1-6 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Surat al-Anbiya'

This is a Meccan surah.

Al-Bukhari said: Muhammad ibn Bashshar told us, Ghundar told us, Shu'bah told us from Abu Ishaq: I heard Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid, from Abdullah, who said: Bani Isra'il, al-Kahf, Maryam, Ta Ha, and al-Anbiya' are among the oldest of the revelations, and they are among my old possessions.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

This is a warning from Allah, mighty and majestic, concerning the nearness of the Hour and its approach, and that people are in heedlessness of it, meaning: they do not act for it, nor do they prepare for it.

Al-Nasa'i said: Ahmad ibn Nasr told us, Hisham ibn Abd al-Malik Abu al-Walid al-Tayalisi told us, Abu Mu'awiyah told us, al-A'mash told us, from Abu Salih, from Abu Sa'id, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding {in heedlessness, turning away}, that he said: "In this world." And the Almighty said: {The command of Allah has come, so do not seek to hasten it} [al-Nahl: 1], and He [the Almighty] said: {The Hour has drawn near and the moon has split. And if they see a sign, they turn away and say: this is a continuous magic} [al-Qamar: 1, 2].

Al-Hafiz Ibn Asakir related in the biography of al-Hasan ibn Hani', Abu Nuwas the poet, that he said: The most poetic of people is the elder, the pure one, Abu al-Atahiyah, when he says:

"People are in their heedlessness, while the millstone of death is grinding..."

He was asked: From where did he take this? He said: From the saying of the Almighty: {The reckoning has drawn near for people, while they are in heedlessness, turning away}.

[He also related, in the biography of "Amir ibn Rabi'ah," through the route of Musa ibn Ubaydah al-Amidi, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, from his father, from Amir ibn Rabi'ah: that a man from the Arabs stayed with him, and Amir treated him honorably as a guest, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ spoke on his behalf. Then the man came to him and said: I have requested from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ a grant of a valley among the Arabs, and I wanted to grant you a portion of it, to be for you and your descendants after you. Amir said: I have no need of your grant. Today a surah was revealed that has distracted us from this world: {The reckoning has drawn near for people, while they are in heedlessness, turning away}.]

Then the Almighty informs that they do not pay heed to the revelation which Allah sent down upon His Messenger, the address being to the Quraysh and those disbelievers who resembled them. He said: {No mention comes to them anew from their Lord} meaning: newly revealed, {except that they listen to it while playing}, as Ibn Abbas said: What is the matter with you, that you ask the People of the Book about what is in their possession, when they have distorted it, altered it, added to it, and subtracted from it, while your Book is the most recent of the books from Allah, which you recite in its pure form, unmixed with corruption. Al-Bukhari related something similar to this.

His saying: {And those who did wrong conferred secretly among themselves} meaning: saying among themselves in secret, {is this not but a human being like yourselves?} meaning the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, considering it improbable that he could be a prophet, since he was a human being like them, so how could he be singled out for revelation apart from them? For this reason He said: {So will you approach magic while you can see?} meaning: will you then follow it, becoming like one who approaches magic while knowing that it is magic? Then the Almighty responded to them concerning what they had fabricated and invented of falsehood.

{He said: My Lord knows the word in the heaven and the earth} meaning: He who knows that, nothing hidden is concealed from Him, and He is the One who sent down this Qur'an, which contains the accounts of the first and the last peoples, which no one is able to produce the like of, except the One who knows the secret in the heavens and the earth.

His saying: {And He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing} meaning: [the All-Hearing] of your sayings, {the All-Knowing} of your states. In this is a threat and a warning to them.

His saying: {Nay, they say: confused dreams; nay, he invented it} this is a report about the stubborn obstinacy of the disbelievers and their deviance, their disagreement among themselves regarding how they describe the Qur'an, their confusion about it, and their straying from it. At times they call it magic, at times they call it poetry, at times they call it confused dreams, and at times they call it a fabrication, as He said: {Look how they strike for you comparisons, and so they have strayed, and cannot find a way} [al-Isra': 48, and al-Furqan: 9].

His saying: {So let him bring us a sign, just as the former ones were sent} meaning: they refer to the she-camel of Salih (peace be upon him), and the signs of Musa (peace be upon him) and Isa (peace be upon him). Allah the Almighty said: {And nothing prevented Us from sending signs except that the former peoples denied them. And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged her} [al-Isra': 59]. For this reason the Almighty said: {No city believed before them which We destroyed, so will these believe?} meaning: We did not give any of the cities to which messengers were sent a sign at the hands of their prophet such that they believed in it, rather they denied it, so We destroyed them for that. Will these people then believe in the signs if they were to see them, unlike those others? Certainly not. Rather, {Indeed, those upon whom the word of your Lord has been justified will not believe, even if every sign came to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96, 97].

All this is so, even though they witnessed, at the hands of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, of the dazzling signs, the decisive proofs, and the clear evidences, what was more manifest and more evident, more overwhelming, more decisive, and more overpowering than what was witnessed with any other of the prophets, may Allah's prayers and peace be upon them all.

Ibn Abi Hatim, may Allah have mercy on him, said: It was mentioned from Zayd ibn al-Hubab, Ibn Lahi'ah told us, al-Harith ibn Zayd al-Hadrami told us, from Ulayy ibn Rabah al-Lakhmi, who said: someone who was present with Ubadah ibn al-Samit told me that he said: We were in the mosque, and Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, may Allah be pleased with him, was with us, some of us reciting the Qur'an to others, when Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul came, bringing with him a cushion and a rug, and he set them down and reclined. He was handsome, eloquent, and argumentative, and he said: O Abu Bakr, tell Muhammad to bring us a sign just as the former peoples had: Musa (peace be upon him) came with the Tablets, Dawud (peace be upon him) came with the Zabur (Psalms), Salih (peace be upon him) came with the she-camel, and Isa (peace be upon him) came with the Gospel and with the Table. Abu Bakr, may Allah be pleased with him, wept. Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came out, and Abu Bakr said: Let us stand up before the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and seek his help against this hypocrite. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "No one should stand up for me; standing is only due to Allah, mighty and majestic." We said: O Messenger of Allah, we have suffered from this hypocrite. He said: "Gabriel said to me: Go out and announce the favors of Allah which He has bestowed upon you, and the distinction with which you have been distinguished. He gave me the glad tidings that I was sent to the red and the black, and He commanded me to warn the jinn, and He gave me His Book while I am unlettered, and He forgave my sin, what was before and what came after, and He mentioned my name in the call to prayer, and He supported me with the angels, and He gave me victory, and He placed terror before me, and He gave me al-Kawthar, and He made my basin one of the greatest basins on the Day of Resurrection, and He promised me the praised station while people are rushing forward with their heads raised, and He placed me at the head of the first group to emerge from among the people, and He will admit, through my intercession, seventy thousand of my nation into Paradise without reckoning, and He gave me authority and dominion, and He placed me in the highest chamber in Paradise, in the Gardens of Delight, so that there is no one above me except the angels who carry the Throne, and He made the spoils of war lawful for me, when they were not made lawful for anyone before us." This hadith is extremely gharib (singular/rare).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

سُورَةُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ

وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ.

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا غُنْدَر، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ عَنِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَالْكَهْفُ، وَمَرْيَمُ، وَطه، وَالْأَنْبِيَاءُ، هُنَّ مِنَ الْعِتَاقِ الْأُوَلِ، وَهُنَّ مِنْ تِلَادِي .

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

هَذَا تَنْبِيهٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَلَى اقْتِرَابِ السَّاعَةِ وَدُنُوِّهَا، وَأَنَّ النَّاسَ فِي غَفْلَةٍ عَنْهَا، أَيْ: لَا يَعْمَلُونَ لَهَا، وَلَا يَسْتَعِدُّونَ مِنْ أَجْلِهَا.

وَقَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ نَصْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ أَبُو الْوَلِيدِ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ ﴿فِي غَفْلَةٍ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ قَالَ: "فِي الدُّنْيَا" ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَتَى أَمْرُ اللَّهِ فَلا تَسْتَعْجِلُوهُ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ١] ، وَقَالَ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿اقْتَرَبَتِ السَّاعَةُ وَانْشَقَّ الْقَمَرُ * وَإِنْ يَرَوْا آيَةً يُعْرِضُوا وَيَقُولُوا سِحْرٌ مُسْتَمِرٌّ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ١، ٢]

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ هَانِئٍ أَبِي نُوَاس الشَّاعِرِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: أَشْعَرُ النَّاسِ الشَّيْخُ الطَّاهِرُ أَبُو الْعَتَاهِيَةِ حَيْثُ يَقُولُ:

النَّاس فِي غَفَلاتِهِمْ ... وَرَحا المِنيَّة تَطْحَنُ ...

فَقِيلَ لَهُ: مِنْ أَيْنَ أَخَذَ هَذَا؟ قَالَ : مِنْ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿اقْتَرَبَ لِلنَّاسِ حِسَابُهُمْ وَهُمْ فِي غَفْلَةٍ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ .

[وَرَوَى فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "عَامِرِ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ"، مِنْ طَرِيقِ مُوسَى بْنِ عُبَيْدَةَ الْآمِدِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ عَنِ أَبِيهِ، عن عامر ابن رَبِيعَةَ: أَنَّهُ نَزَلَ بِهِ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ، فَأَكْرَمَ عَامِرٌ مَثْوَاهُ، وَكَلَّمَ فِيهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَجَاءَهُ الرَّجُلُ فَقَالَ: إِنِّي اسْتَقْطَعْتُ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَادِيًا فِي الْعَرَبِ، وَقَدْ أَرَدْتُ أَنْ أقطعَ لَكَ مِنْهُ قِطْعَةً تَكُونُ لَكَ وَلِعَقِبِكَ مِنْ بَعْدِكَ. فَقَالَ عَامِرٌ: لَا حَاجَةَ لِي فِي قَطِيعَتِكَ، نَزَلَتِ الْيَوْمَ سُورَةٌ أَذْهَلَتْنَا عَنِ الدُّنْيَا: ﴿اقْتَرَبَ لِلنَّاسِ حِسَابُهُمْ وَهُمْ فِي غَفْلَةٍ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ ] .

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُصغون إِلَى الْوَحْيِ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ، وَالْخِطَابُ مَعَ قُرَيْشٍ وَمَنْ شَابَهَهُمْ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿مَا يَأْتِيهِمْ مِنْ ذِكْرٍ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ مُحْدَثٍ﴾ أَيْ: جَدِيدٌ إِنْزَالُهُ ﴿إِلا اسْتَمَعُوهُ وَهُمْ يَلْعَبُونَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: مَا لَكُمْ تَسْأَلُونَ أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ عَمَّا بِأَيْدِيهِمْ وَقَدْ حَرفوه وَبَدَّلُوهُ وَزَادُوا فِيهِ وَنَقَصُوا مِنْهُ، وَكِتَابُكُمْ أَحْدَثُ الْكُتُبِ بِاللَّهِ تَقْرَءُونَهُ مَحْضًا لَمْ يُشَبْ. وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ بِنَحْوِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَسَرُّوا النَّجْوَى الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا﴾ أَيْ: قَائِلِينَ فِيمَا بَيْنَهُمْ خفْيَةً ﴿هَلْ هَذَا إِلا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ﴾ يعنونَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، يَسْتَبْعِدُونَ كَوْنَهُ نَبِيًّا؛ لِأَنَّهُ بَشَرٌ مِثْلُهُمْ، فَكَيْفَ اخْتُصَّ بِالْوَحْيِ دُونَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَتَأْتُونَ السِّحْرَ وَأَنْتُمْ تُبْصِرُونَ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: أَفَتَتْبَعُونَهُ فَتَكُونُونَ كَمَنْ أَتَى السِّحْرَ وَهُوَ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ سِحْرٌ. فَقَالَ تَعَالَى مُجِيبًا لَهُمْ عَمَّا افْتَرَوْهُ وَاخْتَلَقُوهُ مِنَ الْكَذِبِ.

﴿قَالَ رَبِّي يَعْلَمُ الْقَوْلَ فِي السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي يَعْلَمُ ذَلِكَ، لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ خَافِيَةٌ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنَ الْمُشْتَمِلَ عَلَى خَبَرِ الْأَوَّلِينَ وَالْآخَرِينَ، الَّذِي لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ أَحَدٌ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ بمثله، إلا الذي يعلم السر في السموات وَالْأَرْضِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ [أَيِ: السَّمِيعُ] لِأَقْوَالِكُمْ، ﴿الْعَلِيم﴾ بِأَحْوَالِكُمْ. وَفِي هَذَا تَهْدِيدٌ لَهُمْ وَوَعِيدٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ قَالُوا أَضْغَاثُ أَحْلامٍ بَلِ افْتَرَاهُ﴾ هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ تَعَنُّتِ الْكُفَّارِ وَإِلْحَادِهِمْ، وَاخْتِلَافِهِمْ فِيمَا يَصِفُونَ بِهِ الْقُرْآنَ، وَحَيْرَتِهِمْ فِيهِ، وَضَلَالِهِمْ عَنْهُ. فَتَارَةً يَجْعَلُونَهُ سِحْرًا، وَتَارَةً يَجْعَلُونَهُ شِعْرًا، وَتَارَةً يَجْعَلُونَهُ أَضْغَاثَ أَحْلَامٍ، وَتَارَةً يَجْعَلُونَهُ مُفْتَرًى، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿انْظُرْ كَيْفَ ضَرَبُوا لَكَ الأمْثَالَ فَضَلُّوا فَلا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ سَبِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٤٨، وَالْفُرْقَانِ: ٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلْيَأْتِنَا بِآيَةٍ كَمَا أُرْسِلَ الأوَّلُونَ﴾ : يَعْنُونَ نَاقَةَ صَالِحٍ، وَآيَاتِ مُوسَى وَعِيسَى. وَقَدْ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا مَنَعَنَا أَنْ نُرْسِلَ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا أَنْ كَذَّبَ بِهَا الأوَّلُونَ وَآتَيْنَا ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ مُبْصِرَةً فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا﴾ [الْآيَةَ] [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥٩] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا آمَنَتْ قَبْلَهُمْ مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ أَهْلَكْنَاهَا أَفَهُمْ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا آتَيْنَا قَرْيَةً مِنَ الْقُرَى الَّذِينَ بُعِثَ فِيهِمْ الرُّسُلُ آيَةً عَلَى يَدَيْ نَبِيِّهَا فَآمَنُوا بِهَا، بَلْ كَذَّبُوا، فأهلكناهم بِذَلِكَ، أَفَهَؤُلَاءِ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْآيَاتِ لَوْ رَأَوْها دُونَ أُولَئِكَ؟ كَلَّا بَلْ ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦، ٩٧] .

هَذَا كُلُّهُ، وَقَدْ شَاهَدُوا مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ، وَالْحُجَجِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ، وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْبَيِّنَاتِ، عَلَى يَدَيْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَا هُوَ أَظْهَرُ وَأَجْلَى، وَأَبْهَرُ وَأَقْطَعُ وَأَقْهَرُ، مِمَّا شُوهِدَ مَعَ غَيْرِهِ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: ذُكِرَ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ الْحُبَابِ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَارِثُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ الْحَضْرَمِيُّ، عَنْ عُلَيِّ بْنِ رَبَاحٍ اللَّخْمِيِّ، حَدَّثَنِي مَنْ شَهِدَ عُبَادَةَ بْنَ الصَّامِتِ، يَقُولُ: كُنَّا فِي الْمَسْجِدِ وَمَعَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يُقْرِئُ بَعْضُنَا بَعْضًا الْقُرْآنَ، فَجَاءَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بن أبي بن سَلُولَ، وَمَعَهُ نُمْرُقة وزِرْبِيّة، فَوَضَعَ وَاتَّكَأَ، وَكَانَ صَبِيحًا فَصِيحًا جَدِلًا فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ، قُلْ لِمُحَمَّدٍ يَأْتِينَا بِآيَةٍ كَمَا جَاءَ الْأَوَّلُونَ؟ جَاءَ مُوسَى بِالْأَلْوَاحِ، وَجَاءَ دَاوُدُ بِالزَّبُورِ، وَجَاءَ صَالِحٌ بِالنَّاقَةِ، وَجَاءَ عِيسَى بِالْإِنْجِيلِ وَبِالْمَائِدَةِ. فَبَكَى أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: قُومُوا إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ نَسْتَغِيثُ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْمُنَافِقِ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّهُ لَا يُقَامُ لِي، إِنَّمَا يُقَامُ لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ". فَقُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّا لَقِينَا مِنْ هَذَا الْمُنَافِقِ. فَقَالَ:"إِنَّ جِبْرِيلَ قَالَ لِي: اخْرُجْ فَأَخْبِرْ بِنِعَمِ اللَّهِ الَّتِي أَنْعَمَ بِهَا عَلَيْكَ، وَفَضِيلَتِهِ الَّتِي فُضِّلت بِهَا، فَبَشَّرَنِي أَنِّي بُعِثْتُ إِلَى الْأَحْمَرِ وَالْأَسْوَدِ، وَأَمَرَنِي أَنْ أُنْذِرَ الْجِنَّ، وَآتَانِي كِتَابَهُ وَأَنَا أُمِّيٌّ، وَغَفَرَ ذَنْبِي مَا تَقَدَّمَ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وَذَكَرَ اسْمِي فِي الْأَذَانِ وَأَيَّدَنِي بِالْمَلَائِكَةِ، وَآتَانِي النَّصْرَ، وَجَعَلَ الرُّعْبَ أَمَامِي، وَآتَانِي الْكَوْثَرَ، وَجَعَلَ حَوْضِي مِنْ أَعْظَمِ الْحِيَاضِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَوَعَدَنِي الْمَقَامَ الْمَحْمُودَ وَالنَّاسُ مُهْطِعُونَ مُقْنِعُو رُءُوسِهِمْ، وَجَعَلَنِي فِي أَوَّلِ زُمْرَةٍ تَخْرُجُ مِنَ النَّاسِ، وَأَدْخَلَ فِي شَفَاعَتِي سَبْعِينَ أَلْفًا مِنْ أُمَّتِي الْجَنَّةَ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ وَآتَانِي السُّلْطَانَ وَالْمُلْكَ، وَجَعَلَنِي فِي أَعْلَى غُرْفَةٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ فِي جَنَّاتِ النَّعِيمِ ، فَلَيْسَ فَوْقِي أَحَدٌ إِلَّا الْمَلَائِكَةَ الَّذِينَ يَحْمِلُونَ الْعَرْشَ، وَأَحَلَّ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمَ ، وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ كَانَ قَبْلَنَا". وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا.

---

## 21:7-9 — verses 7-9 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, responding to those who denied that messengers could be sent from among mankind: {And We did not send before you except men to whom We revealed}

That is: all the messengers who came before were men from among mankind, none of them was from the angels, as He said in another verse: {And We did not send before you except men to whom We revealed, from among the people of the towns} [Yusuf: 109], and the Almighty said: {Say, "I am not something new among the messengers"} [al-Ahqaf: 9], and the Almighty related, speaking of the past nations that they denied this, saying: {Shall human beings guide us?} [al-Taghabun: 6]. For this reason He said: {So ask the people of the reminder if you do not know}, meaning: ask the people of knowledge among the nations, such as the Jews and the Christians and the rest of the communities, whether the messengers who came to them were human beings or angels. They were only human beings, and this is part of the completeness of God's favor upon His creation, since He sent among them messengers from among themselves who were capable of receiving the message from them and taking it from them.

His saying: {And We did not make them bodies that eat no food}, that is: rather they were indeed bodies that ate food, as the Almighty said: {And We did not send before you any of the messengers except that they ate food and walked in the markets} [al-Furqan: 20], meaning: they were human beings from among mankind, eating and drinking like other people, and entering the markets to earn a livelihood and engage in trade, and this did not harm them nor diminish anything from them, as the polytheists imagined when they said: {What is with this messenger that he eats food and walks in the markets? Why has not an angel been sent down to him to be a warner with him, or why has not a treasure been thrown down to him, or why does he not have a garden from which he may eat?} And the wrongdoers said: {You follow none but a man bewitched} [al-Furqan: 7, 8].

His saying: {And they were not immortal}, that is: in this worldly life, rather they lived and then died, {And We did not grant immortality to any human being before you} [al-Anbiya: 34]. What distinguished them was that revelation came to them from God, Mighty and Majestic, and the angels descended upon them from God with what He decreed concerning His creation, of what He commanded and what He forbade.

His saying: {Then We fulfilled for them the promise}, that is: the promise which their Lord had made to them, "He will surely destroy the wrongdoers." God fulfilled His promise to them and did that. For this reason He said: {So We saved them and whom We willed}, meaning: their followers among the believers, {and We destroyed the transgressors}, that is: those who denied what the messengers brought.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى رادِّا عَلَى مَنْ أَنْكَرَ بِعْثَةَ الرُّسُلِ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا قَبْلَكَ إِلا رِجَالا يُوحَى إِلَيْهِمْ﴾

أَيْ: جَمِيعُ الرُّسُلِ الَّذِينَ تَقَدَّمُوا كَانُوا رِجَالًا مِنَ الْبَشَرِ، لَمْ يَكُنْ فِيهِمْ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ إِلا رِجَالا يُوحَى إِلَيْهِمْ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْقُرَى﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٠٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ مَا كُنْتُ بِدْعًا مِنَ الرُّسُلِ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى حِكَايَةً عَمَّنْ تَقَدَّمَ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ أَنَّهُمْ أَنْكَرُوا ذَلِكَ فَقَالُوا: ﴿أَبَشَرٌ يَهْدُونَنَا﴾ [التَّغَابُنِ:٦] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاسْأَلُوا أَهْلَ الذِّكْرِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيِ:اسْأَلُوا أَهْلَ الْعِلْمِ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ كَالْيَهُودِ وَالنَّصَارَى وَسَائِرِ الطَّوَائِفِ: هَلْ كَانَ الرُّسُلُ الَّذِينَ أَتَوْهُمْ بَشَرًا أَوْ مَلَائِكَةً؟ إِنَّمَا كَانُوا بَشَرًا، وَذَلِكَ مِنْ تَمَامِ نِعمَ اللَّهِ عَلَى خَلْقِهِ؛ إِذْ بَعَثَ فِيهِمْ رُسُلًا مِنْهُمْ يَتَمَكَّنُونَ مِنْ تَنَاوُلِ الْبَلَاغِ مِنْهُمْ وَالْأَخْذِ عَنْهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا جَعَلْنَاهُمْ جَسَدًا لَا يَأْكُلُونَ الطَّعَامَ﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ قَدْ كَانُوا أَجْسَادًا يَأْكُلُونَ الطَّعَامَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا قَبْلَكَ مِنَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ إِلا إِنَّهُمْ لَيَأْكُلُونَ الطَّعَامَ وَيَمْشُونَ فِي الأسْوَاقِ﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٢٠] أَيْ: قَدْ كَانُوا بَشَرًا مِنَ الْبَشَرِ، يَأْكُلُونَ وَيَشْرَبُونَ مِثْلَ النَّاسِ، وَيَدْخُلُونَ الْأَسْوَاقَ لِلتَّكَسُّبِ وَالتِّجَارَةِ، وَلَيْسَ ذَلِكَ بِضَارٍّ لَهُمْ وَلَا نَاقِصٍ مِنْهُمْ شَيْئًا، كَمَا تَوَهَّمَهُ الْمُشْرِكُونَ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿مَالِ هَذَا الرَّسُولِ يَأْكُلُ الطَّعَامَ وَيَمْشِي فِي الأسْوَاقِ لَوْلا أُنزلَ إِلَيْهِ مَلَكٌ فَيَكُونَ مَعَهُ نَذِيرًا أَوْ يُلْقَى إِلَيْهِ كَنز أَوْ تَكُونُ لَهُ جَنَّةٌ يَأْكُلُ مِنْهَا وَقَالَ الظَّالِمُونَ إِنْ تَتَّبِعُونَ إِلا رَجُلا مَسْحُورًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٧، ٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانُوا خَالِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا، بَلْ كَانُوا يَعِيشُونَ ثُمَّ يَمُوتُونَ، ﴿وَمَا جَعَلْنَا لِبَشَرٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ الْخُلْدَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:٣٤] ، وَخَاصَّتُهُمْ أَنَّهُمْ يُوحَى إِلَيْهِمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، تَنَزَّلُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عَنِ اللَّهِ بِمَا يَحْكُمُ فِي خَلْقِهِ مِمَّا يَأْمُرُ بِهِ وَيَنْهَى عَنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ صَدَقْنَاهُمُ الْوَعْدَ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي وَعَدَهُمْ رَبُّهُمْ: "لَيُهْلِكَنَّ الظَّالِمِينَ"، صَدَقَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَعْدَهُ فَفَعَلَ ذَلِكَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُمْ وَمَنْ نَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: أَتْبَاعَهُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، ﴿وَأَهْلَكْنَا الْمُسْرِفِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِمَا جَاءَتِ الرُّسُلُ بِهِ.

---

## 21:10-15 — verses 10-15 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, drawing attention to the nobility of the Qur'an and urging them to recognize its worth: {We have indeed sent down to you a Book in which is your reminder (dhikrukum).} Ibn Abbas said: "your honor (sharafukum)."

Mujahid said: "your discourse." Al-Hasan said: "your religion."

{And it is indeed a reminder for you and for your people, and you will soon be questioned} [al-Zukhruf: 44].

The saying of the Almighty: {And how many a township that was wrongdoing did We shatter} is a form of intensification (expressing great number), just as He said: {And how many generations have We destroyed after Noah} [al-Isra: 17].

And the Almighty said: {How many a township have We destroyed while it was wrongdoing, so it lies in ruins upon its foundations, and abandoned wells, and lofty palaces} [al-Hajj: 45]. His saying: {and We raised up after them another people} means: another nation after them.

{So when they perceived Our punishment} means: when they became certain that the punishment was about to befall them, just as their prophet had warned them, {behold, they were fleeing from it} meaning: they fled, running away.

{Do not flee, and return to that in which you were given luxury, and to your dwellings} this is a mockery of them decreed by fate, meaning: it was said to them, by way of decree: "Do not run away fleeing from the descent of the punishment, and return to the blessings, joy, livelihood, and pleasant dwellings you used to have."

Qatadah said: it is a mockery of them.

{Perhaps you will be questioned} means: about the gratitude you owed for the blessings you had.

{They said, 'Woe to us, indeed we were wrongdoers.'} They confessed their sins at a time when such confession could no longer benefit them. {And that cry of theirs did not cease until We made them a harvested, extinguished people} means: that statement, which was the admission of wrongdoing, continued to be their constant refrain until We cut them down as one cuts a harvest, and their movements and voices were extinguished, utterly stilled.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنَبِّهًا عَلَى شَرَفِ الْقُرْآنِ، وَمُحَرِّضًا لَهُمْ عَلَى مَعْرِفَةِ قَدْرِهِ: ﴿لَقَدْ أَنزلْنَا إِلَيْكُمْ كِتَابًا فِيهِ ذِكْرُكُمْ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: شَرَفُكم.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: حَدِيثُكُمْ. وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ: دِينُكُمْ.

﴿وَإِنَّهُ لَذِكْرٌ لَكَ وَلِقَوْمِكَ وَسَوْفَ تُسْأَلُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٤٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَمْ قَصَمْنَا مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ كَانَتْ ظَالِمَةً﴾ هَذِهِ صِيغَةُ تَكْثِيرٍ، كَمَا قَالَ ﴿وَكَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنَ الْقُرُونِ مِنْ بَعْدِ نُوحٍ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٧] .

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ أَهْلَكْنَاهَا وَهِيَ ظَالِمَةٌ فَهِيَ خَاوِيَةٌ عَلَى عُرُوشِهَا وَبِئْرٍ مُعَطَّلَةٍ وَقَصْرٍ مَشِيدٍ﴾ [الْحَجِّ:٤٥] . وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنْشَأْنَا بَعْدَهَا قَوْمًا آخَرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أُمَّةً أُخْرَى بَعْدَهُمْ.

﴿فَلَمَّا أَحَسُّوا بَأْسَنَا﴾ أَيْ: تَيَقَّنُوا أَنَّ الْعَذَابَ وَاقِعٌ بِهِمْ، كَمَا وَعَدَهُمْ نَبِيُّهُمْ، ﴿إِذَا هُمْ مِنْهَا يَرْكُضُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَفِرُّونَ هَارِبِينَ.

﴿لَا تَرْكُضُوا وَارْجِعُوا إِلَى مَا أُتْرِفْتُمْ فِيهِ وَمَسَاكِنِكُمْ﴾ هَذَا تَهَكُّمٌ بِهِمْ قَدَرًا أَيْ: قِيلَ لَهُمْ قَدَرًا: لَا تَرْكُضُوا هَارِبِينَ مِنْ نُزُولِ الْعَذَابِ، وَارْجِعُوا إِلَى مَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ النِّعْمَةِ وَالسُّرُورِ، وَالْمَعِيشَةِ وَالْمَسَاكِنِ الطَّيِّبَةِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: اسْتِهْزَاءٌ بِهِمْ.

﴿لَعَلَّكُمْ تُسْأَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عَمَّا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنْ أَدَاءِ شُكْرِ النِّعْمَةِ.

﴿قَالُوا يَا وَيْلَنَا إِنَّا كُنَّا ظَالِمِينَ﴾ اعْتَرَفُوا بِذُنُوبِهِمْ حِينَ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ ذَلِكَ، ﴿فَمَا زَالَتْ تِلْكَ دَعْوَاهُمْ حَتَّى جَعَلْنَاهُمْ حَصِيدًا خَامِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا زَالَتْ تِلْكَ الْمَقَالَةُ، وَهِيَ الِاعْتِرَافُ بِالظُّلْمِ، هِجيراهم حَتَّى حَصَدْنَاهُمْ حَصْدًا وَخَمَدَتْ حَرَكَاتُهُمْ وَأَصْوَاتُهُمْ خُمُودًا.

---

## 21:16-20 — verses 16-20 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, the Exalted, informs that He created the heavens and the earth with truth, that is, with justice and equity, {so that He may recompense those who did evil for what they did, and recompense those who did good with the best reward} [al-Najm: 31], and that He did not create that in vain or in jest, as He said: {And We did not create the heaven and the earth and what is between them in falsehood. That is the assumption of those who disbelieve, so woe to those who disbelieve, from the Fire} [Sad: 27].

Regarding His saying, the Exalted: {If We had wanted to take a diversion, We could have taken it from Our own, had We been doers of that}, Ibn Abi Najih said, on the authority of Mujahid: {If We had wanted to take a diversion, We could have taken it from Our own}, meaning: from Ourselves. He is saying: We did not create a garden, nor a fire, nor death, nor resurrection, nor reckoning.

Al-Hasan, Qatadah, and others said: {If We had wanted to take a diversion}, "al-lahw" (the diversion) means woman, in the language of the people of Yemen.

Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said: {If We had wanted to take a diversion, We could have taken it} from the wide-eyed maidens (al-hur al-'in).

Ikrimah and al-Suddi said: what is meant by "al-lahw" here is offspring.

This and what came before it are inseparable in meaning, and it is like His saying, the Exalted: {If Allah had wanted to take a child, He would have chosen from what He creates whatever He willed. Exalted is He} [al-Zumar: 4]. He thus declared Himself absolutely free of taking offspring, all the more so free of what they say of falsehood and untruth, of taking Jesus, or Ezra ('Uzayr), or the angels as offspring, {Exalted and high above what they say, a great highness} [al-Isra: 43].

As for His saying: {had We been doers of that}, Qatadah, al-Suddi, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and Mughirah ibn Miqsam said: meaning, We were not doers of that.

Mujahid said: every instance of "in" in the Qur'an is a form of denial.

As for His saying: {Rather, We cast the truth upon falsehood}, meaning: We make the truth clear so that it obliterates falsehood. For this reason He said: {so it crushes it, and behold, it vanishes}, meaning: it departs and disintegrates. {And woe to you}, that is, O you who say: Allah has a child, {for what you describe}, meaning: for what you say and fabricate.

Then He, the Exalted, informs of the servitude of the angels to Him, and their constancy in obeying Him night and day, saying: {And to Him belongs whoever is in the heavens and the earth, and whoever is with Him}, meaning: the angels, {do not disdain from His worship}, meaning: they do not refrain from it in aversion, as He said: {The Messiah will never disdain to be a servant of Allah, nor will the angels who are near to Him. And whoever disdains His worship and is arrogant, He will gather them all to Himself} [al-Nisa: 172].

As for His saying: {and they do not weary}, meaning: they do not tire and do not grow bored.

{They glorify Him night and day, without flagging}, so they are constant in their work night and day, obedient in intent and action, capable of it, as He, the Exalted, said: {They do not disobey Allah in what He commands them, and they do what they are commanded} [al-Tahrim: 6].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Hakim ibn Hizam said: while the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was among his companions, he said to them: "Do you hear what I hear?" They said: We do not hear anything. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I indeed hear the creaking of the heaven, and it is not to be blamed for creaking, for there is not a space of a hand's span in it except that there is an angel upon it, prostrating or standing." Gharib (singular narration), and they [the compilers of the six major hadith collections] did not report it.

Then Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it by another route, from Yazid ibn Zurai', from Sa'id, from Qatadah, as a mursal (report with a missing link at the Companion level).

Abu Ishaq said, on the authority of Hassan ibn Mukhariq, on the authority of Abdullah ibn al-Harith ibn Nawfal, who said: I sat with Ka'b al-Ahbar while I was a young boy, and I said to him: What do you think of Allah's saying [about the angels], {They glorify Him night and day, without flagging}? Does speech, and the message, and work not distract them from glorification? He said: Who is this boy? They said: from the Banu Abd al-Muttalib. He said: he then kissed my head, and said to me: O my son, He has made glorification for them just as He has made breathing for you. Do you not speak while you are breathing, and walk while you are breathing?

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يخبر تعالى أنه خلق السموات وَالْأَرْضَ بِالْحَقِّ، أَيْ: بِالْعَدْلِ وَالْقِسْطِ، ﴿لِيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَسَاءُوا بِمَا عَمِلُوا وَيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا بِالْحُسْنَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ:٣١] ، وَأَنَّهُ لَمْ يَخْلُقْ ذَلِكَ عَبَثًا وَلَا لَعِبًا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا خَلَقْنَا السَّمَاءَ وَالأرْضَ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا بَاطِلا ذَلِكَ ظَنُّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فَوَيْلٌ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنَ النَّارِ﴾ [ص:٢٧]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَوْ أَرَدْنَا أَنْ نَتَّخِذَ لَهْوًا لاتَّخَذْنَاهُ مِنْ لَدُنَّا إِنْ كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿لَوْ أَرَدْنَا أَنْ نَتَّخِذَ لَهْوًا لاتَّخَذْنَاهُ مِنْ لَدُنَّا﴾ يَعْنِي: مِنْ عِنْدِنَا، يَقُولُ: وَمَا خَلَقْنَا جَنَّةً وَلَا نَارًا، وَلَا مَوْتًا، وَلَا بَعْثًا، وَلَا حِسَابًا.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا: ﴿لَوْ أَرَدْنَا أَنْ نَتَّخِذَ لَهْوًا﴾ اللهو: المرأة بلسان أهل اليمن.

وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخعِي: ﴿لَوْ أَرَدْنَا أَنْ نَتَّخِذَ لَهْوًا لاتَّخَذْنَاهُ﴾ مِنْ الْحُورِ الْعِينِ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ وَالسُّدِّيُّ: الْمُرَادُ بِاللَّهْوِ هَاهُنَا: الْوَلَدُ.

وَهَذَا وَالَّذِي قَبْلَهُ مُتَلَازِمَانِ، وَهُوَ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَوْ أَرَادَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَتَّخِذَ وَلَدًا لاصْطَفَى مِمَّا يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ سُبْحَانَهُ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٤] ، فَنَزَّهَ نَفْسَهُ عَنِ اتِّخَاذِ الْوَلَدِ مُطْلَقًا، لَا سِيَّمَا عَمَّا يَقُولُونَ مِنَ الْإِفْكِ وَالْبَاطِلِ، مِنَ اتِّخَاذِ عِيسَى، أَوِ الْعُزَيْرِ أَوْ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، ﴿سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى عَمَّا يَقُولُونَ عُلُوًّا كَبِيرًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيُّ، وَمُغِيرَةُ بْنُ مِقْسَم، أَيْ: مَا كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: كُلُّ شَيْءٍ فِي الْقُرْآنِ "إِنْ" فَهُوَ إِنْكَارٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ نَقْذِفُ بِالْحَقِّ عَلَى الْبَاطِلِ﴾ أَيْ: نُبَيِّنُ الْحَقَّ فَيَدْحَضُ الْبَاطِلَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَيَدْمَغُهُ فَإِذَا هُوَ زَاهِقٌ﴾ أَيْ: ذَاهِبٌ مُضْمَحِلٌّ، ﴿وَلَكُمُ الْوَيْلُ﴾ أي: أيها القاتلون: لِلَّهِ وَلَدٌ، ﴿مِمَّا تَصِفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تَقُولُونَ وَتَفْتَرُونَ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْ عُبُودِيَّةِ الْمَلَائِكَةِ لَهُ، وَدَأْبِهِمْ فِي طَاعَتِهِ لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَهُ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَنْ عِنْدَهُ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمَلَائِكَةَ، ﴿لَا يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَسْتَنْكِفُونَ عَنْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفَ الْمَسِيحُ أَنْ يَكُونَ عَبْدًا لِلَّهِ وَلا الْمَلائِكَةُ الْمُقَرَّبُونَ وَمَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفْ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ وَيَسْتَكْبِرْ فَسَيَحْشُرُهُمْ إِلَيْهِ جَمِيعًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:١٧٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يَسْتَحْسِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَتْعَبُونَ وَلَا يَملُّون.

﴿يُسَبِّحُونَ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ لَا يَفْتُرُونَ﴾ فَهُمْ دَائِبُونَ فِي الْعَمَلِ لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا، مُطِيعُونَ قَصْدًا وَعَمَلًا قَادِرُونَ عَلَيْهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا يَعْصُونَ اللَّهَ مَا أَمَرَهُمْ وَيَفْعَلُونَ مَا يُؤْمَرُونَ﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ:٦] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي دُلامة الْبَغْدَادِيِّ، أَنْبَأَنَا عَبْدُ الْوَهَّابِ بْنُ عَطَاءٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ صَفْوَانِ بْنِ مُحرِز، عَنْ حَكِيمِ بْنِ حِزَام قَالَ: بَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ أَصْحَابِهِ، إِذْ قَالَ لَهُمْ: "هَلْ تَسْمَعُونَ مَا أَسْمَعُ؟ " قَالُوا: مَا نَسْمَعُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي لَأَسْمَعُ أَطِيطَ السَّمَاءِ، وَمَا تُلَامُ أَنْ تَئِطَّ، وَمَا فِيهَا مَوْضِعِ شِبْر إِلَّا وَعَلَيْهِ مَلَكٌ سَاجِدٌ أَوْ قَائِمٌ". غَرِيبٌ وَلَمْ يُخْرِجُوهُ .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ طَرِيقِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ زُرَيْع، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ مُرْسَلًا.

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ ، عَنْ حَسَّانَ بْنِ مُخَارِقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ نَوْفَلٍ قَالَ: جَلَسْتُ إِلَى كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ وَأَنَا غُلَامٌ، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: أَرَأَيْتَ قَوْلَ اللَّهِ [لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ] ﴿يُسَبِّحُونَ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ لَا يَفْتُرُونَ﴾

أَمَا يَشْغَلُهُمْ عَنِ التَّسْبِيحِ الْكَلَامُ وَالرِّسَالَةُ وَالْعَمَلُ؟. فَقَالَ: فَمَنْ هَذَا الْغُلَامُ؟ فَقَالُوا: مِنْ بَنِي عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ، قَالَ: فَقَبَّلَ رَأْسِي، ثُمَّ قَالَ لِي: يَا بُنَيَّ، إِنَّهُ جَعَلَ لَهُمُ التَّسْبِيحَ، كَمَا جَعَلَ لَكُمُ النَّفَسَ، أَلَيْسَ تَتَكَلَّمُ وَأَنْتَ تَتَنَفَّسُ وَتَمْشِي وَأَنْتَ تَتَنَفَّسُ؟.

---

## 21:21-23 — verses 21-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, Exalted is He, denounces those who took gods besides Him, saying: rather, {they have taken gods from the earth who raise the dead}, meaning: do they give life to the dead and raise them up from the earth? That is, they have no power to do any of that. So how could they make them equals to Allah and worship them alongside Him?

Then He, Exalted is He, informs us that if there existed in reality gods other than Him, the heavens and the earth would have been corrupted. He said: {if there were in them gods}, meaning in the heaven and the earth, {besides Allah, they would have been corrupted}, just as He, Exalted is He, said: {Allah has not taken any son, nor is there any god along with Him. [If there were], then each god would have taken away what he created, and some of them would have overpowered others. Glory be to Allah above what they describe} [al-Mu'minun: 91]. And He said here: {so glory be to Allah, Lord of the Throne, above what they describe}, meaning above what they say, that He has a son or a partner. Glory be to Him, Exalted, Sanctified, and far removed above what they fabricate and invent, a great exaltedness.

His saying: {He is not questioned about what He does, but they will be questioned} means: He is the Judge whose judgment none can overturn, and no one may object to Him, because of His greatness, majesty, and might, His loftiness, wisdom, justice, and kindness. {But they will be questioned} means: He is the one who questions His creation about what they do, as in His saying: {So by your Lord, We will surely question them all, about what they used to do} [al-Hijr: 92-93]. This is like His saying, Exalted is He: {And He grants protection while none can grant protection against Him} [al-Mu'minun: 88].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُنْكِرُ تَعَالَى عَلَى مَنِ اتَّخَذَ مِنْ دُونِهِ آلِهَةً، فَقَالَ: بَلِ ﴿اتَّخَذُوا آلِهَةً مِنَ الأرْضِ هُمْ يُنْشِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَهُمْ يُحْيُونَ الْمَوْتَى وَيَنْشُرُونَهُمْ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ؟ أَيْ: لَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى شَيْءٍ مِنْ ذَلِكَ. فَكَيْفَ جَعَلُوهَا لِلَّهِ نِدًّا وَعَبَدُوهَا مَعَهُ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَوْ كَانَ فِي الْوُجُودِ آلِهَةٌ غَيْرُهُ لَفَسَدَتِ السموات الْأَرْضُ، فَقَالَ ﴿لَوْ كَانَ فِيهِمَا آلِهَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: فِي السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، ﴿لَفَسَدَتَا﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا اتَّخَذَ اللَّهُ مِنْ وَلَدٍ وَمَا كَانَ مَعَهُ مِنْ إِلَهٍ إِذًا لَذَهَبَ كُلُّ إِلَهٍ بِمَا خَلَقَ وَلَعَلا بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ:٩١] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿فَسُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَرْشِ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عَمَّا يَقُولُونَ إِنَّ لَهُ وَلَدًا أَوْ شَرِيكًا، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ وَتَنَزَّهَ عَنِ الَّذِي يَفْتَرُونَ وَيَأْفِكُونَ عُلُوًّا كَبِيرًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا يُسْأَلُ عَمَّا يَفْعَلُ وَهُمْ يُسْأَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْحَاكِمُ الَّذِي لَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، وَلَا يَعْتَرِضُ عَلَيْهِ أَحَدٌ، لِعَظَمَتِهِ وَجَلَالِهِ وَكِبْرِيَائِهِ، وَعُلُوِّهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ وَعَدْلِهِ وَلُطْفِهِ، ﴿وَهُمْ يُسْأَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُوَ سَائِلٌ خَلْقَهُ عَمَّا يَعْمَلُونَ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَوَرَبِّكَ لَنَسْأَلَنَّهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:٩٢، ٩٣] وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ يُجِيرُ وَلا يُجَارُ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ:٨٨] .

---

## 21:24-25 — verses 24-25 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, Exalted, says: rather, {they have taken gods besides Him. Say}, O Muhammad: {bring your proof}, meaning, your evidence for what you claim, {this is the reminder of those with me}, meaning the Qur'an, {and the reminder of those before me}, meaning the earlier scriptures, contrary to what you say and claim. For every book sent down to every prophet who was sent speaks plainly that there is no god but Allah. But you, O polytheists, do not know the truth, and so you turn away from it. This is why He said: {And We did not send before you any messenger except that We revealed to him that there is no god except Me, so worship Me}, just as He said: {And ask those We sent before you of Our messengers, did We make besides the Most Merciful gods to be worshipped?} [al-Zukhruf: 45], and He said: {And We certainly sent into every nation a messenger, saying, worship Allah and avoid taghut (false objects of worship)} [al-Nahl: 36]. So every prophet whom Allah sent called to the worship of Allah alone, without partner, and the fitrah (innate natural disposition) also bears witness to this. The polytheists have no proof, their argument is refuted before their Lord, and upon them is wrath, and for them is severe punishment.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: بَلِ ﴿اتَّخَذُوا مِنْ دُونِهِ آلِهَةً قُلْ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: ﴿هَاتُوا بُرْهَانَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: دَلِيلَكُمْ عَلَى مَا تَقُولُونَ، ﴿هَذَا ذِكْرُ مَنْ مَعِيَ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنَ، ﴿وَذِكْرُ مَنْ قَبْلِي﴾ يَعْنِي: الْكُتُبَ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةَ عَلَى خِلَافِ مَا تَقُولُونَ وَتَزْعُمُونَ، فَكُلُّ كِتَابٍ أُنْزِلَ عَلَى كُلِّ نَبِيٍّ أُرْسِلَ، نَاطِقٌ بِأَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَكِنْ أَنْتُمْ أَيْهَا الْمُشْرِكُونَ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ الْحَقَّ، فَأَنْتُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ عَنْهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا يُوحَى إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاسْأَلْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رُسُلِنَا أَجَعَلْنَا مِنْ دُونِ الرَّحْمَنِ آلِهَةً يُعْبَدُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٤٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:٣٦] ، فَكُلُّ نَبِيٍّ بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَالْفِطْرَةُ شَاهِدَةٌ بِذَلِكَ أَيْضًا، وَالْمُشْرِكُونَ لَا بُرْهَانَ لَهُمْ، وَحُجَّتُهُمْ دَاحِضَةٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ، وَعَلَيْهِمْ غَضَبٌ، وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ.

---

## 21:26-29 — verses 26-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, in response to those who claimed that He, exalted and sanctified is He, has a child from among the angels, as some among the Arabs used to say that the angels are the daughters of God: {Glory be to Him! Rather, they are honored servants.} That is, the angels are servants of God, honored in His sight, in exalted stations and lofty ranks, and they are, in relation to Him, in the utmost state of obedience in both word and deed.

{They do not precede Him in speech, and they act by His command.} That is, they do not put themselves forward before Him with any matter, nor do they oppose Him in what He commands, but rather they hasten to carry it out. His knowledge, exalted is He, encompasses them, so nothing of them is hidden from Him: {He knows what is before them and what is behind them.}

His saying: {And they do not intercede except for one whom He approves} is like His saying: {Who is it that can intercede with Him except by His permission?} [al-Baqarah: 255], and His saying: {And intercession does not benefit with Him except for one whom He permits} [Saba': 23], and there are many other verses conveying this same meaning.

{And they, out of fear of Him,} that is, out of dread and awe of Him, {are apprehensive. And whoever of them should say, "Indeed, I am a god besides Him,"} that is, whoever among them should claim to be a god apart from God, meaning alongside God, {that one We recompense with Hell. Thus do We recompense the wrongdoers,} meaning everyone who says such a thing. This is a conditional statement, and a conditional statement does not necessarily imply that its condition actually occurs, just as in His saying: {Say, "If the Most Merciful had a child, then I would be the first of the worshippers"} [al-Zukhruf: 81], and His saying: {If you associate partners with Him, your deeds will surely be nullified} [al-Zumar: 65].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى رَدًّا عَلَى مَنْ زَعَمَ أَنَّ لَهُ -تَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ-وَلَدًا مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، كَمَنْ قَالَ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ: إِنَّ الْمَلَائِكَةَ بَنَاتُ اللَّهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿سُبْحَانَهُ بَلْ عِبَادٌ مُكْرَمُونَ﴾ أَيِ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِبَادُ اللَّهِ مُكْرَمُونَ عِنْدَهُ، فِي مَنَازِلَ عَالِيَةٍ وَمَقَامَاتٍ سَامِيَةٍ، وَهُمْ لَهُ فِي غَايَةِ الطَّاعَةِ قَوْلًا وَفِعْلًا.

﴿لَا يَسْبِقُونَهُ بِالْقَوْلِ وَهُمْ بِأَمْرِهِ يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَتَقَدَّمُونَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ بِأَمْرٍ، وَلَا يُخَالِفُونَهُ فِيمَا أَمَرَ بِهِ بَلْ يُبَادِرُونَ إِلَى فِعْلِهِ، وَهُوَ تَعَالَى عِلْمه مُحِيطٌ بِهِمْ، فَلَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ مِنْهُمْ خَافِيَةٌ، ﴿يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يَشْفَعُونَ إِلا لِمَنِ ارْتَضَى﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٥] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا لِمَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:٢٣] ، فِي آيَاتٍ كَثِيرَةٍ فِي مَعْنَى ذَلِكَ.

﴿وَهُمْ مِنْ خَشْيَتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ خَوْفِهِ وَرَهْبَتِهِ ﴿مُشْفِقُونَ وَمَنْ يَقُلْ مِنْهُمْ إِنِّي إِلَهٌ مِنْ دُونِهِ﴾ أَيْ: مَنِ ادَّعَى مِنْهُمْ أَنَّهُ إِلَهٌ مَنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، أَيْ: مَعَ اللَّهِ، ﴿فَذَلِكَ نَجْزِيهِ جَهَنَّمَ كَذَلِكَ نَجْزِي الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: كُلُّ مَنْ قَالَ ذَلِكَ، وَهَذَا شَرْطٌ، وَالشَّرْطُ لَا يَلْزَمُ وُقُوعُهُ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قُلْ إِنْ كَانَ لِلرَّحْمَنِ وَلَدٌ فَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْعَابِدِينَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٨١] ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٦٥] .

---

## 21:30-33 — verses 30-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, drawing attention to His complete power and His mighty dominion over His creation of things and His subjugation of all creatures: {Have those who disbelieved not seen} that is, those who deny His divinity and worship others besides Him. Do they not know that Allah alone is self-sufficient in creation, sole in ordering all affairs? So how can it be fitting that anyone other than Him be worshipped, or that anything besides Him be associated with Him? Have they not seen {that the heavens and the earth were a joined mass} that is, everything was connected to everything else, adjoined and piled up, one upon another, at the beginning of creation, and then He split this from that. He made the heavens seven and the earth seven, and He separated between the lowest heaven and the earth with air. Then the sky rained and the earth caused plants to grow. That is why He said: {And We made from water every living thing. Will they not then believe?} that is, while they witness creatures coming into being little by little, visibly before their eyes, and that is proof of the existence of the Maker, the Actor, the Chooser, capable of whatever He wills:

In everything there is a sign for Him
that shows that He is One...

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from his father, from Ikrimah, who said: Ibn Abbas was asked, "Was the night before the day?" He said: "Consider the heavens and the earth when they were a joined mass. Was there anything between them but darkness? That is so you may know that the night was before the day."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... Ibn Umar, that a man came to him asking about the heavens and the earth: {were a joined mass, then We split them apart}. He said: "Go to that elder and ask him, then come back and tell me what he said to you." He went to Ibn Abbas and asked him. Ibn Abbas said: "Yes, the heavens were a joined mass that did not rain, and the earth was a joined mass that did not grow plants. When He created inhabitants for the earth, He split this one open with rain, and split that one open with vegetation." The man returned to Ibn Umar and told him. Ibn Umar said: "Now I know that Ibn Abbas has been given knowledge in the Qur'an. He spoke truly, it was just as he said." Ibn Umar said: "I used to say, I do not like Ibn Abbas's boldness in interpreting the Qur'an, but now I know that he has been given knowledge in the Qur'an."

Atiyyah al-Awfi said: "This one was a joined mass that did not rain, then it rained. And this one was a joined mass that did not grow plants, then it grew plants."

Ismail ibn Abi Khalid said: "I asked Abu Salih al-Hanafi about His saying: {that the heavens and the earth were a joined mass, then We split them apart}. He said: The heaven was one, then He split from it seven heavens, and the earth was one, then He split from it seven earths."

Mujahid said likewise, and added: "The heaven and the earth were not touching each other."

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: "Rather, the heaven and the earth were stuck together, and when He raised the heaven and brought forth the earth from it, that was their splitting apart which Allah mentioned in His Book." Al-Hasan and Qatadah said: "They were together, then He separated between them with this air."

His saying: {And We made from water every living thing} that is, the origin of all living things is from it.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... from Abu Hurayrah, that he said: "O Prophet of Allah, when I see you my eye is cooled and my soul is glad, so tell me about everything." He said: "Everything was created from water."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... from Abu Hurayrah, who said: "I said, O Messenger of Allah, when I see you my soul is glad and my eye is cooled, so inform me about everything." He said: "Everything was created from water." He said: "I said, inform me of a matter which, if I do it, I will enter Paradise." He said: "Spread the greeting of peace, feed the hungry, maintain the ties of kinship, and stand in prayer at night while people are asleep, then enter Paradise in peace."

It was also narrated by Abd al-Samad, Affan, and Bahz, from Hammam. Ahmad alone transmitted it, and this is a chain meeting the standard of the two authentic collections, except that Abu Maymunah is among the men of the Sunan works. His name is Sulaym, and al-Tirmidhi authenticates reports through him. Sa'id ibn Abi Arubah also narrated it from Qatadah as a mursal (report missing a link in its chain) report. And Allah knows best.

His saying: {And We placed in the earth firmly set mountains} that is, mountains by which He made the earth firm, stabilized it, and weighted it down, so that it would not sway with the people, that is, so it would not shake and move, leaving them with no stability upon it, since it is submerged in water except for about a quarter, which is exposed to air and sun, so that its inhabitants may witness the sky and the dazzling signs, wisdom, and proofs within it. That is why He said: {lest it sway with them} that is, so that it would not sway with them.

His saying: {And We placed therein passes as ways} that is, gaps in the mountains through which they travel from one region to another and from one land to another, as is observed on earth: a mountain forms a barrier between one country and another, so Allah places within it an opening, a gap, so that people may travel through it from here to there. That is why He said: {that they may be guided}.

His saying: {And We made the heaven a roof} that is, over the earth, like a dome over it, as He said: {And the heaven We constructed with strength, and indeed, We are its expander} [al-Dhariyat: 47], and He said: {And by the heaven and He who constructed it} [al-Shams: 5], {Have they not looked at the heaven above them, how We constructed it and adorned it, and it has no rifts?} [Qaf: 6]. Construction here means the erecting of a dome, as the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Islam is built upon five," that is, five pillars, and this only occurs with tents, according to what the Arabs were familiar with.

{Protected} that is, elevated and guarded from being reached. Mujahid said: "raised up."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... from Ibn Abbas, that a man said: "O Messenger of Allah, what is this sky?" He said: "A restrained wave, held back from you." A gharib (singular) chain.

His saying: {while they turn away from its signs}, like His saying: {And how many a sign within the heavens and the earth do they pass by, while they are turning away from it} [Yusuf: 105], that is, they do not reflect upon what Allah has created within it of vast expanse, dazzling height, and the adornment of fixed stars and planets during its night, and during its day of this sun which traverses the whole of its orbit in a day and a night, moving to an extent whose measure is known only to the One who determined it, subjected it, and made it move.

Ibn Abi al-Dunya, may Allah have mercy on him, mentioned in his book al-Tafakkur wa al-I'tibar (Reflection and Contemplation) that one of the worshippers among the Children of Israel devoted himself to worship for thirty years. It was the case among them that when a man devoted himself to worship for thirty years, a cloud would shade him. But this man did not see that happen to him as he saw happen to others, so he complained of this to his mother. She said to him: "My son, perhaps you sinned during this period of your worship." He said: "No, by Allah, I know of nothing." She said: "Perhaps you intended something wrong?" He said: "No, nor did I intend anything." She said: "Perhaps you raised your gaze to the sky and then lowered it again without reflecting?" He said: "Yes, often." She said: "That is where you were caught short."

Then He said, drawing attention to some of His signs: {And it is He who created the night and the day} that is, this one in its darkness and stillness, and that one in its light and pleasantness. This one grows long at times and then shortens at other times, and the other is the reverse. {And the sun and the moon}, this one has a light particular to it, an orbit of its own, a period of its own, and a motion and course of its own, and that one has another particular light, another orbit, another course, and another measure. {Each floating in an orbit} [Ya-Sin: 40], that is, revolving.

Ibn Abbas said: "They revolve as the spindle revolves in its whorl." Mujahid said likewise: "The spindle does not revolve except with the whorl, nor does the whorl revolve except with the spindle. Likewise the stars, the sun, and the moon do not revolve except by it, nor does it revolve except by them," as the Almighty said: {[He is] the Cleaver of the daybreak, and He has made the night for rest, and the sun and the moon for calculation. That is the determination of the Exalted in Might, the Knowing} [al-An'am: 96].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنَبِّهًا عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ التَّامَّةِ، وَسُلْطَانِهِ الْعَظِيمِ فِي خَلْقِهِ الْأَشْيَاءَ، وَقَهْرِهِ لِجَمِيعِ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيِ: الْجَاحِدُونَ لِإِلَهِيَّتِهِ العابدون معه غيره، ألم يعلموا أَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْمُسْتَقِلُّ بِالْخَلْقِ، الْمُسْتَبِدُّ بِالتَّدْبِيرِ، فَكَيْفَ يَلِيقُ أَنْ يُعْبَدَ غَيْرُهُ أَوْ يُشْرَكَ بِهِ مَا سِوَاهُ، أَلَمْ يَرَوْا ﴿أَنَّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ كَانَتَا رَتْقًا﴾ أَيْ: كَانَ الْجَمِيعُ مُتَّصِلًا بَعْضُهُ بِبَعْضٍ مُتَلَاصِقٌ مُتَرَاكِمٌ، بَعْضُهُ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ فِي ابْتِدَاءِ الْأَمْرِ، فَفَتَقَ هَذِهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ. فجعل السموات سَبْعًا، وَالْأَرْضَ سَبْعًا، وَفَصَلَ بَيْنَ سَمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَالْأَرْضِ بِالْهَوَاءِ، فَأَمْطَرَتِ السَّمَاءُ وَأَنْبَتَتِ الْأَرْضُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ حَيٍّ أَفَلا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُمْ يُشَاهِدُونَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ تَحْدُثُ شَيْئًا فَشَيْئًا عِيَانًا، وَذَلِكَ دَلِيلٌ عَلَى وُجُودِ الصَّانِعِ الْفَاعِلِ الْمُخْتَارِ الْقَادِرِ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ: فَفِي كُلّ شَيْءٍ لَهُ آيَة ... تَدُلّ علَى أنَّه وَاحد ...

قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ قَالَ: سُئِلَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: اللَّيْلُ كان قبل أو النهار؟ فقال: أرأيتم السموات وَالْأَرْضَ حِينَ كَانَتَا رَتْقًا، هَلْ كَانَ بَيْنَهُمَا إِلَّا ظُلْمَةٌ؟ ذَلِكَ لِتَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّيْلَ قَبْلَ النَّهَارِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ أَبِي حَمْزَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَاتِمٌ، عَنْ حَمْزَةَ بْنِ أَبِي مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ رجلا أتاه يسأله عن السموات وَالْأَرْضِ ﴿كَانَتَا رَتْقًا فَفَتَقْنَاهُمَا﴾ ؟. قَالَ: اذْهَبْ إِلَى ذَلِكَ الشَّيْخِ فَاسْأَلْهُ، ثُمَّ تَعَالَ فَأَخْبِرْنِي بِمَا قَالَ لَكَ. قَالَ: فَذَهَبَ إِلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فسأله. فقال ابن عباس: نعم، كانت السموات رَتْقًا لَا تُمْطِرُ، وَكَانَتْ الْأَرْضُ رَتْقًا لَا تُنْبِتُ.

فَلَمَّا خَلَقَ لِلْأَرْضِ أَهْلًا فَتَقَ هَذِهِ بِالْمَطَرِ، وَفَتْقَ هَذِهِ بِالنَّبَاتِ. فَرَجَعَ الرَّجُلُ إِلَى ابْنِ عُمَرَ فَأَخْبَرَهُ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: الْآنَ قَدْ عَلِمْتُ أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ قَدْ أُوتِيَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ عِلْمًا، صَدَقَ -هَكَذَا كَانَتْ. قَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: قَدْ كُنْتُ أَقُولُ: مَا يُعْجِبُنِي جَرَاءَةُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ عَلَى تَفْسِيرِ الْقُرْآنِ، فَالْآنَ قَدْ عَلِمْتُ أَنَّهُ قَدْ أُوتِيَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ عِلْمًا.

وَقَالَ عَطِيَّةُ العَوْفي: كَانَتْ هَذِهِ رَتْقًا لَا تُمْطِرُ، فَأَمْطَرَتْ. وَكَانَتْ هَذِهِ رَتْقًا لَا تُنْبِتُ، فَأَنْبَتَتْ.

وَقَالَ إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي خَالِدٍ: سَأَلْتُ أَبَا صَالِحٍ الحنَفِي عَنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَنَّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ كَانَتَا رَتْقًا فَفَتَقْنَاهُمَا﴾ ، قَالَ: كَانَتِ السَّمَاءُ وَاحِدَةً، فَفَتَقَ مِنْهَا سَبْعَ سَمَاوَاتٍ، وَكَانَتْ الْأَرْضُ وَاحِدَةً فَفَتَقَ مِنْهَا سَبْعَ أَرْضِينَ.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَزَادَ: وَلَمْ تَكُنِ السَّمَاءُ وَالْأَرْضُ مُتَمَاسَّتَيْنِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: بَلْ كَانَتِ السَّمَاءُ وَالْأَرْضُ مُلْتَزِقَتَيْنِ، فَلَمَّا رَفَعَ السَّمَاءَ وَأَبْرَزَ مِنْهَا الْأَرْضَ، كَانَ ذَلِكَ فَتْقَهُمَا الَّذِي ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ. وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، كَانَتَا جَمِيعًا، فَفَصَلَ بَيْنَهُمَا بِهَذَا الْهَوَاءِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ حَيٍّ﴾ أَيْ: أَصْلُ كل الأحياء منه.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْجَمَاهِرِ ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ بَشِيرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا قَتَادَةُ عَنِ أَبِي مَيْمُونَةَ ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ إِذَا رَأَيْتُكَ قَرَّتْ عَيْنِي، وَطَابَتْ نَفْسِي، فَأَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، قَالَ: "كُلُّ شَيْءٍ خُلِقَ مِنْ مَاءٍ".

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا هَمَّامٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي مَيْمُونَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي إِذَا رَأَيْتُكَ طَابَتْ نَفْسِي، وَقَرَّتْ عَيْنِي، فَأَنْبِئْنِي عَنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ. قَالَ: "كُلُّ شَيْءٍ خُلِقَ مِنْ مَاءٍ" قَالَ: قُلْتُ: أَنْبِئْنِي عَنِ أَمْرٍ إِذَا عملتُ بِهِ دَخَلَتُ الْجَنَّةَ. قَالَ: "أفْش السَّلَامَ، وَأَطْعِمِ الطَّعَامَ، وصِل الْأَرْحَامَ، وَقُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّاسُ نِيَامٌ، ثُمَّ ادْخُلِ الجنَّة بِسَلَامٍ" .

وَرَوَاهُ أَيْضًا عَبْدُ الصَّمَدِ وَعَفَّانُ وبَهْز، عَنْ هَمَّامٍ . تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ، وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ عَلَى شَرْطِ الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، إِلَّا أَنَّ أَبَا مَيْمُونَةَ مِنْ رِجَالِ السُّنَنِ، وَاسْمُهُ سُلَيْمٌ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ يُصَحِّحُ لَهُ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبة، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ مُرْسَلًا وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا فِي الأرْضِ رَوَاسِيَ﴾ أَيْ: جِبَالًا أَرْسَى الْأَرْضَ بِهَا وَقَرَّرَهَا وَثَقَّلَهَا؛ لِئَلَّا تَمِيدَ بِالنَّاسِ، أَيْ: تَضْطَرِبَ وَتَتَحَرَّكَ، فَلَا يَحْصُلُ لَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا قَرَارٌ لِأَنَّهَا غَامِرَةٌ فِي الْمَاءِ إِلَّا مِقْدَارَ الرُّبْعِ، فَإِنَّهُ بَادٍ لِلْهَوَاءِ وَالشَّمْسِ، لِيُشَاهِدَ أَهْلُهَا السَّمَاءَ وَمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْبَاهِرَاتِ، وَالْحِكَمِ وَالدَّلَالَاتِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَنْ تَمِيدَ بِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: لِئَلَّا تَمِيدَ بِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا فِيهَا فِجَاجًا سُبُلا﴾ أَيْ: ثَغْرًا فِي الْجِبَالِ، يَسْلُكُونَ فِيهَا طُرُقًا مِنْ قُطْرٍ إِلَى قُطْرٍ، وَإِقْلِيمٍ إِلَى إِقْلِيمٍ، كَمَا هُوَ الْمُشَاهَدُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، يَكُونُ الْجَبَلُ حَائِلًا بَيْنَ هَذِهِ الْبِلَادِ وَهَذِهِ الْبِلَادِ، فَيَجْعَلُ اللَّهُ فِيهِ فَجْوَةً -ثَغْرَةً-لِيَسْلُكَ النَّاسُ فِيهَا مِنْ هَاهُنَا إِلَى هَاهُنَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَهْتَدُونَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا السَّمَاءَ سَقْفًا﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى الْأَرْضِ وَهِيَ كَالْقُبَّةِ عَلَيْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّمَاءَ بَنَيْنَاهَا بِأَيْدٍ وَإِنَّا لَمُوسِعُونَ﴾ [الذَّارِيَاتِ: ٤٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَالسَّمَاءِ وَمَا بَنَاهَا﴾ [الشَّمْسِ:٥] ، ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَنْظُرُوا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فَوْقَهُمْ كَيْفَ بَنَيْنَاهَا وَزَيَّنَّاهَا وَمَا لَهَا مِنْ فُرُوجٍ﴾ [ق:٦] ، وَالْبِنَاءُ هُوَ نَصْبُ الْقُبَّةِ، كَمَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "بُنِي الْإِسْلَامُ عَلَى خَمْسٍ" أَيْ: خَمْسُ دَعَائِمَ، وَهَذَا لَا يَكُونُ إِلَّا فِي الْخِيَامِ، عَلَى مَا تَعْهَدُهُ الْعَرَبُ.

﴿مَّحْفُوظًا﴾ أَيْ: عَالِيًا مَحْرُوسًا أَنْ يُنال. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: مَرْفُوعًا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الدَّشْتَكي، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، عَنِ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ أَشْعَثَ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ إسحاق القُمِّي-عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، قَالَ رَجُلٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا هَذِهِ السَّمَاءُ، قَالَ: "مَوْجٌ مَكْفُوفٌ عَنْكُمْ" إِسْنَادٌ غَرِيبٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُمْ عَنْ آيَاتِهَا مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ آيَةٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ يَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهَا وَهُمْ عَنْهَا مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ:١٠٥] أَيْ: لَا يَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِيمَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ فِيهَا مِنَ الِاتِّسَاعِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَالِارْتِفَاعِ الْبَاهِرِ، وَمَا زُيِّنَتْ بِهِ مِنَ الْكَوَاكِبِ الثَّوَابِتِ وَالسَّيَّارَاتِ فِي لَيْلِهَا، وَفِي نَهَارِهَا مِنْ هَذِهِ الشَّمْسِ الَّتِي تَقْطَعُ الْفَلَكَ بِكَمَالِهِ، فِي يَوْمٍ وَلَيْلَةٍ فَتَسِيرُ غَايَةً لَا يَعْلَمُ قَدْرَهَا إِلَّا الَّذِي قَدَّرَهَا وَسَخَّرَهَا وَسَيَّرَهَا.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِهِ "التَّفَكُّرُ وَالِاعْتِبَارُ": أَنَّ بَعْضَ عُبَّادِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ تَعَبَّدَ ثَلَاثِينَ سَنَةً، وَكَانَ الرَّجُلُ مِنْهُمْ إِذَا تَعَبَّدَ ثَلَاثِينَ سَنَةً أَظَلَّتْهُ غَمَامَةٌ، فَلَمْ يَرَ ذَلِكَ الرَّجُلُ شَيْئًا مِمَّا كَانَ يَرَى لِغَيْرِهِ، فَشَكَى ذَلِكَ إِلَى أُمِّهِ، فَقَالَتْ لَهُ: يَا بُنَيَّ، فَلَعَلَّكَ أَذْنَبْتَ فِي مُدَّةِ عِبَادَتِكَ هَذِهِ، فَقَالَ: لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا أَعْلَمُ، قَالَتْ: فَلَعَلَّكَ هَمَمْتَ؟ قَالَ: لَا وَلَا هَمَمْتُ. قَالَتْ: فَلَعَلَّكَ رَفَعْتَ بَصَرَكَ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ ثُمَّ رَدَدْتَهُ بِغَيْرِ فِكْرٍ؟ فَقَالَ: نَعَمْ، كَثِيرًا. قَالَتْ: فَمِنْ هَاهُنَا أُتِيتَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُنَبِّهًا عَلَى بَعْضِ آيَاتِهِ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا فِي ظَلَامِهِ وَسُكُونِهِ، وَهَذَا بِضِيَائِهِ وَأُنْسِهِ، يَطُولُ هَذَا تَارَةً ثُمَّ يَقْصُرُ أُخْرَى، وَعَكْسُهُ الْآخَرُ. ﴿وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ﴾ هَذِهِ لَهَا نُورٌ يَخُصُّهَا، وَفَلَكٌ بِذَاتِهِ، وَزَمَانٌ عَلَى حِدَةٍ، وَحَرَكَةٍ وَسَيْرٍ خَاصٍّ، وَهَذَا بِنُورٍ خَاصٍّ آخَرَ، وَفَلَكٍ آخَرَ، وَسَيْرٍ آخَرَ، وَتَقْدِيرٍ آخَرَ، ﴿وَكُلٌّ فِي فَلَكٍ يَسْبَحُونَ﴾ [يس:٤٠] ، أَيْ: يَدُورُونَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَدُورُونَ كَمَا يَدُورُ الْمِغْزَلُ فِي الْفَلْكَةِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: فَلَا يَدُورُ الْمِغْزَلُ إِلَّا بِالْفَلْكَةِ، وَلَا الْفَلْكَةُ إِلَّا بِالْمِغْزَلِ، كَذَلِكَ النُّجُومُ وَالشَّمْسُ وَالْقَمَرُ، لَا يَدُورُونَ إِلَّا بِهِ، وَلَا يَدُورُ إِلَّا بِهِنَّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَالِقُ الإصْبَاحِ وَجَعَلَ اللَّيْلَ سَكَنًا وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ حُسْبَانًا ذَلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٩٦] .

---

## 21:34-35 — verses 34-35 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And We did not grant to any human being before you}, that is, O Muhammad, {immortality}, meaning in this worldly life. Rather, {every one who is upon it will perish, and there will remain the Face of your Lord, Possessor of Majesty and Honor} [al-Rahman: 26, 27].

Some scholars have used this noble verse as evidence that al-Khidr (peace be upon him) died and is not alive until now, because he is a human being, whether he was a wali (saint), a prophet, or a messenger. The Almighty has said: {And We did not grant to any human being before you immortality}.

His saying: {So if you die}, that is, O Muhammad, {would they then be immortal?}, meaning they hope to live on after you. This will not be. Rather, everyone is headed toward extinction. For this reason He said: {Every soul will taste death}. It has been narrated from al-Shafi'i, may Allah have mercy on him, that he recited and cited these two lines of poetry as evidence:

"Men have wished that I would die, but if I die, that is a path in which I am not the first to walk it.

So say to the one who seeks something different from what has already passed: prepare yourself for another turn like it, for it is as if it has already come."

His saying: {And We test you with evil and with good as a trial}, meaning We test you at times with calamities and at other times with blessings, in order to see who is grateful and who is ungrateful, who is patient and who despairs. As Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding {and We test you}: he said, We try you with evil and with good as a trial, with hardship and ease, with health and sickness, with wealth and poverty, with the lawful and the unlawful, with obedience and disobedience, and with guidance and misguidance.

His saying: {And to Us you will be returned}, meaning so that We may repay you for your deeds.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا جَعَلْنَا لِبَشَرٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ﴿الْخُلْدَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا بَلْ ﴿كُلُّ مَنْ عَلَيْهَا فَانٍ وَيَبْقَى وَجْهُ رَبِّكَ ذُو الْجَلالِ وَالإكْرَامِ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٢٦، ٢٧] .

وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ مَنْ ذَهَبَ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى أَنَّ الْخَضِرَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مَاتَ وَلَيْسَ بِحَيٍّ إِلَى الْآنِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ بَشَرٌ، سَوَاءٌ كَانَ وَلِيًّا أَوْ نِبِيًّا أَوْ رَسُولًا وَقَدْ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا جَعَلْنَا لِبَشَرٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ الْخُلْدَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَفَإِنْ مِتَّ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ﴿فَهُمُ الْخَالِدُونَ﴾ ؟! أَيْ: يُؤَمِّلُونَ أَنْ يَعِيشُوا بَعْدَكَ، لَا يَكُونُ هَذَا، بَلْ كُلٌّ إِلَى فَنَاءٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كُلُّ نَفْسٍ ذَائِقَةُ الْمَوْتِ﴾ ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ عَنِ الشَّافِعِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، أَنَّهُ أَنْشَدَ وَاسْتَشْهَدَ بِهَذَيْنَ الْبَيْتَيْنِ: تَمَنَّى رِجَالٌ أَنْ أَمُوتَ وَإِنْ أَمُتْ فَتلْكَ سَبيل لَسْت فيهَا بأوْحد

فقُلْ للَّذي يَبْغي خِلَافَ الَّذِي مَضَى: تَهَيَّأ لأخْرى مثْلها فكَأن قَدِ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَبْلُوكُمْ بِالشَّرِّ وَالْخَيْرِ فِتْنَةً﴾ أَيْ: نَخْتَبِرُكُمْ بِالْمَصَائِبِ تَارَةً، وَبِالنِّعَمِ أُخْرَى، لِنَنْظُرَ مَنْ يَشْكُرُ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرُ، وَمَنْ يَصْبِرُ وَمَنْ يَقْنَطُ، كَمَا قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَنَبْلُوكُمْ﴾ ، يَقُولُ: نَبْتَلِيكُمْ بِالشَّرِّ وَالْخَيْرِ فِتْنَةً، بِالشِّدَّةِ وَالرَّخَاءِ، وَالصِّحَّةِ وَالسَّقَمِ، وَالْغِنَى وَالْفَقْرِ، وَالْحَلَالِ وَالْحَرَامِ، وَالطَّاعَةِ وَالْمَعْصِيَةِ وَالْهُدَى وَالضَّلَالِ..

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِلَيْنَا تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَنُجَازِيكُمْ بِأَعْمَالِكُمْ.

---

## 21:36-37 — verses 36-37 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Prophet ﷺ, {And when those who disbelieve see you} meaning the disbelievers of Quraysh such as Abu Jahl and his likes, {they take you not except as a mockery} meaning they mock you and belittle you, saying: {Is this the one who mentions your gods?} meaning: is this the one who reviles your gods and disparages your intellects? The Almighty said: {while they, at the mention of the Most Merciful, are disbelievers} meaning they are disbelievers in God, and along with this they mock the Messenger of God, as He said in another verse: {And when they see you, they take you not except as mockery, [saying], "Is this the one whom God has sent as a messenger? He almost led us astray from our gods, had we not been steadfast in adherence to them." But they are going to know, when they see the punishment, who is farthest astray in path} [al-Furqan: 41, 42].

His saying: {Man was created of haste}, as He said in another verse: {And man is ever hasty} [al-Isra: 11], meaning in matters.

Mujahid said: God created Adam after everything else, at the end of the day, on the day He created the creatures. When the spirit gave life to his eyes, his tongue, and his head, but had not yet reached his lower parts, he said: "O my Lord, hasten my creation before the sun sets."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The best day on which the sun has risen is Friday. On it Adam was created, on it he was made to enter Paradise, on it he was expelled from it, and on it the Hour will come to pass. And in it there is an hour in which no believer coincides while praying," and he closed his fingers to indicate its shortness, "and asks God for good, except that He gives it to him." Abu Salamah said: Abdullah ibn Salam then said: I know that hour, it is the last hour of the day on Friday, and it is the hour in which God created Adam. The Almighty God said: {Man was created of haste. I will show you My signs, so do not ask Me to hasten}.

The wisdom in mentioning man's haste here is that, having mentioned those who mock the Messenger ﷺ, there arose in people's souls a desire for swift vengeance against them, and impatience for it. So the Almighty God said: {Man was created of haste}, because the Almighty grants respite to the wrongdoer, but when He seizes him, He does not let him escape. He grants a term and then hastens, He waits and then does not delay. For this reason He said: {I will show you My signs} meaning My vengeance, My judgment, and My power over whoever disobeys Me, {so do not ask Me to hasten}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿وَإِذَا رَآكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ يَعْنِي: كُفَّارَ قُرَيْشٍ كَأَبِي جَهْلٍ وَأَشْبَاهِهِ ﴿إِنْ يَتَّخِذُونَكَ إِلا هُزُوًا﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ بِكَ وَيَنْتَقِصُونَكَ، يَقُولُونَ: ﴿أَهَذَا الَّذِي يَذْكُرُ آلِهَتَكُمْ﴾ يَعْنُونُ: أَهَذَا الَّذِي يَسُبُّ آلِهَتَكُمْ وَيُسَفِّهُ أَحْلَامَكُمْ، قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُمْ بِذِكْرِ الرَّحْمَنِ هُمْ كَافِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُمْ كَافِرُونَ بِاللَّهِ، وَمَعَ هَذَا يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَإِذَا رَأَوْكَ إِنْ يَتَّخِذُونَكَ إِلا هُزُوًا أَهَذَا الَّذِي بَعَثَ اللَّهُ رَسُولا. إِنْ كَادَ لَيُضِلُّنَا عَنْ آلِهَتِنَا لَوْلا أَنْ صَبَرْنَا عَلَيْهَا وَسَوْفَ يَعْلَمُونَ حِينَ يَرَوْنَ الْعَذَابَ مَنْ أَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ:٤١، ٤٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿خُلِقَ الإنْسَانُ مِنْ عَجَلٍ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ عَجُولا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١١] أَيْ: فِي الْأُمُورِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: خَلَقَ اللَّهُ آدَمَ بَعْدَ كَلِّ شَيْءٍ مِنْ آخِرِ النَّهَارِ، مِنْ يَوْمِ خَلَقَ الْخَلَائِقَ فَلَمَّا أَحْيَا الرُّوحُ عَيْنَيْهِ وَلِسَانَهُ وَرَأْسَهُ، وَلَمْ يَبْلُغْ أَسْفَلَهُ قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، اسْتَعْجِلْ بِخَلْقِي قَبْلَ غُرُوبِ الشَّمْسِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَان، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَنْبَأَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلْقَمَةَ بْنِ وَقَّاصٍ اللَّيْثِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "خَيْرُ يَوْمٍ طلعت فيه الشَّمْسُ يَوْمُ الْجُمُعَةِ، فِيهِ خُلِقَ آدَمُ وَفِيهِ أُدْخِلَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَفِيهِ أُهْبِطَ مِنْهَا، وَفِيهِ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ، وَفِيهِ سَاعَةٌ لَا يُوَافِقُهَا مُؤْمِنٌ يُصَلِّي -وَقَبَضَ أَصَابِعَهُ قَلَّلَها -فَسَأَلَ اللَّهَ خَيْرًا، إِلَّا أَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ". قَالَ أَبُو سَلَمَةَ: فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ سَلَامٍ: قَدْ عَرَفْتُ تِلْكَ السَّاعَةَ، وَهِيَ آخِرُ سَاعَاتِ النَّهَارِ مِنْ يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي خَلَقَ اللَّهُ فِيهَا آدَمَ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿خُلِقَ الإنْسَانُ مِنْ عَجَلٍ سَأُرِيكُمْ آيَاتِي فَلا تَسْتَعْجِلُونِ﴾ .

وَالْحِكْمَةُ فِي ذِكْرِ عِجَلَةِ الْإِنْسَانِ هَاهُنَا أَنَّهُ لَمَّا ذَكَرَ الْمُسْتَهْزِئِينَ بِالرَّسُولِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ [وَسَلَامُهُ] عَلَيْهِ، وَقَعَ فِي النُّفُوسِ سُرْعَةُ الِانْتِقَامِ مِنْهُمْ وَاسْتَعْجَلَتْ ، فَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿خُلِقَ الإنْسَانُ مِنْ عَجَلٍ﴾ ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى يُمْلِي لِلظَّالِمِ حَتَّى إِذَا أَخَذَهُ لَمْ يُفْلِتْهُ، يُؤَجِّلُ ثُمَّ يُعَجِّلُ، وَيُنْظِرُ ثُمَّ لَا يُؤَخِّرُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿سَأُوْرِيكُمْ آيَاتِي﴾ أَيْ: نَقْمِي وَحُكْمِي وَاقْتِدَارِي عَلَى مَنْ عَصَانِي، ﴿فَلا تَسْتَعْجِلُونِ﴾ .

---

## 21:38-40 — verses 38-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates concerning the polytheists that they also seek to hasten the occurrence of the punishment upon them, out of denial, rejection, disbelief, obstinacy, and treating it as something far-fetched, saying: {And they say, "When will this promise be, if you are truthful?"}

God Almighty said: {If only those who disbelieved knew of the time when they will not be able to keep the Fire away from their faces nor from their backs} that is: if they were certain that it would inevitably befall them, they would not seek to hasten it. And if only they knew of the time when the punishment engulfs them from above them and from beneath their feet, as in {They will have layers of fire above them and layers beneath them} [al-Zumar: 16], and {For them from Hell is a bed and over them coverings} [al-A'raf: 41]. And He said in this verse: {the time when they will not be able to keep the Fire away from their faces nor from their backs}, and He said: {Their garments will be of tar, and the Fire will cover their faces} [Ibrahim: 50]. So the punishment surrounds them from all their sides. {Nor will they be helped} that is: they will have no helper, as He said: {And they will have no protector besides God} [al-Ra'd: 34].

As for His saying: {Rather, it will come to them suddenly} that is, the Fire will come to them suddenly, meaning unexpectedly, {and bewilder them}, that is: it will terrify them so that they submit to it in confusion, not knowing what to do. {And they will not be able to repel it} that is: they will have no means of doing so. {Nor will they be granted respite} that is: this will not be delayed from them even for a single hour.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ أَنَّهُمْ يَسْتَعْجِلُونَ أَيْضًا بِوُقُوعِ الْعَذَابِ بِهِمْ، تَكْذِيبًا وَجُحُودًا وَكُفْرًا وَعِنَادًا وَاسْتِبْعَادًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَيَقُولُونَ مَتَى هَذَا الْوَعْدُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَوْ يَعْلَمُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا حِينَ لَا يَكُفُّونَ عَنْ وُجُوهِهِمُ النَّارَ وَلا عَنْ ظُهُورِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ تَيَقَّنُوا أَنَّهَا وَاقِعَةٌ بِهِمْ لَا مَحَالَةَ لَمَا اسْتَعْجَلُوا، بِهِ وَلَوْ يَعْلَمُونَ حِينَ يَغْشَاهُمُ الْعَذَابُ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ وَمِنْ تَحْتِ أَرْجُلِهِمْ، ﴿لَهُمْ مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ ظُلَلٌ مِنَ النَّارِ وَمِنْ تَحْتِهِمْ ظُلَلٌ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:١٦] ، ﴿لَهُمْ مِنْ جَهَنَّمَ مِهَادٌ وَمِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ غَوَاشٍ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ:٤١] ، وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿حِينَ لَا يَكُفُّونَ عَنْ وُجُوهِهِمُ النَّارَ وَلا عَنْ ظُهُورِهِمْ﴾ وَقَالَ: ﴿سَرَابِيلُهُمْ مِنْ قَطِرَانٍ وَتَغْشَى وُجُوهَهُمُ النَّارُ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ:٥٠] ، فَالْعَذَابُ مُحِيطٌ بِهِمْ مِنْ جَمِيعِ جِهَاتِهِمْ، ﴿وَلا هُمْ يُنْصَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَاصِرَ لَهُمْ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ وَاقٍ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ:٣٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ تَأْتِيهِمْ بَغْتَةً﴾ أَيْ: "تَأْتِيهِمُ النَّارُ بَغْتَةً"، أَيْ: فَجْأَةً ﴿فَتَبْهَتُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: تَذْعَرُهُمْ فَيَسْتَسْلِمُونَ لَهَا حَائِرِينَ، لَا يَدْرُونَ مَا يَصْنَعُونَ، ﴿فَلا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ رَدَّهَا﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ لَهُمْ حِيلَةٌ فِي ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَلا هُمْ يُنْظَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا يُؤَخَّرُ عَنْهُمْ ذَلِكَ ساعة واحدة.

---

## 21:41-43 — verses 41-43 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, consoling His Messenger ﷺ concerning the mockery and denial with which the polytheists were harming him: {And indeed, messengers before you were mocked, but that which they used to mock befell those who scoffed at them} meaning: the punishment whose occurrence they had thought impossible, just as the Almighty said: {And indeed, messengers before you were denied, but they bore patiently the denial and the harm until Our help came to them, and none can alter the words of Allah. And there has certainly come to you some information about the messengers} [al-An'am: 34].

Then the Almighty mentions His favor upon His servants in preserving them by night and by day, and His watching over them and guarding them with His eye that never sleeps, saying: {Say: Who protects you by night and by day from the Most Merciful?} That is: instead of the Most Merciful, meaning other than Him, as the poet said:

"A young girl who never wore fine thin garments, and never tasted pistachios instead of vegetables..."

That is: she never tasted pistachios in place of vegetables.

As for the saying of the Almighty: {Nay, they turn away from the remembrance of their Lord} meaning: they do not acknowledge His favors upon them and His kindness towards them, but rather turn away from His signs and His bounties. Then He said: {Or do they have gods that protect them besides Us?} This is a rhetorical question of denial, reproach, and rebuke, meaning: do they have gods other than Us who protect them and watch over them? The matter is not as they imagined nor as they claimed. This is why He said: {They are not able to help themselves} meaning: these [gods] to which they turned for support, other than Allah, are not able to help even themselves.

As for His saying: {Nor can they be helped by Us} al-'Awfi reported from Ibn 'Abbas concerning {Nor can they be helped by Us}: meaning, they will not be protected or defended. Qatadah said: they will not be granted [from Allah] any good. Others said concerning {Nor can they be helped by Us}: they will not be shielded.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُسَلِّيًا لِرَسُولِهِ [صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ] عَمَّا آذَاهُ بِهِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ مِنَ الِاسْتِهْزَاءِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ: ﴿وَلَقَدِ اسْتُهْزِئَ بِرُسُلٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَحَاقَ بِالَّذِينَ سَخِرُوا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: مِنَ الْعَذَابِ الَّذِي كَانُوا يَسْتَبْعِدُونَ وُقُوعَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ كُذِّبَتْ رُسُلٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَصَبَرُوا عَلَى مَا كُذِّبُوا وَأُوذُوا حَتَّى أَتَاهُمْ نَصْرُنَا وَلا مُبَدِّلَ لِكَلِمَاتِ اللَّهِ وَلَقَدْ جَاءَكَ مِنْ نَبَإِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٣٤] .

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى نِعْمَتَهُ عَلَى عَبِيدِهِ فِي حِفْظِهِ لَهُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، وَكِلَاءَتِهِ وَحِرَاسَتِهِ لَهُمْ بِعَيْنِهِ الَّتِي لَا تَنَامُ، فَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ مَنْ يَكْلَؤُكُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ مِنَ الرَّحْمَنِ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: بَدَلَ الرَّحْمَنِ بِمَعْنَى غَيْرِهِ كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ 

جَارية لَمْ تَلْبَس المُرقَّقا ... وَلَم تَذق منَ البُقول الفُسْتُقا ...

أَيْ: لَمْ تَذُقْ بَدَلَ الْبُقُولِ الْفُسْتُقَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿بَلْ هُمْ عَنْ ذِكْرِ رَبِّهِمْ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِنِعَمِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَإِحْسَانِهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، بَلْ يُعْرِضُونَ عَنِ آيَاتِهِ وَآلَائِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ ﴿أَمْ لَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ تَمْنَعُهُمْ مِنْ دُونِنَا﴾ اسْتِفْهَامُ إِنْكَارٍ وَتَقْرِيعٍ وَتَوْبِيخٍ، أَيْ: أَلَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ تَمْنَعُهُمْ وَتَكْلَؤُهُمْ غَيْرُنَا؟ لَيْسَ الْأَمْرُ كَمَا تَوَهَّمُوا وَلَا كَمَا زَعَمُوا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ نَصْرَ أَنْفُسِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ [الْآلِهَةُ] الَّتِي اسْتَنَدُوا إِلَيْهَا غَيْرَ اللَّهِ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ نَصْرَ أَنْفُسِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا هُمْ مِنَّا يُصْحَبُونَ﴾ قَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلا هُمْ مِنَّا يُصْحَبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُجَارُونَ وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ لَا يُصْحَبُونَ [مِنَ اللَّهِ] بِخَيْرٍ وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: ﴿وَلا هُمْ مِنَّا يُصْحَبُونَ﴾ يمنعون.

---

## 21:44-47 — verses 44-47 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the polytheists: what deluded them and carried them into the misguidance they are in is that they were given enjoyment in the life of this world, and were given comfort, and their lifespan was prolonged in what they were engaged in, so they believed that they were upon something true.

Then He says, admonishing them: {Do they not see that We come to the land, diminishing it from its extremities?} The commentators differed concerning its meaning, and we have presented this earlier in Surat al-Ra'd. The best explanation of it is by His saying: {And We had certainly destroyed the towns that were around you, and We had diversified the signs that perhaps they would return} [al-Ahqaf: 27].

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: he means by that the prevailing of Islam over disbelief.

The meaning is: do they not take heed from God's granting victory to His allies over His enemies, and His destruction of the nations who denied the truth and the wrongdoing towns, and His deliverance of His believing servants? Therefore He says: {Or are they the victors?} meaning: rather they are the defeated, the lowest, the greatest losers, the most despicable.

His saying: {Say, "I only warn you by revelation"} means: I am only conveying from God what I warn you of, of punishment and chastisement. That is nothing but what God has revealed to me. But this avails nothing for one whose insight God has blinded and whose hearing and heart He has sealed. Therefore He says: {And the deaf do not hear the call when they are warned}.

His saying: {And if a whiff of your Lord's punishment should touch them, they would surely say, "O woe to us! Indeed, we were wrongdoers"} means: if the slightest thing of God's punishment were to touch these deniers, they would surely acknowledge their sins and that they had wronged themselves in this worldly life.

His saying: {And We place the scales of justice for the Day of Resurrection, so no soul will be wronged at all} means: We place the just scales for the Day of Resurrection. The majority hold that it is but a single scale, and it is expressed in the plural in consideration of the multiplicity of the deeds weighed in it.

His saying: {So no soul will be wronged at all, and even if it is the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth.
