And sufficient are We as Reckoners}, just as the Almighty says: {And your Lord wrongs no one} [al-Kahf: 49], and He says: {Indeed, God does not wrong even the weight of an atom, and if there is a good deed, He multiplies it and gives from Himself a great reward} [al-Nisa: 40], and Luqman said: {O my son, indeed if it should be the weight of a mustard seed and should be in a rock or in the heavens or in the earth, God will bring it forth. Indeed, God is Subtle, All-Aware} [Luqman: 16].

In the two Sahihs, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Two words, light upon the tongue, heavy in the scale, beloved to the Most Merciful: Glory be to God and praise be to Him, Glory be to God the Magnificent."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abd Allah ibn Amr ibn al-As said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "God, Mighty and Majestic, will single out a man from my nation before the heads of all creation on the Day of Resurrection, and He will unroll before him ninety-nine scrolls, each scroll as far as the eye can see. Then He will say: 'Do you deny anything of this? Have My recording angels who keep watch wronged you?' He will say: 'No, O Lord.' He will say: 'Do you have an excuse, or a good deed?' " He said: "So the man will be dumbfounded and will say: 'No, O Lord.' Then He will say: 'Yes, indeed you have with Us one good deed, and there will be no wrong against you today.' Then a card will be brought out for him on which is written: 'I bear witness that there is no god but God, and that Muhammad is His servant and messenger.' He will say: 'Bring it forth.' The man will say: 'O Lord, what is this card compared to these scrolls?' He will say: 'Indeed, you will not be wronged.' " He said: "So the scrolls will be placed in one pan [and the card in another pan]." He said: "The scrolls became light and the card became heavy." He said: "And nothing is heavier than 'In the name of God, the Most Merciful, the Most Compassionate.'"

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah related it from the hadith of al-Layth ibn Sa'd, through him, and al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (a sound but singularly transmitted report).

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Abd Allah ibn Amr ibn al-As said: The Messenger of God, may God's peace and blessings be upon him, said: "The scales will be set up on the Day of Resurrection, and the man will be brought and placed in one pan, and what has been recorded against him will be placed, and the scale will tip with it." He said: "So he will be sent off toward the Fire." He said: "But when he is being taken away, behold, a caller from the Most Merciful, Mighty and Majestic, will call out: 'Do not hasten, for there remains something for him.' Then a card will be brought on which is written 'There is no god but God,' and it will be placed with the man in the pan until the scale tips in his favor."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from A'ishah, that a man among the companions of the Messenger of God ﷺ sat before him and said: "O Messenger of God, I have slaves who lie to me, betray me, and disobey me, and I beat them and curse them. What is my situation with regard to them?" The Messenger of God ﷺ said to him: "What they have betrayed you in, disobeyed you in, and lied to you about will be reckoned, along with your punishment of them. If your punishment of them was less than their sins, it will be to your credit against them. If your punishment of them was equal to their sins, it will be even, neither for you nor against you. And if your punishment of them exceeded their sins, then retribution will be taken from you for them, the excess that remains against you." The man then began to weep before the Messenger of God ﷺ and cry out, so the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "What is the matter with him? Does he not recite the Book of God?: {And We place the scales of justice for the Day of Resurrection, so no soul will be wronged at all, and even if it is the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth. And sufficient are We as Reckoners}." The man then said: "O Messenger of God, I find nothing better than to part with these," meaning his slaves, "I call you to witness that they are all free."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ: إِنَّمَا غَرَّهُمْ وَحَمَلَهُمْ عَلَى مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّلَالِ، أَنَّهُمْ مُتّعوا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا، وَنُعِّمُوا وَطَالَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْعُمُرُ فِيمَا هُمْ فِيهِ، فَاعْتَقَدُوا أَنَّهُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ وَاعِظًا لَهُمْ: ﴿أَفَلا يَرَوْنَ أَنَّا نَأْتِي الأرْضَ نَنْقُصُهَا مِنْ أَطْرَافِهَا﴾ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي مَعْنَاهُ، وَقَدْ أَسْلَفْنَاهُ فِي سُورَةِ "الرَّعْدِ"، وَأَحْسَنُ مَا فُسِّرَ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَهْلَكْنَا مَا حَوْلَكُمْ مِنَ الْقُرَى وَصَرَّفْنَا الآيَاتِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:٢٧] .

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: يَعْنِي بِذَلِكَ ظُهُورَ الْإِسْلَامِ عَلَى الْكُفْرِ.

وَالْمَعْنَى: أَفَلَا يَعْتَبِرُونَ بِنَصْرِ اللَّهِ لِأَوْلِيَائِهِ عَلَى أَعْدَائِهِ، وَإِهْلَاكِهِ الْأُمَمَ الْمُكَذِّبَةَ وَالْقُرَى الظَّالِمَةَ، وَإِنْجَائِهِ لِعِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أَفَهُمُ الْغَالِبُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: بَلْ هُمْ الْمَغْلُوبُونَ الْأَسْفَلُونَ الْأَخْسَرُونَ الْأَرْذَلُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ إِنَّمَا أُنْذِرُكُمْ بِالْوَحْيِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا أَنَا مُبَلِّغٌ عَنِ اللَّهِ مَا أُنْذِرُكُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ، لَيْسَ ذَلِكَ إِلَّا عَمَّا أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيَّ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يُجْدِي هَذَا عَمَّنْ أَعْمَى اللَّهُ بَصِيرَتَهُ، وَخَتَمَ عَلَى سَمْعِهِ وَقَلْبِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلا يَسْمَعُ الصُّمُّ الدُّعَاءَ إِذَا مَا يُنْذَرُونَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَئِنْ مَسَّتْهُمْ نَفْحَةٌ مِنْ عَذَابِ رَبِّكَ لَيَقُولُنَّ يَا وَيْلَنَا إِنَّا كُنَّا ظَالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَئِنْ مَسَّ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ أَدْنَى شَيْءٍ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ، لَيَعْتَرِفُنَّ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا ظَالِمِينَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَضَعُ الْمَوَازِينَ الْقِسْطَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ فَلا تُظْلَمُ نَفْسٌ شَيْئًا﴾ أَيْ: وَنَضَعُ الْمَوَازِينَ الْعَدْلَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ. الْأَكْثَرُ عَلَى أَنَّهُ إِنَّمَا هُوَ مِيزَانٌ وَاحِدٌ، وَإِنَّمَا جُمِعَ بِاعْتِبَارِ تَعَدُّدِ الْأَعْمَالِ الْمَوْزُونَةِ فِيهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلا تُظْلَمُ نَفْسٌ شَيْئًا وَإِنْ كَانَ مِثْقَالَ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ أَتَيْنَا بِهَا وَكَفَى بِنَا حَاسِبِينَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا يَظْلِمُ رَبُّكَ أَحَدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ:٤٩] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ وَإِنْ تَكُ حَسَنَةً يُضَاعِفْهَا وَيُؤْتِ مِنْ لَدُنْهُ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:٤٠] ، وَقَالَ لُقْمَانُ: ﴿يَا بُنَيَّ إِنَّهَا إِنْ تَكُ مِثْقَالَ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ فَتَكُنْ فِي صَخْرَةٍ أَوْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ أَوْ فِي الأرْضِ يَأْتِ بِهَا اللَّهُ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَطِيفٌ خَبِيرٌ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ:١٦] .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ -ﷺ: "كَلِمَتَانِ خَفِيفَتَانِ عَلَى اللِّسَانِ، ثَقِيلَتَانِ فِي الْمِيزَانِ، حَبِيبَتَانِ إِلَى الرَّحْمَنِ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ وَبِحَمْدِهِ، سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ الْعَظِيمِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ الطَّالَقَاني، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ لَيْثِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، حَدَّثَنِي عَامِرُ بْنُ يَحْيَى، عَنِ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْحُبُلِيِّ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ يَقُولُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إن الله عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَسْتَخْلِصُ رَجُلًا مِنْ أُمَّتِي عَلَى رُءُوسِ الْخَلَائِقِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيَنْشُرُ عَلَيْهِ تِسْعَةً وَتِسْعِينَ سِجِلًّا كُلُّ سِجِلٍّ مَدُّ الْبَصَرِ، ثُمَّ يقول أتنكر من هذا شيئًا؟ أَظْلَمَتْكَ كَتَبَتِي الْحَافِظُونَ؟ قَالَ: لَا يَا رَبِّ، قَالَ: أَفَلَكَ عُذْرٌ، أَوْ حَسَنَةٌ؟ " قَالَ: فَيُبْهَتُ الرَّجُلُ فَيَقُولُ: لَا يَا رَبِّ. فَيَقُولُ: بَلَى، إِنَّ لَكَ عِنْدَنَا حَسَنَةً وَاحِدَةً، لَا ظُلْمَ الْيَوْمَ عَلَيْكَ. فَيُخْرِجُ لَهُ بِطَاقَةً فِيهَا: "أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَأَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا عَبْدُهُ وَرَسُولُهُ" فَيَقُولُ: أَحْضِرُوهُ، فَيَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، مَا هَذِهِ الْبِطَاقَةُ مَعَ هَذِهِ السِّجِلَّاتِ؟ فَيَقُولُ: إِنَّكَ لَا تُظْلَمُ، قَالَ: "فَتُوضَعُ السِّجِلَّاتُ فِي كِفَّةٍ [وَالْبِطَاقَةُ فِي كِفَّةٍ] " ، قَالَ: "فَطَاشَتِ السِّجِلَّاتُ وَثَقُلَتِ الْبِطَاقَةُ" قَالَ: "وَلَا يَثْقُلُ شَيْءٌ بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ" .

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ اللَّيْثِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، بِهِ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا قُتَيْبَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ يَحْيَى، عَنْ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْحُبُلِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "تُوضَعُ الْمَوَازِينُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَيُؤْتَى بِالرَّجُلِ، فَيُوضَعُ في كفة، فيوضع ما أحصى عليه، فتايل بِهِ الْمِيزَانُ" قَالَ: "فَيُبْعَثُ بِهِ إِلَى النَّارِ" قَالَ: فَإِذَا أَدْبَرَ بِهِ إِذَا صَائِحٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَقُولُ: [لَا تَعْجَلُوا] ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ بَقِيَ لَهُ، فَيُؤْتَى بِبِطَاقَةٍ فِيهَا "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" فَتُوضَعُ مَعَ الرَّجُلِ فِي كِفَّةٍ حَتَّى يَمِيلَ بِهِ الْمِيزَانُ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو نُوحٍ قُرَادٌ أَنْبَأَنَا لَيْثُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ مَالِكِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّ رَجُلًا مِنْ أَصْحَابِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، جَلَسَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ لِي مَمْلُوكِينَ، يَكْذِبُونَنِي، وَيَخُونُونَنِي، وَيَعْصُونَنِي، وَأَضْرِبُهُمْ وَأَشْتُمُهُمْ، فَكَيْفَ أَنَا مِنْهُمْ؟ فَقَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يُحْسَبُ مَا خَانُوكَ وَعَصَوْكَ وَكَذَّبُوكَ وَعِقَابُكَ إِيَّاهُمْ، إِنْ كَانَ عِقَابُكَ إِيَّاهُمْ دُونَ ذُنُوبِهِمْ، كَانَ فَضْلًا لَكَ [عَلَيْهِمْ] وَإِنْ كَانَ عِقَابُكَ إِيَّاهُمْ بِقَدْرِ ذُنُوبِهِمْ، كَانَ كَفَافًا لَا لَكَ وَلَا عَلَيْكَ، وَإِنْ كَانَ عِقَابُكَ إِيَّاهُمْ فَوْقَ ذُنُوبِهِمْ، اقْتُصَّ لَهُمْ مِنْكَ الْفَضْلُ الَّذِي يَبْقَى قِبَلَكَ". فَجَعَلَ الرَّجُلُ يَبْكِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: وَيَهْتِفُ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ما لَهُ أَمَا يَقْرَأُ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ؟: ﴿وَنَضَعُ الْمَوَازِينَ الْقِسْطَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ فَلا تُظْلَمُ نَفْسٌ شَيْئًا وَإِنْ كَانَ مِثْقَالَ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ أَتَيْنَا بِهَا وَكَفَى بِنَا حَاسِبِينَ﴾ فَقَالَ الرَّجُلُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا أَجِدُ شَيْئًا خَيْرًا مِنْ فِرَاقِ هَؤُلَاءِ -يَعْنِي عَبِيدَهُ-إِنِّي أُشْهِدُكَ أَنَّهُمْ أحرار كلهم .

---

## 21:48-50 — verses 48-50 (shared commentary)

### Translation

It has already been noted that Allah, Exalted is He, frequently joins together the mention of Musa and Muhammad, Allah's blessings and peace be upon them both, and the mention of their two books. This is why He said: {And We had certainly given Musa and Harun the Furqan} (peace be upon them both). Mujahid said: it means the Book. Abu Salih said: the Torah. Qatadah said: the Torah, its lawful and unlawful matters, and that by which Allah distinguished between truth and falsehood. Ibn Zayd said: it means victory.

The comprehensive statement on this matter is that the heavenly books contain the distinction between truth and falsehood, guidance and misguidance, error and right direction, the lawful and the unlawful, and that which produces light in the hearts, along with guidance, fear, turning back to God, and reverent awe. This is why He said: {a Furqan, a light, and a reminder for the God-fearing}, meaning a reminder for them and an admonition.

Then He described them, saying: {those who fear their Lord unseen}, similar to His saying: {whoever fears the Most Merciful unseen and comes with a penitent heart} [Qaf: 33], and His saying: {Indeed, those who fear their Lord unseen will have forgiveness and a great reward} [al-Mulk: 12]. {and they are, of the Hour, apprehensive}, meaning fearful and anxious.

Then Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And this is a blessed reminder which We have sent down}, meaning the mighty Qur'an, which falsehood cannot approach from before it or from behind it, a revelation from One who is Wise, Praiseworthy. {Are you then rejecting it?}, meaning: do you deny it while it is at the utmost degree of clarity and manifestness?

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ التَّنْبِيهُ عَلَى أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى كَثِيرًا مَا يَقْرِنُ بَيْنَ ذِكْرِ مُوسَى وَمُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمَا، وَبَيْنَ كِتَابَيْهِمَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى وَهَارُونَ الْفُرْقَانَ﴾ . قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي: الْكِتَابَ. وَقَالَ أَبُو صَالِحٍ: التَّوْرَاةُ، وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: التَّوْرَاةُ، حَلَالُهَا وَحَرَامُهَا، وَمَا فَرَّقَ اللَّهُ بَيْنَ الْحَقِّ وَالْبَاطِلِ. وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: يَعْنِي: النَّصْرَ.

وَجَامِعُ الْقَوْلِ فِي ذَلِكَ: أَنَّ الْكُتُبَ السَّمَاوِيَّةَ تَشْتَمِلُ عَلَى التَّفْرِقَةِ بَيْنَ الْحَقِّ وَالْبَاطِلِ، وَالْهُدَى وَالضَّلَالِ، وَالْغَيِّ وَالرَّشَادِ، وَالْحَلَالِ وَالْحَرَامِ، وَعَلَى مَا يُحَصِّلُ نُورًا فِي الْقُلُوبِ، وَهِدَايَةً وَخَوْفًا وَإِنَابَةً وَخَشْيَةً؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿الْفُرْقَانَ وَضِيَاءً وَذِكْرًا لِلْمُتَّقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: [تَذْكِيرًا] لَهُمْ وَعِظَةً.

ثُمَّ وَصَفَهُمْ فَقَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَخْشَوْنَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَيْبِ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿مَنْ خَشِيَ الرَّحْمَنَ بِالْغَيْبِ وَجَاءَ بِقَلْبٍ مُنِيبٍ﴾ [ق:٣٣] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَخْشَوْنَ رَبَّهُمْ بِالْغَيْبِ لَهُمْ مَغْفِرَةٌ وَأَجْرٌ كَبِيرٌ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:١٢] ، ﴿وَهُمْ مِنَ السَّاعَةِ مُشْفِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: خَائِفُونَ وَجِلُونَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهَذَا ذِكْرٌ مُبَارَكٌ أَنزلْنَاهُ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنُ الْعَظِيمُ، الذِي لَا يَأْتِيهِ الْبَاطِلُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ، وَلَا مِنْ خَلْفِهِ تَنْزِيلٌ مِنْ حَكِيمٍ حَمِيدٍ، ﴿أَفَأَنْتُمْ لَهُ مُنْكِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفَتُنْكِرُونَهُ وَهُوَ فِي غَايَةِ [الْجَلَاءِ] وَالظُّهُورِ؟.

---

## 21:51-56 — verses 51-56 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us about His close friend Ibrahim (peace be upon him), that He gave him his right guidance before, that is, from his youth He inspired in him the truth and the argument against his people, as the Almighty said: {And that is Our argument which We gave to Ibrahim against his people} [al-An'am: 83].

As for what is mentioned in reports about him being placed by his father in an underground chamber while he was a nursing infant, and that he was brought out after some days and looked at the star and the created things, reflecting upon them, and what many exegetes and others have narrated of this story, most of it consists of tales of the Children of Israel (isra'iliyyat). Whatever of it agrees with the truth found in what we have from the infallible source [i.e., the Prophet ﷺ], we accept it because it agrees with what is sound. Whatever contradicts any of that, we reject it. And whatever contains neither agreement nor contradiction, we neither affirm it as true nor reject it as false, but rather we leave it in suspension. As for material of this last kind, many of the early generations permitted its transmission, though much of it has no benefit and yields nothing useful for religion. Had there been in it any benefit returning to those under religious obligation in their religion, this complete and comprehensive Shari'ah would have made it clear.

What we follow in this tafsir is turning away from most of these isra'iliyyat reports, because of the waste of time involved in them, and because much of what they contain is fabrication that was circulated among them, for they make no distinction between the sound and the defective among their reports, as the precise, memorizing scholarly authorities (huffaz) of this nation have established.

What is intended here is that God Almighty informs us that He had given Ibrahim his right guidance before, that is, before that [incident]. His saying, {and We were of him fully aware}, means: he was fit for that.

Then He said: {When he said to his father and his people, "What are these statues to which you are devoted?"} This is the right guidance that he was given from his youth: the denunciation of his people for worshipping idols besides God, Mighty and Majestic. So he said: {What are these statues to which you are devoted?}, meaning, devoted in worship of them.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] al-Asbagh ibn Nubatah said: Ali passed by a group of people playing chess and said, "What are these statues to which you are devoted? For one of you to touch a burning coal until it is extinguished would be better for him than to touch it."

{They said, "We found our fathers worshipping them."} They had no argument except the practice of their misguided forefathers. Therefore He said: {You and your fathers have been in manifest error}, that is, the address to your fathers, whose practice you cite as your argument, is like the address to you. Both you and they are in error, off the straight path.

When he thus exposed the foolishness of their reasoning, declared their fathers to be misguided, and belittled their gods, {they said, "Have you come to us with the truth, or are you one of those who jest?"} They meant: is this speech coming from you said in jest, or are you serious about it? For we have never heard of such a thing before you.

{He said, "Rather, your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, who originated them,"} meaning: your Lord, besides whom there is no god, is the one who created the heavens [and the earth] and what they contain of created things, who initiated their creation, and He is the Creator of all things. {And I am among those who bear witness to that}, meaning: and I bear witness that there is no god besides Him and no lord other than Him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ خَلِيلِهِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ آتَاهُ رُشْدَهُ مِنْ قَبْلُ، أَيْ: مِنْ صِغَرِهِ أَلْهَمَهُ الْحَقَّ وَالْحُجَّةَ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتِلْكَ حُجَّتُنَا آتَيْنَاهَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٨٣] ، وَمَا يُذْكَرُ مِنَ الْأَخْبَارِ عَنْهُ فِي إِدْخَالِ أَبِيهِ لَهُ فِي السِّرْبِ، وَهُوَ رَضِيعٌ، وَأَنَّهُ خَرَجَ بِهِ بَعْدَ أَيْامٍ، فَنَظَرَ إِلَى الْكَوْكَبِ وَالْمَخْلُوقَاتِ، فَتَبَصَّرَ فِيهَا وَمَا قَصَّهُ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ وَغَيْرِهِمْ -فَعَامَّتُهَا أَحَادِيثُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَمَا وَافَقَ مِنْهَا الْحَقَّ مِمَّا بِأَيْدِينَا عَنِ الْمَعْصُومِ قَبِلْنَاهُ لِمُوَافَقَتِهِ الصَّحِيحَ، وَمَا خَالَفَ شَيْئًا مِنْ ذَلِكَ رَدَدْنَاهُ، وَمَا لَيْسَ فِيهِ مُوَافَقَةٌ وَلَا مُخَالَفَةٌ لَا نصدقه ولا نكذبه، بل نجعله وفقًا، وَمَا كَانَ مِنْ هَذَا الضَّرْبِ مِنْهَا فَقَدْ تَرَخَّصَ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ السَّلَفِ فِي رِوَايَتِهَا، وَكَثِيرٌ مِنْ ذَلِكَ مَا لَا فَائِدَةَ فِيهِ، وَلَا حاصل له مِمَّا يُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ فِي الدِّينِ. وَلَوْ كَانَتْ فِيهِ فَائِدَةٌ تَعُودُ عَلَى الْمُكَلَّفِينَ فِي دِينِهِمْ لَبَيَّنَتْهُ هَذِهِ الشَّرِيعَةُ الْكَامِلَةُ الشَّامِلَةُ. وَالَّذِي نَسْلُكُهُ فِي هَذَا التَّفْسِيرِ الْإِعْرَاضُ عَنْ كَثِيرٍ مِنَ الْأَحَادِيثِ الْإِسْرَائِيلِيَّةِ، لِمَا فِيهَا مِنْ تَضْيِيعِ الزَّمَانِ، وَلِمَا اشْتَمَلَ عَلَيْهِ كَثِيرٌ مِنْهَا مِنَ الْكَذِبِ الْمُرَوَّجِ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَإِنَّهُمْ لَا تَفْرِقَةَ عِنْدَهُمْ بَيْنَ صَحِيحِهَا وَسَقِيمِهَا كَمَا حَرَّرَهُ الْأَئِمَّةُ الْحُفَّاظُ الْمُتْقِنُونَ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ.

وَالْمَقْصُودُ هَاهُنَا: أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ آتَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ رُشْدَهُ، مِنْ قَبْلُ، أَيْ: مِنْ قَبْلِ ذَلِكَ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكُنَّا بِهِ عَالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَكَانَ أَهْلًا لِذَلِكَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿إِذْ قَالَ لأبِيهِ وَقَوْمِهِ مَا هَذِهِ التَّمَاثِيلُ الَّتِي أَنْتُمْ لَهَا عَاكِفُونَ﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الرُّشْدُ الَّذِي أُوتِيهِ مِنْ صِغَرِهِ، الْإِنْكَارُ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ فِي عِبَادَةِ الْأَصْنَامِ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَقَالَ: ﴿مَا هَذِهِ التَّمَاثِيلُ الَّتِي أَنْتُمْ لَهَا عَاكِفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مُعْتَكِفُونَ عَلَى عِبَادَتِهَا.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّبَّاحُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ الضَّرِيرُ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعْدُ بْنُ طَرِيفٍ، عَنِ الْأَصْبَغِ بْنِ نُبَاتَةَ، قَالَ: مَرَّ عَلِيٌّ، عَلَى قَوْمٍ يَلْعَبُونَ بِالشِّطْرَنْجِ، فَقَالَ: مَا هَذِهِ التَّمَاثِيلُ الَّتِي أَنْتُمْ لَهَا عَاكِفُونَ؟ لَأَنْ يَمَسَّ أَحَدُكُمْ جَمْرًا حَتَّى يُطْفَأَ خَيْرٌ لَهُ مِنْ أَنْ يَمَسَّهَا.

﴿قَالُوا وَجَدْنَا آبَاءَنَا لَهَا عَابِدِينَ﴾ : لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ حُجَّةٌ سِوَى صَنِيعِ آبَائِهِمُ الضُّلَّالِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ كُنْتُمْ أَنْتُمْ وَآبَاؤُكُمْ فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ أَيِ: الْكَلَامُ مَعَ آبَائِكُمُ الَّذِينَ احْتَجَجْتُمْ بِصَنِيعِهِمْ كَالْكَلَامِ مَعَكُمْ، فَأَنْتُمْ وَهُمْ فِي ضَلَالٍ عَلَى غَيْرِ الطَّرِيقِ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ.

فَلَمَّا سَفَّهَ أَحْلَامَهُمْ، وَضَلَّلَ آبَاءَهُمْ، وَاحْتَقَرَ آلِهَتَهُمْ ﴿قَالُوا أَجِئْتَنَا بِالْحَقِّ أَمْ أَنْتَ مِنَ اللاعِبِينَ﴾ يَقُولُونَ : هَذَا الْكَلَامُ الصَّادِرُ عَنْكَ تَقُولُهُ لَاعِبًا أَوْ مُحِقًّا فِيهِ؟ فَإِنَّا لَمْ نَسْمَعْ بِهِ قَبْلَكَ.

﴿قَالَ بَل رَبُّكُمْ رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ الَّذِي فَطَرَهُنَّ﴾ أَيْ: رَبُّكُمْ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، هُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السموات [وَالْأَرْضَ] وَمَا حَوَتْ مِنَ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ الَّذِي ابْتَدَأَ خَلْقَهُنَّ، وَهُوَ الْخَالِقُ لِجَمِيعِ الْأَشْيَاءِ ﴿وَأَنَا عَلَى ذَلِكُمْ مِنَ الشَّاهِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَأَنَا أَشْهَدُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

---

## 21:57-63 — verses 57-63 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Then the Friend of Allah (al-Khalil, i.e. Ibrahim) swore an oath which some of his people heard, that he would surely scheme against their idols, meaning: he would surely persist in harming them and breaking them, after they turned away departing, that is, to their festival. For they had a festival to which they used to go out.

Al-Suddi said: When the time of that festival approached, his father said, "O my son, if only you would go out with us to our festival, our religion would please you!" So he went out with them, and when he was partway along the road, he threw himself to the ground and said, "Indeed I am sick." So they began passing by him as he lay fallen, saying, "What is wrong?" and he would say, "I am sick." When the majority of them had passed and only the weaker ones remained, he said: {By Allah, I will surely scheme against your idols}, and those remaining ones heard him.

Abu Ishaq said, from Abu al-Ahwas, from Abdullah, who said: When the people of Ibrahim went out to their festival, they passed by him and said, "O Ibrahim, will you not come out with us?" He said, "I am sick." And indeed the day before he had said: {By Allah, I will surely scheme against your idols after you have turned away departing}, and some people among them heard him.

As for His saying, {So he made them into fragments}, meaning: rubble, he broke them all, {except a large one belonging to them}, meaning: except the idol that was great among them, as He said: {Then he turned upon them, striking with his right hand} [al-Saffat: 93].

As for His saying, {that perhaps they would return to it}, they mentioned that he placed the axe in the hand of their chief idol, so that perhaps they would believe that it was the one who, out of jealousy for itself and disdain that these small idols should be worshipped alongside it, had broken them.

{They said, "Who has done this to our gods? He is indeed among the wrongdoers"}, meaning: when they returned and witnessed what the Friend of Allah had done to their idols, of humiliation and degradation indicating their lack of divinity and the feebleness of the minds of their worshippers, {they said, "Who has done this to our gods? He is indeed among the wrongdoers"}, meaning: in this deed of his.

{They said, "We heard a young man mention them who is called Ibrahim"}, meaning: those who had heard him swear that he would surely scheme against them said: {We heard a young man}, that is, a youth, {mention them who is called Ibrahim}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: Allah sent no prophet except while he was young, and no scholar was given knowledge except while he was young, and he recited this verse: {They said, "We heard a young man mention them who is called Ibrahim"}.

As for His saying, {They said, "Then bring him before the eyes of the people"}, meaning: before the assembly, in the great gathering, in the presence of all the people. This was the greatest objective for Ibrahim, that it should become clear in this great assembly the extent of their ignorance and the poverty of their reason in worshipping these idols, which could not repel harm from themselves nor possess any power to help themselves. So how could anything of that sort be sought from them?

{They said, "Was it you who did this to our gods, O Ibrahim?" He said, "Rather, it was this, their chief, who did it}, meaning the one he had left unbroken, {so ask them, if they can speak"}. He intended by this that they would hasten of their own accord to acknowledge that the idols could not speak, for such a thing could not proceed from this idol, since it was inanimate matter.

In the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Hisham ibn Hassan, from Muhammad ibn Sirin, from Abu Hurairah: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Ibrahim (peace be upon him) never told a lie except three times: two of them concerning the matter of Allah, his saying {Rather, it was this, their chief, who did it}, and his saying {I am sick}." He said: "And while he was traveling in the land of a tyrant among the tyrants, with Sarah accompanying him, he stopped at a place, and a man came to the tyrant and said, 'A man has come down into your land accompanied by a woman, the most beautiful of people.' So he sent for him, and he came, and he said, 'What relation is this woman to you?' He said, 'She is my sister.' He said, 'Then go and send her to me.' So he went to Sarah and said, 'This tyrant has asked me about you, and I have told him that you are my sister, so do not contradict me before him, for you are indeed my sister in the Book of Allah, and there is no Muslim on earth besides me and you.' So Ibrahim brought her, then stood to pray. When she entered his presence and he saw her, he reached toward her and took hold of her, but he was seized violently. He said, 'Pray to Allah for me, and I will not harm you.' So she prayed for him, and he was released. He then reached toward her again and took hold of her, and he was seized as before or worse. He did this a third time, and he was seized as in the two previous times, so he said, 'Pray to Allah, and I will not harm you.' So she prayed for him, and he was released. Then he called the nearest of his guards and said, 'You have not brought me a human being, you have brought me a devil. Take her out and give her Hagar.' So she was taken out and given Hagar, and she came forward. When Ibrahim sensed her coming, he turned from his prayer and said, 'What happened?' She said, 'Allah restrained the scheme of the disbelieving, immoral one, and he gave me Hagar to serve me.'" Muhammad ibn Sirin said: Abu Hurairah, when he narrated this hadith, would say, "So that is your mother, O children of the water of the sky."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ثُمَّ أَقْسَمَ الْخَلِيلُ قَسَمًا أَسْمَعَهُ بَعْضَ قَوْمِهِ لَيَكِيدَنَّ أَصْنَامَهُمْ، أَيْ: لَيَحْرِصَنَّ عَلَى أَذَاهُمْ وَتَكْسِيرِهِمْ بَعْدَ أَنْ يُوَلُّوا مُدْبِرِينَ أَيْ: إِلَى عِيدِهِمْ. وَكَانَ لَهُمْ عيد يخرجون إليه.

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: لَمَّا اقْتَرَبَ وَقْتُ ذَلِكَ الْعِيدِ قَالَ أَبُوهُ: يَا بُنَيَّ، لَوْ خَرَجْتَ مَعَنَا إِلَى عِيدِنَا لَأَعْجَبَكَ دِينُنَا! فَخَرَجَ مَعَهُمْ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ بِبَعْضِ الطَّرِيقِ أَلْقَى نَفْسَهُ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ. وَقَالَ: إِنِّي سَقِيمٌ، فَجَعَلُوا يَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهِ وَهُوَ صَرِيعٌ، فَيَقُولُونَ: مَهْ! فَيَقُولُ: إِنِّي سَقِيمٌ، فَلَمَّا جَازَ عَامَّتُهُمْ وَبَقِيَ ضُعَفَاؤُهُمْ قَالَ: ﴿تَاللَّهِ لأكِيدَنَّ أَصْنَامَكُمْ﴾ فَسَمِعَهُ أُولَئِكَ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: لَمَّا خَرَجَ قَوْمُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، إِلَى عِيدِهِمْ مَرُّوا عَلَيْهِ فَقَالُوا: يَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ أَلَا تَخْرُجُ مَعَنَا؟ قَالَ: إِنِّي سَقِيمٌ. وَقَدْ كَانَ بِالْأَمْسِ قَالَ: ﴿تَاللَّهِ لأكِيدَنَّ أَصْنَامَكُمْ بَعْدَ أَنْ تُوَلُّوا مُدْبِرِينَ﴾ فَسَمِعَهُ نَاسٌ مِنْهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَجَعَلَهُمْ جُذَاذًا﴾ أَيْ: حُطَامًا كَسَّرَهَا كُلَّهَا ﴿إِلا كَبِيرًا لَهُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: إِلَّا الصَّنَمَ الْكَبِيرَ عِنْدَهُمْ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَرَاغَ عَلَيْهِمْ ضَرْبًا بِالْيَمِينِ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:٩٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ إِلَيْهِ يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ ذَكَرُوا أَنَّهُ وَضَعَ الْقَدُومَ فِي يَدِ كَبِيرِهِمْ، لَعَلَّهُمْ يَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي غَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ، وَأَنِفَ أَنْ تُعْبَدَ مَعَهُ هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامُ الصِّغَارُ، فَكَسَّرَهَا.

﴿قَالُوا مَنْ فَعَلَ هَذَا بِآلِهَتِنَا إِنَّهُ لَمِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: حِينَ رَجَعُوا وَشَاهَدُوا مَا فَعَلَهُ الْخَلِيلُ بِأَصْنَامِهِمْ مِنَ الْإِهَانَةِ وَالْإِذْلَالِ الدَّالِّ عَلَى عَدَمِ إِلَهِيَّتِهَا، وَعَلَى سَخَافَةِ عُقُولِ عَابِدِيهَا ﴿قَالُوا مَنْ فَعَلَ هَذَا بِآلِهَتِنَا إِنَّهُ لَمِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي صَنِيعِهِ هَذَا.

﴿قَالُوا سَمِعْنَا فَتًى يَذْكُرُهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ﴾ أَيْ: قَالَ مَنْ سَمِعَهُ يَحْلِفُ أَنَّهُ لَيَكِيدَنَّهُمْ: ﴿سَمِعْنَا فَتًى﴾ أَيْ: شَابًّا ﴿يَذْكُرُهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَوْفٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ، عَنْ قَابُوسٍ [عَنْ أَبِيهِ] ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: مَا بَعَثَ اللَّهُ نَبِيًّا إِلَّا شَابًّا، وَلَا أُوتِيَ الْعَلَمَ عَالِمٌ إِلَّا وَهُوَ شَابٌّ، وَتَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿قَالُوا سَمِعْنَا فَتًى يَذْكُرُهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قَالُوا فَأْتُوا بِهِ عَلَى أَعْيُنِ النَّاسِ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى رُءُوسِ الْأَشْهَادِ فِي الْمَلَإِ الْأَكْبَرِ بِحَضْرَةِ النَّاسِ كُلِّهِمْ، وَكَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْمَقْصُودَ الْأَكْبَرَ لِإِبْرَاهِيمَ أَنْ يَتَبَيَّنَ فِي هَذَا الْمَحْفِلِ الْعَظِيمِ كَثْرَةُ جَهْلِهِمْ وَقِلَّةُ عَقْلِهِمْ فِي عِبَادَةِ هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامِ الَّتِي لَا تَدْفَعُ عَنْ نَفْسِهَا ضَرًّا، وَلَا تَمْلِكُ لَهَا نَصْرًا، فَكَيْفَ يُطْلَبُ مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ مِنْ ذَلِكَ؟.

﴿قَالُوا أَأَنْتَ فَعَلْتَ هَذَا بِآلِهَتِنَا يَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ قَالَ بَلْ فَعَلَهُ كَبِيرُهُمْ هَذَا﴾ يَعْنِي: الَّذِي تَرَكَهُ لَمْ يَكْسِرْهُ ﴿فَاسْأَلُوهُمْ إِنْ كَانُوا يَنْطِقُونَ﴾ وَإِنَّمَا أَرَادَ بِهَذَا أَنْ يُبَادِرُوا مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ، فَيَعْتَرِفُوا أَنَّهُمْ لَا يَنْطِقُونَ، فَإِنَّ هَذَا لَا يَصْدُرُ عَنْ هَذَا الصَّنَمِ، لِأَنَّهُ جَمَادٌ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ هِشَامُ بْنُ حَسَّانَ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَمْ يَكْذِبْ غَيْرَ ثَلَاثٍ: ثِنْتَيْنِ فِي ذَاتِ اللَّهِ ، قَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ فَعَلَهُ كَبِيرُهُمْ هَذَا﴾ وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿إِنِّي سَقِيمٌ﴾ قَالَ: "وَبَيْنَا هُوَ يَسِيرُ فِي أرض جبار من الجبابرة ومعه سَارَةُ، إِذْ نَزَلَ مَنْزِلًا فَأَتَى الْجَبَّارَ رَجُلٌ، فَقَالَ: إِنَّهُ قَدْ نَزَلَ بِأَرْضِكَ رَجُلٌ مَعَهُ امْرَأَةٌ أَحْسَنُ النَّاسِ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِ فَجَاءَ، فَقَالَ: مَا هَذِهِ الْمَرْأَةُ مِنْكَ؟ قَالَ: هِيَ أُخْتِي. قَالَ: فَاذْهَبْ فَأَرْسِلْ بِهَا إِلَيَّ، فَانْطَلَقَ إِلَى سَارَةَ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ هَذَا الْجَبَّارَ سَأَلَنِي عَنْكِ فَأَخْبَرْتُهُ أَنَّكِ أُخْتِي فَلَا تُكَذِّبِينِي عِنْدَهُ، فَإِنَّكِ أُخْتِي فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَيْسَ فِي الْأَرْضِ مُسْلِمٌ غَيْرِي وَغَيْرُكِ، فَانْطَلَقَ بِهَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ ثُمَّ قَامَ يُصَلِّي. فَلَمَّا أَنْ دَخَلَتْ عَلَيْهِ فَرَآهَا أَهْوَى إِلَيْهَا، فَتَنَاوَلَهَا، فَأُخِذَ أَخْذًا شَدِيدًا، فَقَالَ: ادْعِي اللَّهَ لِي وَلَا أَضُرُّكِ، فَدَعَتْ لَهُ فَأُرْسِلَ، فَأَهْوَى إِلَيْهَا، فَتَنَاوَلَهَا فَأُخِذَ بِمِثْلِهَا أَوْ أَشَدَّ. فَفَعَلَ ذَلِكَ الثَّالِثَةَ فَأُخِذَ، [فَذَكَرَ] مِثْلَ الْمَرَّتَيْنِ الْأُولَيَيْنِ فَقَالَ ادْعِي اللَّهَ فَلَا أَضُرُّكِ. فَدَعَتْ، لَهُ فَأُرْسِلَ، ثُمَّ دَعَا أَدْنَى حُجَّابِهِ، فَقَالَ: إِنَّكَ لَمْ تَأْتِنِي بِإِنْسَانٍ، وَإِنَّمَا أَتَيْتَنِي بِشَيْطَانٍ، أَخْرِجْهَا وَأَعْطِهَا هَاجَرَ، فَأُخْرِجَتْ وَأُعْطِيَتْ هَاجَرَ، فَأَقْبَلَتْ، فَلَمَّا أَحَسَّ إِبْرَاهِيمُ بِمَجِيئِهَا انْفَتَلَ مِنْ صِلَاتِهِ، قَالَ : مَهْيَم؟ قَالَتْ: كَفَى اللَّهُ كَيْدَ الْكَافِرِ الْفَاجِرِ، وَأَخْدَمَنِي هَاجَرَ" قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِيرِينَ وَكَانَ : أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ إِذَا حَدَّثَ بِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ قَالَ: فَتِلْكَ أُمُّكُمْ يَا بَنِي مَاءِ السَّمَاءِ

---

## 21:64-67 — verses 64-67 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the people of Ibrahim (peace be upon him) when he said to them what he said: {So they turned to themselves} that is, with blame for their failure to guard and watch over their gods, and they said: {Indeed, it is you who are the wrongdoers} that is, in leaving them neglected with no guardian beside them. {Then they were turned upside down upon their heads} that is, then they hung their heads down toward the ground and said: {You have certainly known that these do not speak}. Qatadah said: an evil bewilderment overtook the people, so they said: {You have certainly known that these do not speak}.

Al-Suddi said: {Then they were turned upside down upon their heads} means, in confusion (fitnah).

Ibn Zayd said: it means, in opinion.

The statement of Qatadah is clearer in meaning, because they only did that out of bewilderment and helplessness. This is why they said to him: {You have certainly known that these do not speak}, meaning: how can you say to us, "ask them, if they can speak," when you know that they do not speak? At that point, when they had acknowledged this, Ibrahim said to them: {Then do you worship, besides Allah, that which does not benefit you at all nor harm you} that is, since they do not speak, and they neither harm nor benefit, why then do you worship them besides Allah?

{Uff to you and to what you worship besides Allah. Then will you not use reason?}

That is: will you not reflect upon the misguidance and gross disbelief you are in, which can only be promoted upon an ignorant, wrongdoing, sinful person? So he established the proof against them and bound them to it. This is why the Almighty said: {And that was Our argument which We gave to Ibrahim against his people} [al-An'am: 83].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ قَوْمِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حِينَ قَالَ لَهُمْ مَا قَالَ: ﴿فَرَجَعُوا إِلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْمَلَامَةِ فِي عَدَمِ احْتِرَازِهِمْ وَحِرَاسَتِهِمْ لِآلِهَتِهِمْ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ أَنْتُمُ الظَّالِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي تَرْكِكِمْ لَهَا مُهْمَلَةً لَا حَافِظَ عِنْدَهَا، ﴿ثُمَّ نُكِسُوا عَلَى رُءُوسِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: ثُمَّ أَطْرَقُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ فَقَالُوا: ﴿لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا هَؤُلاءِ يَنْطِقُونَ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَدْرَكَتِ الْقَوْمَ حَيْرَةُ سُوءٍ فَقَالُوا: ﴿لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا هَؤُلاءِ يَنْطِقُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿ثُمَّ نُكِسُوا عَلَى رُءُوسِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْفِتْنَةِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: أَيْ فِي الرَّأْيِ.

وَقَوْلُ قَتَادَةَ أَظْهَرُ فِي الْمَعْنَى؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ إِنَّمَا فَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ حَيْرَةً وَعَجْزًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا لَهُ: ﴿لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا هَؤُلاءِ يَنْطِقُونَ﴾ ، فَكَيْفَ تَقُولُ لَنَا: سَلُوهُمْ إِنْ كَانُوا يَنْطِقُونَ، وَأَنْتَ تَعْلَمُ أَنَّهَا لَا تَنْطِقُ فَعِنْدَهَا قَالَ لَهُمْ إِبْرَاهِيمُ لَمَّا اعْتَرَفُوا بِذَلِكَ: ﴿أَفَتَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَنْفَعُكُمْ شَيْئًا وَلا يَضُرُّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا كَانَتْ لَا تَنْطِقُ ، وَهِيَ لَا تَضُرُّ وَلَا تَنْفَعُ، فَلِمَ تَعْبُدُونَهَا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ.

﴿أُفٍّ لَكُمْ وَلِمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ أَفَلا تَعْقِلُونَ﴾

أَيْ: أَفَلَا تَتَدَبَّرُونَ مَا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّلَالِ وَالْكُفْرِ الْغَلِيظِ، الَّذِي لَا يُرَوَّجُ إِلَّا عَلَى جَاهِلٍ ظَالِمٍ فَاجِرٍ؟ فَأَقَامَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْحُجَّةَ، وَأَلْزَمَهُمْ بِهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتِلْكَ حُجَّتُنَا آتَيْنَاهَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٨٣] .

---

## 21:68-70 — verses 68-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When their argument was refuted, their powerlessness became manifest, the truth appeared and falsehood was repelled, they resorted to using the authority of their kingship. They said: {Burn him and support your gods, if you are going to do anything.} They gathered a very great quantity of firewood. Al-Suddi said: to the point that if a woman fell ill, she would vow, if she recovered, to bring firewood for burning Ibrahim. Then they placed it in a hollow pit in the ground and set it ablaze, and it produced enormous sparks and a towering flame, the like of which had never been kindled before. They placed Ibrahim (peace be upon him) in the sling of a catapult, at the direction of a man from the desert Arabs of Persia, from the Kurds (Shu'ayb al-Jibba'i said his name was Haizun). God caused the earth to swallow him, so that he sinks into it continually until the Day of Resurrection. When they cast Ibrahim into the fire he said: "God is sufficient for me, and He is the best guardian," as al-Bukhari related from Ibn Abbas, who said: "God is sufficient for me, and He is the best guardian" was said by Ibrahim when he was cast into the fire, and it was said by Muhammad when it was said to them: {Indeed, the people have gathered against you, so fear them. But it increased them in faith, and they said, God is sufficient for us, and He is the best guardian} [Al Imran: 173].

Al-Hafiz Abu Ya'la said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "When Ibrahim (peace be upon him) was cast into the fire, he said: O God, You in heaven are One, and I on earth am one who worships You."

It is also related that when they began to bind him, he said: "There is no god but You, glory be to You, to You belongs all praise, and to You belongs all dominion, You have no partner."

Shu'ayb al-Jibba'i said: his age at that time was sixteen years. God knows best.

Some of the early scholars mentioned that Gabriel presented himself to him while he was in the air, and said: "Do you have any need?" He said: "Of you, no. [But of God, yes.]"

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said, and it is also related from Ibn Abbas: When Ibrahim was cast in, the keeper of the rain began saying, "When will I be commanded to send down rain?" He said: But the command of God came faster than his command. God, Mighty and Majestic, said: {O fire, be coolness and safety upon Ibrahim.} He said: there remained no fire on earth that was not extinguished.

Ka'b al-Ahbar said: no one benefited from fire that day, and the fire burned nothing of Ibrahim's except his bonds.

Al-Thawri related, from al-A'mash, from a shaykh, from Ali ibn Abi Talib, regarding {We said, O fire, be coolness and safety upon Ibrahim}: [he said: it grew so cold upon him that it nearly killed him, until it was said: {and safety}], meaning: do not harm him.

Ibn Abbas and Abu al-'Aliyah said: had God, Mighty and Majestic, not said {and safety}, its coldness would have harmed Ibrahim.

Juwaybir related from al-Dahhak, regarding {be coolness and safety upon Ibrahim}: he said, they built for him an enclosure of thick firewood and lit fire in it from every side, and he awoke unharmed by any of it, until God extinguished it. He said: and they mention that Gabriel was with him, wiping the sweat from his face, and nothing else touched him from it.

Al-Suddi said: the angel of shade was with him in it.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] al-Minhal ibn 'Amr said: I was informed that Ibrahim was cast into the fire, and he said: he remained in it either fifty or forty [days]. He said: I never spent days and nights more pleasant in living than when I was in it. I wish that all my life and living were like my living when I was in it.

Abu Zur'ah ibn 'Amr ibn Jarir related from Abu Hurayrah, who said: the best thing that the father of Ibrahim said, when the covering was lifted from him while he was in the fire, and he found him being sprinkled on his brow, was: "How excellent is the Lord, your Lord, O Ibrahim!"

Qatadah said: no creature came that day except that it worked to extinguish the fire away from him, except the gecko. Al-Zuhri said: the Prophet ﷺ commanded that it be killed and named it a "little corrupt one" (fuwaysiq).

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] the freedwoman of al-Fakih ibn al-Mughirah al-Makhzumi said: I entered upon Aishah and saw a spear in her house. I said: O Mother of the Believers, what do you do with this spear? She said: We kill these geckos with it. The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When Ibrahim was cast into the fire, there was no creature on earth except that it worked to extinguish the fire, except the gecko, for it used to blow on the fire toward Ibrahim." So the Messenger of God ﷺ commanded us to kill it.

Regarding His saying: {And they intended for him a plot, but We made them the greatest losers}, meaning: the defeated, the lowest, because they intended a plot against the Prophet of God, so God plotted against them and saved him from the fire, and they were defeated there.

Atiyyah al-'Awfi said: When Ibrahim was cast into the fire, their king came to look at him, and a spark flew and landed on his thumb, burning it like a tuft of wool.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا دَحَضت حُجَّتُهُمْ، وَبَانَ عَجْزُهُمْ، وَظَهَرَ الْحَقُّ، وَانْدَفَعَ الْبَاطِلُ، عَدَلُوا إِلَى اسْتِعْمَالِ جَاهِ مُلْكِهِمْ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿حَرِّقُوهُ وَانْصُرُوا آلِهَتَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ فَاعِلِينَ﴾ فَجَمَعُوا حَطَبًا كَثِيرًا جِدًّا -قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: حَتَّى إِنْ كَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ تَمْرَضُ، فَتَنْذُرُ إِنْ عُوفِيَتْ أَنْ تَحْمِلَ حَطَبًا لِحَرِيقِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ-ثُمَّ جَعَلُوهُ فِي جَوْبة مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، وَأَضْرَمُوهَا نَارًا، فَكَانَ لَهَا شَرَرٌ عَظِيمٌ وَلَهَبٌ مُرْتَفِعٌ، لَمْ تُوقَدْ قَطُّ نَارٌ مِثْلُهَا، وَجَعَلُوا إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي كِفَّةِ الْمَنْجَنِيقِ بِإِشَارَةِ رَجُلٍ مِنْ أَعْرَابِ فَارِسَ مِنَ الْأَكْرَادِ -قَالَ شُعَيب الْجِبَائِيُّ: اسْمُهُ هِيزُنُ-فَخَسَفَ اللَّهُ بِهِ الْأَرْضَ، فَهُوَ يَتَجَلْجَلُ فِيهَا إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَلَمَّا أَلْقَوْهُ قَالَ: "حَسْبِيَ اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ"، كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "حَسْبِي اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ" قَالَهَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ حِينَ أُلْقِيَ فِي النَّارِ، وَقَالَهَا مُحَمَّدٌ حِينَ قَالُوا: ﴿إِنَّ النَّاسَ قَدْ جَمَعُوا لَكُمْ فَاخْشَوْهُمْ فَزَادَهُمْ إِيمَانًا وَقَالُوا حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٧٣] .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ هِشَامٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم "لما أُلْقِيَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي النَّارِ قَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنَّكَ فِي السَّمَاءِ وَاحِدٌ، وَأَنَا فِي الْأَرْضِ وَاحِدٌ أَعْبُدُكَ" .

وَيُرْوَى أَنَّهُ لَمَّا جَعَلُوا يُوثِقُونَهُ قَالَ: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ لَكَ الْحَمْدُ، وَلَكَ الْمُلْكُ، لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ .

وَقَالَ شُعَيْبٌ الْجِبَائِيُّ: كَانَ عُمْرُهُ سِتَّ عَشْرَةَ سَنَةً. فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَذَكَرَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ أَنَّهُ عَرَضَ لَهُ جِبْرِيلُ وَهُوَ فِي الْهَوَاءِ، فَقَالَ: أَلِكَ حَاجَةٌ؟ فَقَالَ: أَمَّا إِلَيْكَ فَلَا [وَأَمَّا من الله فبلى] .

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ -وَيُرْوَى عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَيْضًا-قَالَ: لَمَّا أُلقيَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ جَعَلَ خَازِنُ الْمَطَرِ يَقُولُ: مَتَى أُومَرُ بِالْمَطَرِ فَأَرْسِلُهُ؟ قَالَ: فَكَانَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ أَسْرَعَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ: [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] ﴿يَا نَارُ كُونِي بَرْدًا وَسَلامًا عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ﴾ قَالَ: لَمْ يَبْقَ نَارٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ إِلَّا طُفِئَتْ.

وَقَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ: لَمْ يَنْتَفِعْ [أَحَدٌ] يَوْمَئِذٍ بِنَارٍ، وَلَمْ تُحْرِقِ النَّارُ مِنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ سِوَى وِثَاقِهِ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ شَيْخٍ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ: ﴿قُلْنَا يَا نَارُ كُونِي بَرْدًا وَسَلامًا عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ﴾ [قَالَ: بَرَدَتْ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى كَادَتْ تَقْتُلُهُ، حَتَّى قِيلَ: ﴿وَسَلامًا﴾ ] ، قَالَ: لَا تضرِّيه.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: لَوْلَا أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَسَلامًا﴾ لَآذَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ بَرْدُها.

وَقَالَ جُوَيبر، عَنِ الضَّحَّاكِ: ﴿كُونِي بَرْدًا وَسَلامًا عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ﴾ قَالَ: صَنَعُوا لَهُ حَظِيرَةً مِنْ حَطَب جَزْل، وَأَشْعَلُوا فِيهِ النَّارَ مِنْ كُلِّ جَانِبٍ، فَأَصْبَحَ وَلَمْ يصِبه مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ حَتَّى أَخْمَدَهَا اللَّهُ -قَالَ: وَيَذْكُرُونَ أَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ كَانَ مَعَهُ يَمْسَحُ وَجْهَهُ مِنَ الْعَرَقِ، فَلَمْ يُصِبْه مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ غيرُ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: كَانَ مَعَهُ فِيهَا مَلَكُ الظِّلِّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا يُوسُفُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا مِهْران، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي خَالِدٍ، عَنِ المِنْهَال بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: أَخُبِرْتُ أَنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ أُلْقِيَ فِي النَّارِ، فَقَالَ: كَانَ فِيهَا إِمَّا خَمْسِينَ وَإِمَّا أَرْبَعِينَ، قَالَ: مَا كُنْتُ أَيْامًا وَلَيَالِيَ قَطُّ أَطْيَبَ عَيْشًا إِذْ كُنْتُ فِيهَا، وَدِدْتُ أَنَّ عَيْشِي وَحَيَاتِي كُلَّهَا مِثْلُ عَيْشِي إِذْ كُنْتُ فِيهَا.

وَقَالَ أَبُو زُرْعَة بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: إِنَّ أَحْسَنَ [شَيْءٍ] قَالَ أَبُو إِبْرَاهِيمَ -لَمَّا رُفِعَ عنه الطبق وهو في النار، وجده يرش جَبِينُهُ-قَالَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: نعْمَ الرَّبُّ رَبُّكَ يَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: لَمْ يَأْتِ يَوْمَئِذٍ دَابَّةٌ إِلَّا أَطْفَأَتْ عَنْهُ النَّارَ، إِلَّا الوَزَغ -وَقَالَ الزُّهْرِيُّ: أَمَرَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: بِقَتْلِهِ وَسَمَّاهُ فُوَيْسِقًا .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ ابْنُ أَخِي ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنِي عَمِّي، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرُ بْنُ حَازِمٍ، أَنَّ نَافِعًا حَدَّثَهُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَتْنِي مَوْلَاةُ الْفَاكِهِ بْنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ الْمَخْزُومِيِّ قَالَتْ: دَخَلْتُ عَلَى عَائِشَةَ فَرَأَيْتُ فِي بَيْتِهَا رُمْحًا. فَقُلْتُ: يَا أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، مَا تَصْنَعِينَ بِهَذَا الرُّمْحِ؟ فَقَالَتْ: نَقْتُلُ بِهِ هَذِهِ الْأَوْزَاغَ، إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حِينَ أُلْقِيَ فِي النَّارِ، لَمْ يَكُنْ فِي الْأَرْضِ دَابَّةٌ إِلَّا تُطْفِئُ النَّارَ، غَيْرَ الوَزَغ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ يَنْفُخُ عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ"، فَأَمَرَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِقَتْلِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَرَادُوا بِهِ كَيْدًا فَجَعَلْنَاهُمُ الأخْسَرِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الْمَغْلُوبِينَ الْأَسْفَلِينَ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ أَرَادُوا بِنَبِيِّ اللَّهِ كَيْدًا، فَكَادَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَنَجَّاهُ مِنَ النَّارِ، فَغُلِبُوا هُنَالِكَ.

وَقَالَ عَطِيَّةُ الْعَوْفِيُّ: لَمَّا ألقِيَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ فِي النَّارِ، جَاءَ مَلِكُهُمْ لِيَنْظُرَ إِلَيْهِ فَطَارَتْ شَرَارَةٌ فَوَقَعَتْ عَلَى إِبْهَامِهِ، فَأَحْرَقَتْهُ مِثْلَ الصُّوفَةِ.

---

## 21:71-75 — verses 71-75 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about Ibrahim (peace be upon him), that Allah delivered him from the fire of his people, and brought him out from among them as an emigrant to the land of al-Sham, to the sanctified land within it, as al-Rabi' ibn Anas said, from Abu al-'Aliyah, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, concerning His saying: {to the land which We blessed for the worlds}, he said: al-Sham, and there is no sweet water except that it comes forth from beneath the Rock.

Abu al-'Aliyah said the same as well.

Qatadah said: he was in the land of Iraq, and Allah delivered him to al-Sham, [and al-Sham used to be called the pillar of the abode of migration, and whatever was diminished from the earth was added to al-Sham], and whatever was diminished from al-Sham was added to Palestine. It used to be said: it is the land of the gathering and the resurrection, and in it 'Isa son of Maryam (peace be upon him) will descend, and in it al-Masih al-Dajjal (the Antichrist) will perish.

Ka'b al-Ahbar said concerning His saying: {to the land which We blessed for the worlds}, that it means to Harran.

Al-Suddi said: Ibrahim and Lut set out toward al-Sham, and Ibrahim met Sarah, who was the daughter of the king of Harran. She had denounced her people over their religion, so he married her on condition that he would not change her.

Ibn Jarir related this, and it is gharib (a singular report) [and what is well known is that she was the daughter of his paternal uncle, and that he brought her out with him as an emigrant from his land].

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: to Makkah; do you not hear His saying: {Indeed, the first House established for mankind was that at Bakkah, blessed and a guidance for the worlds} [Al 'Imran: 96]?

And His saying: {And We granted him Ishaq and Ya'qub as nafilah (an additional gift)}. 'Ata' and Mujahid said: it means a gift.

Ibn 'Abbas, Qatadah, and al-Hakam ibn 'Uyaynah said: the nafilah is the child of the child, meaning that Ya'qub was born of Ishaq, as He said: {So We gave her glad tidings of Ishaq, and after Ishaq, of Ya'qub} [Hud: 71].

'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: he asked for one, saying: {My Lord, grant me one of the righteous} [al-Saffat: 100], so Allah gave him Ishaq and added Ya'qub for him as nafilah.

{And each of them We made righteous}, meaning: all of them were people of goodness and righteousness. {And We made them leaders}, meaning: to be followed as examples. {Guiding by Our command}, meaning: calling to Allah by His permission. Therefore He said: {And We inspired them to do good deeds, to establish prayer, and to give zakat}, this being a case of joining the specific to the general. {And they were worshippers of Us}, meaning: doers of what they commanded people to do.

Then He follows this by mentioning Lut, who is Lut son of Haran son of Azar. He had believed in Ibrahim, followed him, and emigrated with him, as the Almighty said: {So Lut believed him, and said: Indeed I am an emigrant to my Lord} [al-'Ankabut: 26]. So Allah gave him judgment and knowledge, and revealed to him, and made him a prophet, and sent him to Sodom and its surrounding settlements. But they opposed him and disbelieved him, so Allah destroyed them and brought ruin upon them, as He recounted their story in more than one place in His Mighty Book. Therefore He said: {And We delivered him from the town that used to commit vile deeds. Indeed, they were an evil, wicked people. And We admitted him into Our mercy; indeed, he was among the righteous}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، أَنَّهُ سَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ نَارِ قَوْمِهِ، وَأَخْرَجَهُ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ مُهَاجِرًا إِلَى بِلَادِ الشَّامِ، إِلَى الْأَرْضِ الْمُقَدَّسَةِ مِنْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عَنْ أبي بْنِ كَعْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِلَى الأرْضِ الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ قَالَ: الشَّامُ، وَمَا مِنْ مَاءٍ عَذْبٍ إِلَّا يَخْرُجُ مِنْ تَحْتِ الصَّخْرَةِ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ أَيْضًا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانَ بِأَرْضِ الْعِرَاقِ، فَأَنْجَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَى الشَّامِ، [وَكَانَ يُقَالُ لِلشَّامِ: عِمَادُ دَارِ الْهِجْرَةِ، وَمَا نَقَصَ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ زِيدَ فِي الشَّامِ] وَمَا نَقَصَ مِنَ الشَّامِ زِيدَ فِي فِلَسْطِينَ. وَكَانَ يُقَالُ: هِيَ أَرْضُ الْمَحْشَرِ وَالْمَنْشَرِ، وَبِهَا يَنْزِلُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَبِهَا يَهْلِكُ الْمَسِيحُ الدَّجَّالُ.

وَقَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِلَى الأرْضِ الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ إِلَى حَرَّانَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: انْطَلَقَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ وَلُوطٌ قِبَل الشَّامِ، فَلَقِيَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ سَارَةَ، وَهِيَ ابْنَةُ مَلِكِ حَرَّانَ، وَقَدْ طَعَنَتْ عَلَى قَوْمِهَا فِي دِينِهِمْ، فَتَزَوَّجَهَا عَلَى أَلَّا يُغَيِّرَهَا.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَهُوَ غَرِيبٌ [وَالْمَشْهُورُ أَنَّهَا ابْنَةُ عَمِّهِ، وَأَنَّهُ خَرَجَ بِهَا مُهَاجِرًا مِنْ بِلَادِهِ] .

وَقَالَ العَوفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِلَى مَكَّةَ؛ أَلَا تَسْمَعُ قَوْلَهُ: ﴿إِنَّ أَوَّلَ بَيْتٍ وُضِعَ لِلنَّاسِ لَلَّذِي بِبَكَّةَ مُبَارَكًا وَهُدًى لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:٩٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ نَافِلَةً﴾ قَالَ عَطَاءٌ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ: عَطِيَّةً.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالْحَكَمُ بْنُ عُيينة: النَّافِلَةُ وَلَدُ الْوَلَدِ، يَعْنِي: أَنَّ يَعْقُوبَ وَلَدَ إِسْحَاقَ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَبَشَّرْنَاهَا بِإِسْحَاقَ وَمِنْ وَرَاءِ إِسْحَاقَ يَعْقُوبَ﴾ [هُودٍ:٧١] .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: سَأَلَ وَاحِدًا فَقَالَ: ﴿رَبِّ هَبْ لِي مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:١٠٠] ، فَأَعْطَاهُ اللَّهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَزَادَهُ يَعْقُوبَ نَافِلَةً.

﴿وَكُلا جَعَلْنَا صَالِحِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَمِيعُ أَهْلُ خَيْرٍ وَصَلَاحٍ، ﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ أَئِمَّةً﴾ أَيْ: يُقْتَدَى بِهِمْ، ﴿يَهْدُونَ بِأَمْرِنَا﴾ أَيْ: يَدْعُونَ إِلَى اللَّهِ بِإِذْنِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَوْحَيْنَا إِلَيْهِمْ فِعْلَ الْخَيْرَاتِ وَإِقَامَ الصَّلاةِ وَإِيتَاءَ الزَّكَاةِ﴾ مِنْ بَابِ عَطْفِ الْخَاصِّ عَلَى الْعَامِّ، ﴿وَكَانُوا لَنَا عَابِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَاعِلِينَ لِمَا يَأْمُرُونَ النَّاسَ بِهِ.

ثُمَّ عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ لُوطٍ -وَهُوَ لُوطُ بْنُ هَارَانَ بْنِ آزَرَ-كَانَ قَدْ آمَنَ بِإِبْرَاهِيمَ، وَاتَّبَعَهُ، وَهَاجَرَ مَعَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَآمَنَ لَهُ لُوطٌ وَقَالَ إِنِّي مُهَاجِرٌ إِلَى رَبِّي﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ:٢٦] ، فَآتَاهُ اللَّهُ حُكْمًا وَعِلْمًا، وَأَوْحَى إِلَيْهِ، وَجَعَلَهُ نَبِيًّا، وَبَعَثَهُ إِلَى سَدُومَ وَأَعْمَالِهَا، فَخَالَفُوهُ وَكَذَّبُوهُ، فَأَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ ودَمَّر عَلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا قَصَّ خَبَرَهُمْ فِي غَيْرِ مَوْضِعٍ مِنْ كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَنَجَّيْنَاهُ مِنَ الْقَرْيَةِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ تَعْمَلُ الْخَبَائِثَ إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَوْمَ سَوْءٍ فَاسِقِينَ * وَأَدْخَلْنَاهُ فِي رَحْمَتِنَا إِنَّهُ مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ﴾ .

---

## 21:76-77 — verses 76-77 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of His answering His servant and messenger Noah, peace be upon him, when he supplicated against his people after they had denied him: {So he called upon his Lord, "I am overcome, so help me"} [al-Qamar: 10], and {Noah said, "My Lord, do not leave upon the earth any dweller among the disbelievers. Indeed, if You leave them, they will mislead Your servants and will not beget except a wicked one, a disbeliever"} [Nuh: 26, 27]. This is why He says here: {When he called out before, and We answered him and saved him and his family}, meaning those who believed in him, as He said: {and your family, except those upon whom the word has already gone forth, and whoever believed; and none believed with him except a few} [Hud: 40].

His saying: {from the great distress}, means from the hardship, the denial, and the harm he suffered. For he remained among them a thousand years less fifty, calling them to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, and none of them believed except a few. They used to seek him out to harm him, and they enjoined one another, generation after generation, age after age, to oppose him.

His saying: {and We aided him against the people}, means We rescued him and delivered him victorious over the people {who denied Our signs. Indeed, they were an evil people, so We drowned them all together}, meaning Allah destroyed them all, and did not leave a single one of them upon the face of the earth, since their prophet had supplicated against them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ اسْتِجَابَتِهِ لِعَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حِينَ دَعَا عَلَى قَوْمِهِ لَمَّا كَذَّبُوهُ: ﴿فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ أَنِّي مَغْلُوبٌ فَانْتَصِرْ﴾ [القمر:١٠] ، ﴿وَقَالَ نُوحٌ رَبِّ لَا تَذَرْ عَلَى الأرْضِ مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ دَيَّارًا. إِنَّكَ إِنْ تَذَرْهُمْ يُضِلُّوا عِبَادَكَ وَلا يَلِدُوا إِلا فَاجِرًا كَفَّارًا﴾ [نُوحٍ:٢٦، ٢٧] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿إِذْ نَادَى مِنْ قَبْلُ فَاسْتَجَبْنَا لَهُ فَنَجَّيْنَاهُ وَأَهْلَهُ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِهِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَهْلَكَ إِلا مَنْ سَبَقَ عَلَيْهِ الْقَوْلُ وَمَنْ آمَنَ وَمَا آمَنَ مَعَهُ إِلا قَلِيلٌ﴾ [هُودٍ:٤٠] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مِنَ الْكَرْبِ الْعَظِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الشِّدَّةِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ وَالْأَذَى، فَإِنَّهُ لَبِثَ فِيهِمْ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ إِلَّا خَمْسِينَ عَامًا يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِهِ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا الْقَلِيلُ، وَكَانُوا يَقْصِدُونَ لِأَذَاهُ وَيَتَوَاصَوْنَ قَرْنًا بَعْدَ قَرْنٍ، وَجِيلًا بَعْدَ جِيلٍ عَلَى خِلَافِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَصَرْنَاهُ مِنَ الْقَوْمِ﴾ أَيْ: وَنَجَّيْنَاهُ وَخَلَّصْنَاهُ مُنْتَصِرًا مِنَ الْقَوْمِ ﴿الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَوْمَ سَوْءٍ فَأَغْرَقْنَاهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِعَامَّةٍ، وَلَمْ يُبْقِ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ منهم أحدًا؛ إذ دعا عليهم نبيهم.

---

## 21:78-82 — verses 78-82 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ibn Ishaq said, from Murrah, from Ibn Mas'ud: that cultivated field was a vineyard whose clusters had grown. Shurayh said the same.

Ibn Abbas said: al-nafsh (nafsh) means grazing.

Shurayh, al-Zuhri, and Qatadah said: nafsh occurs at night. Qatadah added: and al-haml (haml) occurs during the day.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb and Harun ibn Idris al-Asamm told us, they said al-Muharibi told us, from Ash'ath, from Abu Ishaq, from Murrah, from Ibn Mas'ud, concerning His saying {And David and Solomon, when they judged concerning the field, when the people's sheep grazed therein at night}: he said, it was a vineyard whose clusters had grown, and the sheep ruined it. He said: David ruled that the sheep should go to the owner of the vineyard. Solomon said: something other than this, O Prophet of Allah! He said: What is that? He said: You give the vineyard to the owner of the sheep, so that he tends it until it returns to how it was, and you give the sheep to the owner of the vineyard so that he benefits from them, until, when the vineyard has returned to how it was, you give the vineyard back to its owner and give the sheep back to their owner. That is the meaning of His saying: {So We made Solomon understand it}.

Al-'Awfi related likewise from Ibn Abbas.

Hammad ibn Salamah said, from Ali ibn Zayd, Khalifah told us, from Ibn Abbas, who said: David ruled that the sheep should go to the owners of the field. The shepherds went out, and the dogs went with them. Solomon said to them: How did he rule between you? They told him, and he said: Had I been given charge of your matter I would have ruled otherwise than this! David was informed of this, so he summoned him and said: How would you judge between them? He said: I would give the sheep to the owner of the field, so that its offspring, milk, clarified butter, and other benefits would be his, and the owners of the sheep would sow for the people of the field the equivalent of their crop. Then, when the crop had reached the state it had been in, the owners of the field would take the crop and return the sheep to their owners.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father told us, Sa'id ibn Sulayman told us, Khudayj told us, from Abu Ishaq, from Murrah, from Masruq, who said: the field into which the sheep grazed at night was in fact a vineyard into which the sheep grazed, leaving neither leaf nor cluster of grapes without eating it. They came to David, and he awarded them ownership of the sheep themselves. Solomon said: No, rather the sheep should be taken and given to the people of the vineyard, so that its milk and benefit would be theirs, and the people of the sheep should be given the vineyard so that they might repair it and restore it until it returned to how it had been on the night the sheep grazed in it. Then the people of the sheep would be given back their sheep, and the people of the vineyard their vineyard.

Shurayh, Murrah, Mujahid, Qatadah, Ibn Zayd, and others said the same.

Ibn Jarir said: Ibn Abi Ziyad told us, Yazid ibn Harun told us, Isma'il informed us, from 'Amir, who said: two men came to Shurayh, and one of them said: this man's sheep cut through some yarn of mine. Shurayh said: was it by day or by night? For if it was by day, the owner of the sheep is free of liability, but if it was by night, he is liable. Then he recited {And David and Solomon, when they judged concerning the field, when [the sheep] grazed therein}, the verse.

What Shurayh said resembles what Imam Ahmad, Abu Dawud, and Ibn Majah related, from the hadith of al-Layth ibn Sa'd, from al-Zuhri, from Haram ibn Muhayyisah: that the she-camel of al-Bara' ibn 'Azib entered an enclosed garden and caused damage in it, so the Messenger of Allah ﷺ ruled that the owners of gardens must guard them during the day, and whatever livestock damage occurs at night, its owners are liable for it. This hadith has been criticized for a defect, and we have discussed it at length in the Book of Rulings (al-Ahkam). And success is with Allah.

Concerning His saying {So We made Solomon understand it, and to each We gave judgment and knowledge}, Ibn Abi Hatim said:

my father told us, Musa ibn Isma'il told us, Hammad told us, from Humayd: that when Iyas ibn Mu'awiyah was appointed a judge, al-Hasan came to him and wept. He said: what makes you weep? He said: O Abu Sa'id, it has reached me that judges are of three kinds: a man who exerts effort and errs, he is in the Fire; a man swayed by desire, he is in the Fire; and a man who exerts effort and is correct, he is in Paradise. Al-Hasan al-Basri said: In what Allah has related of the story of David and Solomon (peace be upon them) and the prophets, there is a ruling that refutes what these people say. Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And David and Solomon, when they judged concerning the field, when the people's sheep grazed therein, and We were witnesses to their judgment}. Allah praised Solomon and did not blame David. Then he (al-Hasan) said: Allah has imposed three conditions upon judges: that they not sell it for a small price, that they not follow desire in it, and that they fear no one in it. Then he recited {O David, indeed We have made you a successor upon the earth, so judge between the people in truth and do not follow desire, lest it lead you astray from the path of Allah} [Sad: 26], and He said {So do not fear the people but fear Me} [al-Ma'idah: 44], and He said {And do not sell My verses for a small price} [al-Ma'idah: 44].

I say: as for the prophets (peace be upon them), all of them are infallible, supported by Allah, Mighty and Majestic is He. There is no disagreement about this among the verifying scholars, whether of the earlier or later generations. As for those other than them, it is established in Sahih al-Bukhari, from 'Amr ibn al-'As, that he said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When a judge exerts effort and is correct, he has two rewards, and when he exerts effort and errs, he has one reward." This hadith explicitly refutes what Iyas imagined, that a judge who exerts effort and errs is in the Fire. And Allah knows best.

And in the Sunan: "Judges are of three kinds: one judge in Paradise, and two judges in the Fire. A man who knows the truth and rules by it, he is in Paradise. A man who judges between people out of ignorance, he is in the Fire. And a man who knows the truth and rules contrary to it, he is in the Fire."

Similar to this story mentioned in the Qur'an is what Imam Ahmad related in his Musnad, where he said: 'Ali ibn Hafs told us, Warqa' informed us, from Abu al-Zinad, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "While two women, each with a son of hers, were together, a wolf came and took one of the two boys. They brought their dispute to David, and he ruled in favor of the elder woman, and they left. Solomon then summoned them and said: bring me the knife, I will cut him in two between them. The younger woman said: may Allah have mercy on you, he is her son, do not cut him. So he ruled in favor of the younger woman."

Al-Bukhari and Muslim included it in their Sahihs, and al-Nasa'i placed a chapter heading on it in the Book of Judgments: "Chapter: the judge implying a ruling contrary to the true one in order to elicit the truth."

Likewise the story related by the Hafiz Abu al-Qasim ibn 'Asakir in the biography of "Solomon (peace be upon him)" in his history, by the route of al-Hasan ibn Sufyan, from Safwan ibn Salih, from al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Sa'id ibn Bishr, from Qatadah, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas, who mentioned a lengthy story, the summary of which is: that a beautiful woman in the time of the Children of Israel was solicited by four of their chiefs, and she refused each of them. So they agreed among themselves against her, and testified against her before David (peace be upon him) that she had allowed a dog of hers, which she had accustomed to this from her, to have intercourse with her. So he ordered that she be stoned. When the evening of that day came, Solomon sat, and children gathered with him, like him in age, and he set himself up as judge. Four of them dressed themselves in the guise of those men, and another in the guise of the woman, and they testified against her that she had allowed a dog to have intercourse with her. Solomon said: separate them from one another. He said to the first of them: what was the color of the dog? He said: black. So he set him aside, and summoned the next and asked him about its color, and he said: red. And the next said: dusky. And the next said: white. So he ordered that they be killed. This was related to David, who at once summoned those four men and asked them separately about the color of that dog, and they disagreed among themselves, so he ordered that they be killed.

Concerning His saying {And We subjected the mountains to glorify Us along with David, and the birds as well, and We were the ones who did that}: this was because of the beauty of his voice in reciting his scripture, the Psalms (al-Zabur). When he chanted it, the birds would stop in the air and respond to him in unison, and the mountains would echo back to him at both ends of the day. For this reason, when the Prophet ﷺ passed by Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, who was reciting the Qur'an at night, and he had a very beautiful voice, he stopped and listened to his recitation, and said: "This man has been given one of the flutes (mazamir) of the family of David." He said: O Messenger of Allah, had I known you were listening, I would have adorned it for you most beautifully.

Abu 'Uthman al-Nahdi said: I never heard the sound of a cymbal, nor a lute, nor a flute, like the voice of Abu Musa, may Allah be pleased with him. And yet it was said of him: he has been given a flute among the flutes of the family of David.

Concerning His saying {And We taught him the making of coats of armor for you, that they might protect you from your [enemy in] battle}...

That is, the making of coats of mail.

Qatadah said: coats of mail before him were only flat plates, and he was the first to link them into rings. As He, exalted is He, said: {And We softened iron for him. Make full coats of mail and measure well the links} [Saba: 10, 11], meaning: do not make the ring too wide so that the nail becomes loose, and do not make the nail too thick so that it tears the ring. That is why He said: {that it may protect you from your violence [in battle]}, meaning: in fighting, {so will you be grateful?}, meaning: for the favor of Allah upon you, in what He inspired to His servant David, teaching him that for your sake.

His saying: {And to Solomon [We subjected] the wind, forceful} means: We subjected to Solomon the forceful wind, {running by his command to the land which We had blessed}, meaning the land of Syria, {and We are ever knowing of all things}. This was because he had a wooden platform, upon which was placed everything he needed of the affairs of the kingdom, horses, camels, tents, and soldiers. Then he would command the wind to lift it, so it would enter beneath it, then lift it up and carry it, while the birds shaded him from the heat, to wherever he wished on earth. Then he would descend, and its equipment and wood would be set down. Allah, exalted is He, said: {So We subjected to him the wind, blowing gently by his command wherever he directed} [Sad: 36], and He said: {Its morning course was a month's journey and its afternoon course was a month's journey} [Saba: 12].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: it was mentioned from Sufyan ibn Uyaynah, from Abu Sinan, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: six hundred thousand seats used to be set up for Solomon. The believers among mankind would sit closest to him, then behind them would sit the believers among the jinn, then he would command the birds to shade them, then he would command the wind, and it would carry him, peace be upon him.

Abdullah ibn Ubayd ibn Umayr said: Solomon would command the wind, and it would gather like a great mountain mass, like a mountain, then he would order his carpet to be set upon the highest place of it, then he would call for a winged horse, which would rise until it ascended upon his carpet, then he would command the wind, and it would rise with him past every high point beneath the sky, while he kept his head lowered, not turning right or left, out of reverence for Allah, mighty and majestic is He, and out of gratitude, knowing how small was his portion within the dominion of Allah, exalted is He, until the wind set him down wherever it wished to set him down.

His saying: {And of the devils were those who dived for him} means: in the water, extracting pearls and other things. {And did work besides that}, meaning: other than that, as He, exalted is He, said: {and the devils, every builder and diver, and others bound together in shackles} [Sad: 37, 38].

His saying: {and We were guardians for them} means: Allah guarded him so that none of the devils could reach him with harm. Rather, all of them were within His grasp and under His subjugation, none of them daring to draw near to him or approach him. Rather, he had authority over them: if he wished, he released, and if he wished, he confined whichever of them he wished. That is why He said: {and others bound together in shackles}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُرّة، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: كَانَ ذَلِكَ الْحَرْثُ كَرْمًا قَدْ نَبَتَتْ عَنَاقِيدُهُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ شُرَيْح.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: النَّفْشُ: الرَّعْيُ.

وَقَالَ شُرَيح، وَالزُّهْرِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ: النَّفْشُ بِاللَّيْلِ. زَادَ قَتَادَةُ: والهَمْلُ بِالنَّهَارِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْب وَهَارُونُ بْنُ إدريسَ الْأَصَمُّ قَالَا حدثنا المحاربي، عن أشعت، عَنِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُرّة، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَدَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ إِذْ يَحْكُمَانِ فِي الْحَرْثِ إِذْ نَفَشَتْ فِيهِ غَنَمُ الْقَوْمِ﴾ قَالَ: كَرْمٌ قَدْ أَنْبَتَتْ عَنَاقِيدُهُ، فَأَفْسَدَتْهُ. قَالَ: فَقَضَى دَاوُدُ بالغَنَم لِصَاحِبِ الكَرْم، فَقَالَ سُلَيْمَانُ: غيرُ هَذَا يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ! قَالَ: وَمَا ذَاكَ؟ قَالَ: تَدْفَعُ الْكَرْمَ إِلَى صَاحِبِ الْغَنَمِ، فَيَقُومُ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى يَعُودَ كَمَا كَانَ، وَتَدْفَعُ الْغَنَمَ إِلَى صَاحِبِ الْكَرْمِ فيُصيب مِنْهَا حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ الْكَرْمُ كَمَا كَانَ دَفَعْتَ الْكَرْمَ إِلَى صَاحِبِهِ، وَدَفَعْتَ الْغَنَمَ إِلَى صَاحِبِهَا، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَفَهَّمْنَاهَا سُلَيْمَانَ﴾ .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ.

وَقَالَ حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا خَلِيفَةُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: فَحَكَمَ دَاوُدُ بِالْغَنَمِ لِأَصْحَابِ الْحَرْثِ، فَخَرَجَ الرِّعاء مَعَهُمُ الْكِلَابُ، فَقَالَ لَهُمْ سُلَيْمَانُ: كَيْفَ قَضَى بَيْنَكُمْ؟

فَأَخْبَرُوهُ، فَقَالَ: لَوْ وَلَيْتُ أَمْرَكُمْ لقضيتُ بِغَيْرِ هَذَا! فَأُخْبِرَ بِذَلِكَ دَاوُدُ، فَدَعَاهُ فَقَالَ: كَيْفَ تَقْضِي بَيْنَهُمْ؟ قَالَ أَدْفَعُ الْغَنَمَ إِلَى صَاحِبِ الْحَرْثِ، فَيَكُونُ لَهُ أَوْلَادُهَا وَأَلْبَانُهَا وَسِلَاؤُهَا وَمَنَافِعُهَا ويبذُر أَصْحَابُ الْغَنَمِ لِأَهْلِ الْحَرْثِ مثلَ حَرْثِهِمْ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ الْحَرْثُ الَّذِي كَانَ عَلَيْهِ أَخَذَ أَصْحَابُ الْحَرْثِ الحرثَ وَرَدُّوا الْغَنَمَ إِلَى أَصْحَابِهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا خُدَيْج، عَنِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُرَّة، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ قَالَ: الْحَرْثُ الَّذِي نَفَشَتْ فِيهِ الْغَنَمُ إِنَّمَا كَانَ كَرْمًا نَفَشَتْ فِيهِ الْغَنَمُ، فَلَمْ تَدَع فِيهِ وَرَقَةً وَلَا عُنْقُودًا مِنْ عِنَبٍ إِلَّا أَكَلَتْهُ، فَأَتَوْا دَاوُدَ، فَأَعْطَاهُمْ رِقَابَهَا، فَقَالَ سُلَيْمَانُ: لَا بَلْ تُؤْخَذُ الْغَنَمُ فَيُعْطَاهَا أهلُ الْكَرْمِ، فَيَكُونُ لَهُمْ لَبَنُهَا وَنَفْعُهَا، وَيُعْطَى أَهْلُ الْغَنَمِ الْكَرْمَ فَيُصْلِحُوهُ وَيُعَمِّرُوهُ حَتَّى يَعُودَ كَالَّذِي كَانَ لَيْلَةَ نَفَشت فِيهِ الْغَنَمُ، ثُمَّ يُعطَى أهل الغنم غنمهم، وأهل الكرم كرمهم.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ شُرَيح، ومُرَّة، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَنْبَأَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ، عَنْ عَامِرٍ، قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلَانِ إِلَى شُرَيح، فَقَالَ أَحَدُهُمَا: إِنَّ شَاةَ هَذَا قَطَعَتْ غَزَلًا لِي، فَقَالَ شُرَيْحٌ: نَهَارًا أَمْ لَيْلًا؟ فَإِنْ كَانَ نَهَارًا فَقَدْ بَرِئَ صَاحِبُ الشَّاةِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ لَيْلًا ضَمِن، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿وَدَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ إِذْ يَحْكُمَانِ فِي الْحَرْثِ إِذْ نَفَشَتْ فِيهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ شُرَيح شَبِيهٌ بِمَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ اللَّيْثِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ حَرام بْنِ مُحَيْصة ؛ أَنَّ نَاقَةَ الْبَرَاءِ بْنِ عَازِبٍ دَخَلَتْ حَائِطًا، فَأَفْسَدَتْ فِيهِ، فَقَضَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَى أَهْلِ الْحَوَائِطِ حِفْظَهَا بِالنَّهَارِ، وَمَا أَفْسَدَتِ الْمَوَاشِي بِاللَّيْلِ ضَامِنٌ عَلَى أَهْلِهَا . وَقَدْ عُلِّل هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ، وَقَدْ بَسَطْنَا الْكَلَامَ عَلَيْهِ فِي كِتَابِ "الْأَحْكَامِ" وَبِاللَّهِ التَّوْفِيقُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَفَهَّمْنَاهَا سُلَيْمَانَ وَكُلا آتَيْنَا حُكْمًا وَعِلْمًا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ؛ أَنَّ إِيَاسَ بْنَ مُعَاوِيَةَ لَمَّا اسْتَقْضَى أَتَاهُ الْحَسَنُ فَبَكَى، قَالَ مَا يُبْكِيكَ؟ قَالَ يَا أَبَا سَعِيدٍ، بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ الْقُضَاةَ: رَجُلٌ اجْتَهَدَ فَأَخَطَأَ، فَهُوَ فِي النَّارِ، وَرَجُلٌ مَالَ بِهِ الْهَوَى فَهُوَ فِي النَّارِ، وَرَجُلٌ اجْتَهَدَ فَأَصَابَ فَهُوَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ. فَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: إِنَّ فِيمَا قَصَّ اللَّهُ مَنْ نَبَأِ دَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، وَالْأَنْبِيَاءِ حُكْمًا يَرُدُّ قَوْلَ هَؤُلَاءِ النَّاسِ عَنْ قَوْلِهِمْ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَدَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ إِذْ يَحْكُمَانِ فِي الْحَرْثِ إِذْ نَفَشَتْ فِيهِ غَنَمُ الْقَوْمِ وَكُنَّا لِحُكْمِهِمْ شَاهِدِينَ﴾ فَأَثْنَى اللَّهُ عَلَى سُلَيْمَانَ وَلَمْ يَذُمَّ دَاوُدَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ -يَعْنِي: الْحَسَنَ-: إِنَّ اللَّهَ اتَّخَذَ عَلَى الْحُكَمَاءِ ثَلَاثًا: لَا يَشْتَرُونَ بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا وَلَا يَتَّبِعُونَ فِيهِ الْهَوَى، وَلَا يَخْشَوْنَ فِيهِ أَحَدًا، ثُمَّ تَلَا ﴿يَا دَاوُدُ إِنَّا جَعَلْنَاكَ خَلِيفَةً فِي الأرْضِ فَاحْكُمْ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ بِالْحَقِّ وَلا تَتَّبِعِ الْهَوَى فَيُضِلَّكَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ] ﴾ [ص:٢٦] وَقَالَ: ﴿فَلا تَخْشَوُا النَّاسَ وَاخْشَوْنِ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٤٤] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَلا تَشْتَرُوا بِآيَاتِي ثَمَنًا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٤٤] .

قُلْتُ: أَمَّا الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، فَكُلُّهُمْ مَعْصُومُونَ مُؤيَّدون مِنَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. وَهَذَا مِمَّا لَا خِلَافَ فِيهِ بَيْنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ الْمُحَقِّقِينَ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ، وَأَمَّا مَنْ سِوَاهُمْ فَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا اجْتَهَدَ الْحَاكِمُ فَأَصَابَ فَلَهُ أجران، وَإِذَا اجْتَهَدَ فَأَخْطَأَ فَلَهُ أَجْرٌ" فَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ يَرُدُّ نَصًّا مَا تَوَهَّمَهُ "إِيَاسٌ" مِنْ أَنَّ الْقَاضِيَ إِذَا اجْتَهَدَ فَأَخَطَأَ فَهُوَ فِي النَّارِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَفِي السُّنَنِ: "الْقُضَاةُ ثَلَاثَةٌ: قَاضٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَقَاضِيَانِ فِي النَّارِ: رَجُلٌ عَلِمَ الْحَقَّ وَقَضَى بِهِ فَهُوَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَرَجُلٌ حَكَمَ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ عَلَى جَهْلٍ فَهُوَ فِي النَّارِ، وَرَجُلٌ عَلِمَ الْحَقَّ وَقَضَى بِخِلَافِهِ، فَهُوَ فِي النَّارِ .

وَقَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ الْمَذْكُورَةِ فِي الْقُرْآنِ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ حَفْص، أَخْبَرَنَا وَرْقاء عَنْ أَبِي الزِّنَاد، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "بَيْنَمَا امْرَأَتَانِ مَعَهُمَا ابْنَانِ لَهُمَا، جَاءَ الذِّئْبُ فَأَخَذَ أَحَدَ الِابْنَيْنِ، فَتَحَاكَمَتَا إِلَى دَاوُدَ، فَقَضَى بِهِ لِلْكُبْرَى، فَخَرَجَتَا. فَدَعَاهُمَا سُلَيْمَانُ فَقَالَ: هَاتُوا السِّكِّينَ أَشُقُّهُ بَيْنَهُمَا، فَقَالَتِ الصُّغْرَى: يَرْحَمُكَ اللَّهُ هُوَ ابْنُهَا، لَا تَشُقه، فَقَضَى بِهِ لِلصُّغْرَى" .

وَأَخْرَجَهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ في صحيحهما وَبَوَّبَ عَلَيْهِ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي كِتَابِ الْقَضَاءِ: (بَابُ الْحَاكِمُ يُوهِمُ خِلَافَ الْحُكْمِ لِيَسْتَعْلِمَ الْحَقَّ) .

وَهَكَذَا القصة التي أوردها الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ بْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ" مِنْ تَارِيخِهِ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ بِشْرٍ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ -فَذَكَرَ قِصَّةً مُطَوَّلَةً مُلَخَّصُهَا-: أَنَّ امْرَأَةً حَسْنَاءَ فِي زَمَانِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، رَاوَدَهَا عَنْ نَفْسِهَا أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنْ رُؤَسَائِهِمْ، فَامْتَنَعَتْ عَلَى كُلٍّ مِنْهُمْ، فَاتَّفَقُوا فِيمَا بَيْنَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا، فَشَهِدُوا عَلَيْهَا عِنْدَ دَاوُدَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهَا مَكَّنت مِنْ نَفْسِهَا كَلْبًا لَهَا، قَدْ عَوَّدَتْهُ ذَلِكَ مِنْهَا، فَأَمَرَ بِرَجْمِهَا. فَلَمَّا كَانَ عَشِيَّةَ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمِ، جَلَسَ سُلَيْمَانُ، وَاجْتَمَعَ مَعَهُ وِلْدانٌ، مِثْلُهُ، فَانْتَصَبَ حَاكِمًا وَتَزَيَّا أَرْبَعَةٌ مِنْهُمْ بِزِيِّ أُولَئِكَ، وَآخَرُ بِزِيِّ الْمَرْأَةِ، وَشَهِدُوا عَلَيْهَا بِأَنَّهَا مكَنت مِنْ نَفْسِهَا كَلْبًا، فَقَالَ سُلَيْمَانُ: فَرِّقُوا بَيْنَهُمْ. فَقَالَ لِأَوَّلِهِمْ: مَا كَانَ لَوْنُ الْكَلْبِ؟ فَقَالَ: أَسْوَدُ. فَعَزَلَهُ، وَاسْتَدْعَى الْآخَرَ فَسَأَلَهُ عَنْ لَوْنِهِ، فَقَالَ: أَحْمَرُ. وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ: أَغْبَشُ. وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ: أَبْيَضُ. فَأَمَرَ بِقَتْلِهِمْ، فَحُكِيَ ذَلِكَ لِدَاوُدَ، فَاسْتَدْعَى مِنْ فَوْرِهِ بِأُولَئِكَ الْأَرْبَعَةِ، فَسَأَلَهُمْ مُتَفَرِّقِينَ عَنْ لَوْنِ ذَلِكَ الْكَلْبِ، فَاخْتَلَفُوا عَلَيْهِ، فأمر بقتلهم .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَسَخَّرْنَا مَعَ دَاوُدَ الْجِبَالَ يُسَبِّحْنَ وَالطَّيْرَ وَكُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ﴾ : وَذَلِكَ لِطِيبِ صَوْتِهِ بِتِلَاوَةِ كِتَابِهِ الزَّبُورِ، وَكَانَ إِذَا تَرَنَّم بِهِ تَقِفُ الطَّيْرُ فِي الْهَوَاءِ، فَتُجَاوِبُهُ، وتَرد عَلَيْهِ الْجِبَالُ تَأْوِيبًا؛ وَلِهَذَا لمَّا مَرَّ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ عَلَى أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، وَهُوَ يَتْلُو الْقُرْآنَ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ، وَكَانَ لَهُ صَوْتٌ طَيِّبٌ [جَدًا] . فَوَقَفَ وَاسْتَمَعَ لِقِرَاءَتِهِ، وَقَالَ: "لَقَدْ أُوتِيَ هَذَا مَزَامِيرَ آلِ دَاوُدَ". قَالَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَوْ عَلِمْتُ أَنَّكَ تَسْمَعُ لِحَبَّرْتُهُ لَكَ تَحْبِيرًا .

وَقَالَ أَبُو عُثْمَانَ النَّهْدِيُّ: مَا سَمِعْتُ صَوْتَ صَنْج وَلَا بَرَبْطَ وَلَا مِزْمَارٍ مِثْلَ صَوْتِ أَبِي مُوسَى رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَمَعَ هَذَا قَالَ: لَقَدْ أُوتِيَ مِزْمَارًا مِنْ مَزَامِيرِ آلِ دَاوُدَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَلَّمْنَاهُ صَنْعَةَ لَبُوسٍ لَكُمْ لِيُحْصِنَكُمْ مِنْ بَأْسِكُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي صَنْعَةَ الدُّرُوعِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: إِنَّمَا كَانَتِ الدُّرُوعُ قَبْلَهُ صَفَائِحَ، وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ سَرَدَهَا حلَقًا. كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَلَنَّا لَهُ الْحَدِيدَ. أَنِ اعْمَلْ سَابِغَاتٍ وَقَدِّرْ فِي السَّرْدِ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:١٠، ١١] أَيْ: لَا تُوَسِّعِ الْحَلْقَةَ فَتُقْلِقَ الْمِسْمَارَ، وَلَا تُغْلِظِ الْمِسْمَارَ فتَقَدّ الحَلْقة؛ وَلِهَذَا قال: ﴿لِيُحْصِنَكُمْ مِنْ بَأْسِكُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: فِي الْقِتَالِ، ﴿فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ شَاكِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: نِعَمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ، لِمَا أَلْهَمَ بِهِ عَبْدَهُ دَاوُدَ، فَعَلَّمَهُ ذَلِكَ مِنْ أَجْلِكُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلِسُلَيْمَانَ الرِّيحَ عَاصِفَةً﴾ أَيْ: وَسَخَّرْنَا لِسُلَيْمَانَ الرِّيحَ الْعَاصِفَةَ، ﴿تَجْرِي بِأَمْرِهِ إِلَى الأرْضِ الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا﴾ يَعْنِي أَرْضَ الشَّامِ، ﴿وَكُنَّا بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَالِمِينَ﴾ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ لَهُ بِسَاطٌ مِنْ خَشَبٍ، يُوضَعُ عَلَيْهِ كُلُّ مَا يَحْتَاجُ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ أُمُورِ الْمَمْلَكَةِ، وَالْخَيْلِ وَالْجِمَالِ وَالْخِيَامِ وَالْجُنْدِ، ثُمَّ يَأْمُرُ الرِّيحَ أَنْ تَحْمِلَهُ فَتَدْخُلَ تَحْتَهُ، ثُمَّ تَحْمِلَهُ فَتَرْفَعَهُ وَتَسِيرَ بِهِ، وَتُظِلُّهُ الطَّيْرُ مِنَ الْحَرِّ، إِلَى حَيْثُ يَشَاءُ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، فَيَنْزِلُ وَتُوضَعُ آلَاتُهُ وَخُشُبُهُ ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَسَخَّرْنَا لَهُ الرِّيحَ تَجْرِي بِأَمْرِهِ رُخَاءً حَيْثُ أَصَابَ﴾ [ص:٣٦] ، وَقَالَ ﴿غُدُوُّهَا شَهْرٌ وَرَوَاحُهَا شَهْرٌ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:١٢] .

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: ذُكِرَ عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي سِنَان، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: كَانَ يُوضَع لِسُلَيْمَانَ سِتُّمِائَةِ أَلْفِ كُرْسِيٍّ، فَيَجْلِسُ مِمَّا يَلِيهِ مُؤْمِنُو الْإِنْسِ، ثُمَّ يَجْلِسُ مِنْ وَرَائِهِمْ مُؤْمِنُو الْجِنِّ، ثُمَّ يَأْمُرُ الطَّيْرَ فَتُظِلُّهُمْ، ثُمَّ يَأْمُرُ الرِّيحَ فَتَحْمِلُهُ ﷺ .
