وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ؛ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: بَيَّنَ لَهُمْ مَا يَتَّقُونَ وَمَا يَأْتُونَ ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذِهِ أُمَّتُكُمْ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً﴾ أَيْ: سُنَّتُكُمْ سُنَّةٌ وَاحِدَةٌ. فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذِهِ﴾ إِنَّ وَاسْمُهَا، وَ ﴿أُمَّتُكُمْ﴾ خَبَرُ إِنَّ، أَيْ: هَذِهِ شَرِيعَتُكُمُ الَّتِي بَيَّنْتُ لَكُمْ وَوَضَّحْتُ لَكُمْ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً﴾ نُصِبَ عَلَى الْحَالِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَنَا رَبُّكُمْ فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الرُّسُلُ كُلُوا مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ وَاعْمَلُوا صَالِحًا إِنِّي بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ عَلِيمٌ * وَإِنَّ هَذِهِ أُمَّتُكُمْ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً وَأَنَا رَبُّكُمْ فَاتَّقُونِ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ:٥١، ٥٢] ، وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "نَحْنُ مَعْشَرَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ أَوْلَادُ عَلات دِينُنَا وَاحِدٌ"، يَعْنِي: أَنَّ الْمَقْصُودَ هُوَ عِبَادَةُ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ بِشَرَائِعَ مُتَنَوِّعَةٍ لِرُسُلِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِكُلٍّ جَعَلْنَا مِنْكُمْ شِرْعَةً وَمِنْهَاجًا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٤٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَقَطَّعُوا أَمْرَهُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ أَيِ: اخْتَلَفَتِ الْأُمَمُ عَلَى رُسُلِهَا، فَمِنْ بَيْنِ مُصَدق لَهُمْ وَمُكَذِّبٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كُلٌّ إِلَيْنَا رَاجِعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فيجازَى كُلٌّ بِحَسَبِ عَمَلِهِ، إِنْ خَيْرًا فَخَيْرٌ، وَإِنْ شَرًّا فَشَرٌّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ مِنَ الصَّالِحَاتِ وَهُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ﴾ أَيْ: قَلْبُهُ مُصَدِّقٌ، وَعَمِلَ عَمَلًا صَالِحًا، ﴿فَلا كُفْرَانَ لِسَعْيِهِ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّا لَا نُضِيعُ أَجْرَ مَنْ أَحْسَنَ عَمَلا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ:٣٠] أَيْ: لَا يُكْفَر سعيُه، وَهُوَ عَمَلُهُ، بَلْ يُشْكَر، فَلَا يُظْلَمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنَّا لَهُ كَاتِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُكتب جميعُ عَمَلِهِ، فَلَا يَضيع عَلَيْهِ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ.

---

## 21:95-97 — verses 95-97 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And it is forbidden for a town}. Ibn Abbas said: it has become established, meaning: a decreed matter, that the people of every town who have been destroyed shall not be returned to this world before the Day of Resurrection. This is what Ibn Abbas, Abu Ja'far al-Baqir, Qatadah, and more than one other have stated explicitly.

In another report from Ibn Abbas: {that they shall not return}, meaning: they shall not repent.

The first view is more evident, and God knows best.

His saying: {until, when Gog and Magog are unleashed}: We have already mentioned that they are descendants of Adam (peace be upon him), indeed they are also from the offspring of Noah, from the children of Yafith, the father of the Turks, the Turks being a remnant of them who were left behind the barrier built by Dhu al-Qarnayn.

He said: {This is a mercy from my Lord. But when the promise of my Lord comes, He will level it to the ground, and the promise of my Lord is ever true. And We shall leave them that day surging over one another, and the trumpet will be blown, and We shall gather them all together} [al-Kahf: 98, 99]. And He said in this noble verse: {until, when Gog and Magog are unleashed and they descend rapidly from every elevated place}, meaning: they hasten in walking toward corruption.

Al-hadab (the elevated place) refers to raised ground, as stated by Ibn Abbas, Ikrimah, Abu Salih, al-Thawri, and others. This is their description at the moment of their emergence, as if the listener were witnessing it. {And none can inform you like the All-Aware} [Fatir: 14]: this is the report of One who knows what was and what will be, who knows the unseen of the heavens and the earth, there is no deity but Him.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ubaydullah ibn Abi Yazid said: Ibn Abbas saw children leaping upon one another while playing, and Ibn Abbas said: this is how Gog and Magog will emerge.

Mention of their emergence has come in numerous hadiths from the Prophetic Sunnah.

The first hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "Gog and Magog will be unleashed, and they will come forth just as God, Mighty and Majestic, said": {and they descend rapidly from every elevated place}. They will overwhelm the people, and the Muslims will withdraw from them into their cities and fortresses, gathering their livestock to themselves. And they [Gog and Magog] will drink up the waters of the earth, until one of them passes by a river and they drink all that is in it, leaving it dry, so that those who come after them pass by that river and say: there was once water here. Until no one remains among the people except one in a fortress or a city, one of them will say: these are the people of the earth, we have finished with them, only the people of heaven remain. He said: "Then one of them will shake his spear and throw it toward the sky, and it will return to him stained with blood, as a trial and a test. While they are in that state, God, Mighty and Majestic, will send worms into their necks like the worms that appear in the necks of locusts, and they will wake up dead, with no sound heard from them. The Muslims will say: is there not a man who will sell his own life for us, to go and see what this enemy has done?" He said: "So a man among them will strip himself, expecting to be killed, having resolved himself to it, and he will go down and find them dead, one upon another, and he will call out: O company of Muslims, rejoice, for God, Mighty and Majestic, has spared you your enemy. They will then come out of their cities and fortresses and let their livestock loose, and their livestock will find no pasture except their flesh, and it will thrive on it as well as it has ever thrived on any vegetation it has ever come upon."

Ibn Majah also related it, through the hadith of Yunus ibn Bukayr, from Ibn Ishaq, with the same chain.

The second hadith: Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] al-Nawwas ibn Sam'an al-Kilabi said: The Messenger of God ﷺ mentioned the Dajjal one morning, lowering his voice and raising it, until we thought he was among a grove of palm trees. [When we went to him in the evening, he perceived that in our faces, and we asked him, saying: O Messenger of God, you mentioned the Dajjal this morning, lowering your voice and raising it, until we thought he was among a grove of palm trees.] He said: "Something other than the Dajjal frightens me more for you. If he emerges while I am among you, then I will be his adversary on your behalf, and if he emerges while I am not among you, then each man will be his own adversary, and God is my successor over every Muslim. He is a young man with tightly curled hair, and his eye protrudes, and he emerges from a gap between Syria and Iraq, and he will wreak corruption right and left. O servants of God, stand firm."

We said: O Messenger of God, how long will he remain on the earth? He said: "Forty days, one day like a year, one day like a month, one day like a week, and the rest of his days like your ordinary days."

We said: O Messenger of God, that day which is like a year, will the prayers of a single day and night suffice us for it? He said: "No, estimate for it its proper measure."

We said: O Messenger of God, how fast will he travel through the earth? He said: "Like rain driven by the wind." He said: "He will pass by a settlement and call its people, and they will respond to him, and he will command the sky to rain and the earth to bring forth vegetation, and their grazing herds will return to them in the evening with humps taller than ever, udders fuller than ever, and flanks more filled out than ever. And he will pass by another settlement and call them, but they will reject his word, and so their wealth will follow after him, and they will wake up in drought, having nothing left of their possessions. And he will pass by a ruin and say to it: bring forth your treasures, and its treasures will follow him like swarms of bees." He said: "And he will order a man to be killed, and he will strike him with the sword and cut him into two pieces the distance of an arrow's throw apart, then he will call him, and he will come forward toward him, [his face beaming with joy]."

While they are in that state, God, Mighty and Majestic, will send the Messiah, son of Mary, and he will descend at the white minaret, east of Damascus, wearing two garments dyed with saffron, placing his hands on the wings of two angels. He will pursue him [the Dajjal] and overtake him, and kill him at the gate of Ludd in the east.

He said: "While they are in that state, God, Mighty and Majestic, will reveal to Jesus, son of Mary: I have brought forth servants of Mine against whom none has the power to fight, so take My servants to safety at the Mount. Then God, Mighty and Majestic, will send Gog and Magog, and they will be as God said: {descending rapidly from every elevated place}. Jesus and his companions will implore God, Mighty and Majestic, and God will send upon them a worm in their necks, and they will wake up dead as one soul.

Then Jesus and his companions will come down, and they will not find on earth a single house that is not filled with their stench and rot. Jesus and his companions will implore God, and He will send upon them birds with necks like those of Bactrian camels, and they will carry them off and cast them wherever God wills."

Ibn Jabir said: Ata ibn Yazid al-Saksaki told me, from Ka'b or another, who said: they will cast them into al-Mahbil. [Ibn Jabir said: I said, O Abu Yazid, where is al-Mahbil?] He said: the place where the sun rises.

He said: "God will send a rain that no house of clay or hair-tent will keep out, for forty days, and it will wash the earth until it leaves it like a smooth polished surface, and it will be said to the earth: bring forth your fruit and restore your blessing." He said: "On that day, a group of people will eat from a single pomegranate and shelter in its rind, and blessing will be placed in milk, such that a single milk-she-camel will suffice a great multitude of people, and a milk-cow will suffice a whole clan, and a sheep from the flock will suffice a household."

He said: "While they are in that state, God, Mighty and Majestic, will send a pleasant wind beneath their armpits, and it will take the soul of every Muslim, or he said: every believer, and there will remain only the worst of people, copulating openly like donkeys, and upon them the Hour will come."

Muslim alone related it, without al-Bukhari, and the rest of the compilers of the Sunan related it through various chains from Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid ibn Jabir, with the same content. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (good and authentic).

The third hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from the aunt of Ibn Harmalah, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ delivered a sermon while his finger was bandaged from a scorpion sting, and he said: "You say: there is no enemy, yet you will continue to fight an enemy until Gog and Magog come, broad of face, small of eyes, reddish-haired, descending rapidly from every elevated place, as though their faces were hammered shields."

Ibn Abi Hatim likewise related it through the hadith of Muhammad ibn Amr, from Khalid ibn Abdullah ibn Harmalah al-Mudliji, from an aunt of his, from the Prophet ﷺ, mentioning the same.

The fourth hadith: it has already come earlier in the tafsir of the end of Surat al-A'raf, from the narration of Imam Ahmad, from Hushaym, from al-'Awwam, from Jabalah ibn Suhaym, from Mu'thir ibn 'Afazah, from Ibn Mas'ud, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "On the night I was taken on the Night Journey, I met Ibrahim, Musa, and 'Isa (peace be upon them)." He said: "They discussed together the matter of the Hour, and referred the matter to Ibrahim. He said: 'I have no knowledge of it.' So they referred the matter to Musa, and he said: 'I have no knowledge of it.' So they referred the matter to 'Isa, and he said: 'As for its occurrence, none knows it except Allah. But regarding it, my Lord made a covenant with me that the Dajjal will emerge.'"

He said: "'And I have with me two rods, and when he sees me he will melt as lead melts.'" He said: "'Allah will then destroy him when he sees me, until even the stone and the tree will say: O Muslim, there is a disbeliever beneath me, so come and kill him.'" He said: "'So Allah will destroy them, then the people will return to their lands and homelands.'" He said: "'At that point Ya'juj and Ma'juj will emerge, {and they will swarm down from every hill}, and they will trample their lands. They will come upon nothing without destroying it, and they will not pass by any water without drinking it.'" He said: "'Then the people will return to me complaining of them, and I will call upon Allah against them, and He will destroy them and cause them to die, until the earth becomes putrid from the stench of them, and Allah will send down rain that will sweep away their bodies until it casts them into the sea. Now among the things my Lord made a covenant with me is that when that occurs, the Hour will be like a pregnant woman at full term, whose family does not know when she will suddenly give birth, by night or by day.'"

Ibn Majah related it from Muhammad ibn Bashshar, from Yazid ibn Harun, from al-'Awwam ibn Hawshab, with the same chain, similarly, and he added: "Al-'Awwam said: the confirmation of this was found in the Book of Allah, Mighty and Majestic: {until, when Ya'juj and Ma'juj are let loose and they swarm down from every hill}."

Ibn Jarir related it here from the hadith of Jabalah, with the same chain.

The hadiths on this subject are very numerous, and likewise the reports from the early generations (salaf).

Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim related, from the hadith of Ma'mar, from more than one narrator, from Humayd ibn Hilal, from Abu al-Sayf, who said: Ka'b said: "When the emergence of Ya'juj and Ma'juj draws near, they will dig until those nearest to them can hear the striking of their axes. When night comes, they will say: 'We will come tomorrow and break through.' But Allah will restore it as it was. So they will come the next day and find that Allah has restored it as it was, and they will dig again until those nearest them hear the striking of their axes. When night comes, Allah will place upon the tongue of one of them the words: 'We will come tomorrow and break through, if Allah wills.' So they will come the next day and find it as they left it, and they will dig until they break through. The first group will pass by the lake and drink its water, then the second group will pass and lick its mud, then the third group will pass and say: 'There was once water here.' People will flee from them, and nothing will be able to stand against them. Then they will shoot their arrows toward the sky, and the arrows will return to them stained with blood, and they will say: 'We have overcome the people of the earth and the people of heaven.' Then 'Isa the son of Maryam (peace be upon him) will invoke against them, saying: 'O Allah, we have no power and no strength against them, so suffice us against them by whatever means You will.' So Allah will send upon them a worm called al-Nagaf, which will penetrate their necks, and Allah will send upon them birds which will seize them with their beaks and cast them into the sea. And Allah will bring forth a spring called 'al-Hayat' (Life), by which Allah will purify the earth and cause it to grow vegetation, until even a single pomegranate will satisfy an entire household (sakan)." He was asked: "What is the sakan, O Ka'b?" He said: "The people of the house." He said: "While the people are in that state, a cry will come to them that Dhu al-Suwayqatayn intends them." He said: "So 'Isa the son of Maryam will send an advance guard of seven hundred, or between seven hundred and eight hundred, and when they are partway along the road, Allah will send a pleasant wind from Yemen, which will take the soul of every believer, and there will remain only the rabble of the people, who will copulate openly as animals copulate. The likeness of the Hour at that time is like that of a man circling around his mare, waiting for when she will give birth." Ka'b said: "Whoever presumes to say anything beyond what I have said, or beyond this knowledge of mine, is one who overreaches himself."

This is among the best of the accounts of Ka'b al-Ahbar, on account of what is attested to it by authentic reports.

It is established in hadith that 'Isa the son of Maryam will perform Hajj to the Ancient House. Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Sa'id said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "This House will surely be visited for Hajj and 'Umrah after the emergence of Ya'juj and Ma'juj." Al-Bukhari alone related it.

And His saying, {and the true promise draws near}, meaning: the Day of Resurrection. When these terrors, earthquakes, and tumults occur, the Hour will have drawn near and approached. And when it comes and takes place, the disbelievers will say: {This is a hard day} [al-Qamar: 8]. Therefore He, Exalted is He, said: {then behold, the eyes of those who disbelieved are fixedly staring}, that is, from the severity of what they witness of the tremendous events: {Oh, woe to us}, meaning, they will say: {Oh, woe to us, we were indeed in heedlessness of this}, that is, in worldly life, {rather, we were wrongdoers}, acknowledging their wrongdoing against themselves, at a point where that acknowledgment will not benefit them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَحَرَامٌ عَلَى قَرْيَةٍ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَجَبَ، يَعْنِي: قَدَرًا مُقَدرًا أَنَّ أَهْلَ كُلِّ قَرْيَةٍ أُهْلِكُوا أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُرْجَعُونَ إِلَى الدُّنْيَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ. هَكَذَا صَرَّحَ بِهِ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الْبَاقِرُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَنَّهُمْ لَا يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَتُوبُونَ.

وَالْقَوْلُ الْأَوَّلُ أَظْهَرُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُتِحَتْ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ﴾ : قَدْ قَدَّمْنَا أَنَّهُمْ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بَلْ هُمْ مِنْ نَسْلِ نُوحٍ أَيْضًا مِنْ أَوْلَادِ يَافِثَ أَبِي التُّرْكِ، وَالتُّرْكُ شِرْذِمَةٌ مِنْهُمْ، تُرِكُوا مِنْ وَرَاءِ السَّدِّ الَّذِي بَنَاهُ ذُو الْقَرْنَيْنِ.

وَقَالَ: ﴿هَذَا رَحْمَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّي فَإِذَا جَاءَ وَعْدُ رَبِّي جَعَلَهُ دَكَّاءَ وَكَانَ وَعْدُ رَبِّي حَقًّا. وَتَرَكْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَمُوجُ فِي بَعْضٍ وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ فَجَمَعْنَاهُمْ جَمْعًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ:٩٨، ٩٩] ، وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُتِحَتْ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ وَهُمْ مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَبٍ يَنْسِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُسْرِعُونَ فِي الْمَشْيِ إِلَى الْفَسَادِ.

والحَدَب: هُوَ الْمُرْتَفِعُ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَالثَّوْرِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُمْ، وَهَذِهِ صِفَتُهُمْ فِي حَالِ خُرُوجِهِمْ، كَأَنَّ السَّامِعَ مُشَاهِدٌ لِذَلِكَ، ﴿وَلا يُنَبِّئُكَ مِثْلُ خَبِيرٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ:١٤] : هَذَا إِخْبَارُ عَالِمٍ مَا كَانَ وَمَا يَكُونُ، الَّذِي يَعْلَمُ غَيْبَ السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي يَزِيدَ قَالَ: رَأَى ابُن عَبَّاسٍ صِبْيَانًا يَنْزُو بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ، يَلْعَبُونَ، فَقَالَ ابن عباس: هكذا يَخْرُجُ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ ذِكْرُ خُرُوجِهِمْ فِي أَحَادِيثَ مُتَعَدِّدَةٍ مِنَ السُّنَّةِ النَّبَوِيَّةِ:

فَالْحَدِيثُ الْأَوَّلُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ عُمَر بْنِ قَتَادَةَ، عن محمود بن لَبيد، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "يُفتَح يأجوجُ ومأجوجُ، فَيَخْرُجُونَ كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ": ﴿ [وَهُمْ] مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَبٍ يَنْسِلُونَ﴾ ، فيغشونَ النَّاسَ، وَيَنْحَازُ الْمُسْلِمُونَ عَنْهُمْ إِلَى مَدَائِنِهِمْ وَحُصُونِهِمْ ، وَيَضُمُّونَ إِلَيْهِمْ مواشيَهم، وَيَشْرَبُونَ مِيَاهَ الْأَرْضِ، حَتَّى أَنَّ بعضَهم لَيَمُرُّ بِالنَّهْرِ، فَيَشْرَبُونَ مَا فِيهِ حَتَّى يَتْرُكُوهُ يَبَسا، حَتَّى أَنَّ مَنْ بَعْدَهُمْ لَيَمُرُّ بِذَلِكَ النَّهْرِ فَيَقُولُ : قَدْ كَانَ هَاهُنَا مَاءٌ مَرَّةً حَتَّى إِذَا لَمْ يبقَ مِنَ النَّاسِ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا أحدٌ فِي حِصْنٍ أَوْ مَدِينَةٍ قَالَ قَائِلُهُمْ: هَؤُلَاءِ أهلُ الْأَرْضِ، قَدْ فَرَغْنَا مِنْهُمْ، بَقِيَ أهلُ السَّمَاءِ. قَالَ: "ثُمَّ يَهُزُّ أَحَدُهُمْ حَرْبَتَهُ، ثُمَّ يَرْمِي بِهَا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ، فَتَرْجِعُ إِلَيْهِ مُخْتَضبَةً دَمًا؛ لِلْبَلَاءِ وَالْفِتْنَةِ. فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ دُودًا فِي أَعْنَاقِهِمْ كنَغَف الْجَرَادِ الَّذِي يَخْرُجُ فِي أَعْنَاقِهِ، فَيُصْبِحُونَ مَوْتًى لَا يُسمَع لَهُمْ حِسٌّ، فَيَقُولُ الْمُسْلِمُونَ: أَلَا رَجُلٌ يَشْري لَنَا نَفْسَهُ، فَيَنْظُرُ مَا فَعَلَ هَذَا الْعَدُوُّ؟ " قَالَ: "فَيَتَجَرَّدُ رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ مُحْتَسِبًا نَفْسَهُ، قَدْ أَوْطَنَهَا عَلَى أَنَّهُ مَقْتُولٌ، فَيَنْزِلُ فَيَجِدُهُمْ مَوْتًى، بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ، فَيُنَادِي: يَا مَعْشَرَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، أَلَا أَبْشِرُوا، إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ قَدْ كَفَاكُمْ عَدُوَّكُمْ، فَيَخْرُجُونَ مِنْ مَدَائِنِهِمْ وَحُصُونِهِمْ ويُسَرِّحون مَوَاشِيَهُمْ، فَمَا يَكُونُ لَهَا رَعْيٌ إِلَّا لُحُومَهُمْ، فَتَشْكر عَنْهُ كَأَحْسَنِ مَا شَكرَت عَنْ شَيْءٍ مِنَ النَّبَاتِ أَصَابَتْهُ قَطُّ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ يُونُسَ بْنِ بُكَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، بِهِ .

الْحَدِيثُ الثَّانِي: قَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ أَبُو الْعَبَّاسِ الدِّمَشْقِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ يَزِيدَ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، حَدَّثَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ جَابِرٍ الطَّائِيُّ -قَاضِي حِمْصَ-حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ جُبَير بْنِ نُفَير الْحَضْرَمِيُّ، عَنِ أَبِيهِ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ النَّوّاس بْنَ سمْعانَ الْكِلَابِيَّ قَالَ: ذَكَرَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ الدَّجَّالَ ذَاتَ غَداة، فخَفَض فِيهِ ورَفَع، حَتَّى ظَنَنَّاهُ فِي طَائِفَةِ النَّخْلِ، [فَلَمَّا رُحْنَا إِلَيْهِ عَرَفَ ذَلِكَ فِي وُجُوهِنَا، فَسَأَلْنَاهُ فَقُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ذَكَرْتَ الدَّجَّالَ الْغَدَاةَ، فَخَفَّضْتَ فِيهِ وَرَفَّعْتَ حَتَّى ظَنَنَّاهُ فِي طَائِفَةِ النَّخْلِ] . فَقَالَ: "غَيْرُ الدَّجَّالِ أخْوَفُني عَلَيْكُمْ، فَإِنْ يَخْرُجْ وَأَنَا فِيكُمْ فَأَنَا حَجِيجُه دُونَكُمْ، وَإِنْ يَخْرُجْ وَلَسْتُ فِيكُمْ فَامْرُؤٌ حَجِيجُ نَفْسِهِ، وَاللَّهُ خَلِيفَتِي عَلَى كُلِّ مُسْلِمٍ: إنه شاب جَعْدُ قَطَط عينه طَافِيَةٌ، وَإِنَّهُ يَخْرُجُ خَلَةَ بَيْنَ الشَّامِ وَالْعِرَاقِ، فَعَاثَ يَمِينًا وَشِمَالًا يَا عِبَادَ اللَّهِ اثْبُتُوا".

قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا لُبْثُهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ؟ قَالَ: "أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، يَوْمٌ كَسَنَةٍ، وَيَوْمٌ كَشَهْرٍ، وَيَوْمٌ كَجُمُعَةٍ، وَسَائِرُ أَيَّامِهِ كَأَيَّامِكُمْ".

قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، فَذَاكَ الْيَوْمُ الَّذِي هُوَ كَسَنَةٍ، أَتَكْفِينَا فِيهِ صَلَاةُ يَوْمٍ وَلَيْلَةٍ؟ قَالَ: "لَا اقْدِرُوا لَهُ قَدْرَهُ".

قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، فَمَا إِسْرَاعُهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ؟ قَالَ: "كَالْغَيْثِ اسْتَدْبَرَتْهُ الرِّيحُ". قَالَ: "فَيَمُرُّ بِالْحَيِّ فَيَدْعُوهُمْ فَيَسْتَجِيبُونَ لَهُ، فَيَأْمُرُ السَّمَاءَ فَتُمْطِرُ، وَالْأَرْضَ فَتُنْبِتُ، وَتَرُوحُ عَلَيْهِمْ سَارِحَتُهُمْ وَهِيَ أَطْوَلُ مَا كَانَتْ ذُرَى، وَأَمَدُّهُ خَوَاصِرَ، وَأَسْبَغُهُ ضُرُوعًا. وَيَمُرُّ بِالْحَيِّ فَيَدْعُوهُمْ فَيَرُدُّونَ عَلَيْهِ قولَه، فَتَتْبَعُهُ أَمْوَالُهُمْ، فَيُصْبِحُونَ مُمْحلين، لَيْسَ لَهُمْ مِنْ أَمْوَالِهِمْ. وَيَمُرُّ بالخَربة فَيَقُولُ لَهَا: أَخْرِجِي كُنُوزَكِ، فَتَتْبَعُهُ كُنُوزُهَا كَيَعَاسِيبِ النَّحْلِ". قَالَ: "وَيَأْمُرُ بِرَجُلٍ فيُقتَل، فَيَضْرِبُهُ بِالسَّيْفِ فَيَقْطَعُهُ جَزْلتين رَمْيَةَ الغَرَض، ثُمَّ يَدْعُوهُ فَيُقْبِلُ إِلَيْهِ [يَتَهَلَّلُ وَجْهُهُ] .

فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ الْمَسِيحَ ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ، فَيَنْزِلُ عِنْدَ الْمَنَارَةِ الْبَيْضَاءِ، شَرْقِيَّ دِمَشْقَ، بَيْنَ مَهْرُودَتَين وَاضِعًا يَدَه عَلَى أَجْنِحَةِ مَلَكين، فَيَتْبَعُهُ فَيُدْرِكُهُ، فَيَقْتُلُهُ عِنْدَ بَابِ لُدّ الشَّرْقِيِّ".

قَالَ: "فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ كَذَلِكَ، إِذْ أَوْحَى اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ إِلَى عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ: أَنِّي قَدْ أَخْرَجْتُ عِبَادًا مِنْ عِبَادِي لَا يَدَانِ لَكَ بِقِتَالِهِمْ، فَحَوّز عِبَادِي إِلَى الطُّورِ، فَيَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَأْجُوجَ وَمَأْجُوجَ، وَهُمْ كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَبٍ يَنْسِلُونَ﴾ فَيَرْغَبُ عِيسَى وَأَصْحَابُهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَيُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَغَفًا فِي رِقَابِهِمْ، فَيُصْبِحُونَ فَرْسى، كَمَوْتِ نَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ.

فَيَهْبِطُ عِيسَى وَأَصْحَابُهُ، فَلَا يَجِدُونَ فِي الْأَرْضِ بَيْتًا إِلَّا قَدْ مَلَأَهُ زَهَمُهم ونَتْنهُم، فَيَرْغَبُ عِيسَى وَأَصْحَابُهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَيُرْسِلُ عَلَيْهِمْ طَيْرًا كَأَعْنَاقِ البُخْت، فَتَحْمِلُهُمْ فَتَطْرَحُهُمْ حَيْثُ شَاءَ اللَّهُ".

قَالَ ابْنُ جَابِرٍ فَحَدَّثَنِي عَطَاءُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ السَّكْسَكيّ ، عَنْ كَعْبٍ -أَوْ غَيْرِهِ-قَالَ: فَتَطْرَحُهُمْ بالمَهْبِل. [قَالَ ابْنُ جَابِرٍ: فَقُلْتُ: يَا أَبَا يَزِيدَ، وَأَيْنَ المَهْبِل؟] ، قَالَ: مَطْلَعُ الشَّمْسِ.

قَالَ: "وَيُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ مَطَرًا لَا يَكُنَّ مِنْهُ بَيْتُ مَدَر وَلَا وَبَر أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، فَيَغْسِلُ الْأَرْضَ حَتَّى يَتْرُكَهَا كالزّلَقَةِ، وَيُقَالُ لِلْأَرْضِ: أَنْبِتِي ثَمَرَتَكِ، ورُدي بَرَكَتَكِ". قَالَ: "فَيَوْمَئِذٍ يَأْكُلُ النَّفَرُ مِنَ الرُّمَّانَةِ وَيَسْتَظِلُّونَ بقحْفها، ويُبَارك فِي الرَسْل، حَتَّى إِنَّ اللَّقْحَةَ مِنَ الْإِبِلِ لَتَكْفِي الفِئَامَ مِنَ النَّاسِ، وَاللَّقْحَةَ مِنَ الْبَقَرِ تَكْفِي الْفَخِذَ، وَالشَّاةَ مِنَ الْغَنَمِ تَكْفِي أَهْلَ الْبَيْتِ".

قَالَ: "فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ ، إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ رِيحًا طَيِّبَةً تَحْتَ آبَاطِهِمْ، فَتَقْبِضُ رُوحَ كُلِّ مُسْلِمٍ -أَوْ قَالَ: كُلِّ مُؤْمِنٍ-وَيَبْقَى شِرَارُ النَّاسِ يَتَهَارَجُونَ تَهَارُجَ الْحَمِيرِ، وَعَلَيْهِمْ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ دُونَ الْبُخَارِيِّ، فَرَوَاهُ مَعَ بَقِيَّةِ أَهْلِ السُّنَنِ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

الْحَدِيثُ الثَّالِثُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنِ ابْنِ حَرْمَلَة، عَنْ خَالَتِهِ قَالَتْ: خَطَبَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ عَاصِبٌ أصبعُه مِنْ لَدْغَةِ عَقْرب، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّكُمْ تَقُولُونَ: "لَا عَدُوَّ ، وَإِنَّكُمْ لَا تَزَالُونَ تُقَاتِلُونَ عَدُوًّا، حَتَّى يَأْتِيَ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ عِرَاضُ الْوُجُوهِ، صِغَارُ الْعُيُونِ، صُهْبَ الشِّعَافِ، مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَب يَنْسِلُونَ، كَأَنَّ وُجُوهَهُمُ المَجَانّ المُطرَقة" .

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ حَرْمَلة الْمُدْلِجِيِّ، عَنْ خَالَةٍ لَهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ .

الْحَدِيثُ الرَّابِعُ: قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ آخِرِ سُورَةِ الْأَعْرَافِ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، عَنْ هُشَيْم، عَنِ العَوَّام، عَنْ جَبَلَة بْنِ سُحَيْم، عَنْ مُؤثر بْنِ عَفَازَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: لَقِيتُ لَيْلَةَ أُسْرِيَ بِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَمُوسَى وَعِيسَى، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ: فَتَذَاكَرُوا أَمْرَ السَّاعَةِ، فَرَدُّوا أَمْرَهُمْ إِلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ، فَقَالَ: لَا عِلْمَ لِي بِهَا . فَرَدُّوا أَمْرَهُمْ إِلَى مُوسَى، فَقَالَ: لَا عِلْمَ لِي بِهَا . فَرَدُّوا أَمْرَهُمْ إِلَى عِيسَى، فَقَالَ: أَمَّا وَجْبَتها فلا يعلم بها أحد إلا الله، وَفِيهَا عَهِدَ إِلَيَّ رَبِّيَ أَنَّ الدَّجَّالَ خَارِجٌ".

قَالَ: "وَمَعِي قَضِيبَانِ، فَإِذَا رَآنِي ذَابَ كَمَا يَذُوبُ الرَّصَاصُ" قَالَ: "فَيُهْلِكُهُ اللَّهُ إِذَا رَآنِي، حَتَّى إِنَّ الْحَجَرَ وَالشَّجَرَ يَقُولُ: يَا مُسْلِمُ إِنَّ تَحْتِي كَافِرًا، فَتَعَالَ فَاقْتُلْهُ". قَالَ: "فَيُهْلِكُهُمُ اللَّهُ، ثُمَّ يَرْجِعُ النَّاسُ إِلَى بِلَادِهِمْ وَأَوْطَانِهِمْ". قَالَ: "فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ يَخْرُجُ يأجوج ومأجوج وهم مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَب يَنسلون، فَيَطَؤُونَ بِلَادَهُمْ، لَا يَأْتُونَ عَلَى شَيْءٍ إِلَّا أَهْلَكُوهُ، وَلَا يَمُرُّونَ عَلَى مَاءٍ إِلَّا شَرِبُوهُ". قَالَ: "ثُمَّ يَرْجِعُ النَّاسُ إِلَيَّ يَشْكُونَهُمْ، فَأَدْعُو اللَّهَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَيُهْلِكُهُمْ وَيُمِيتُهُمْ، حَتَّى تَجوى الْأَرْضُ مِنْ نَتْن رِيحِهِمْ، وَيُنْزِلُ اللَّهُ الْمَطَرَ فَيَجْتَرِفُ أَجْسَادَهُمْ، حَتَّى يَقْذِفَهُمْ فِي الْبَحْرِ. فَفِيمَا عَهِدَ إِلَيَّ رَبِّي أَنَّ ذَلِكَ إِذَا كَانَ كَذَلِكَ، أَنَّ السَّاعَةَ كَالْحَامِلِ المُتِمّ، لَا يَدْرِي أَهْلُهَا مَتَى تَفْجُؤهم بِوِلَادِهَا لَيْلًا أَوْ نَهَارًا".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ بَشَّارٍ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، عَنِ العَوَّام بْنِ حَوْشَب، به ، نَحْوَهُ وَزَادَ: "قَالَ العَوَّام، وَوُجِدَ تَصْدِيقُ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُتِحَتْ يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ وَهُمْ مِنْ كُلِّ حَدَبٍ يَنْسِلُونَ﴾ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هَاهُنَا مِنْ حَدِيثِ جَبَلَةَ، بِهِ .

وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا، وَالْآثَارُ عَنِ السَّلَفِ كَذَلِكَ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابُن جَرِيرٍ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَعْمَر، عَنْ غَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ بْنِ هِلَالٍ، عَنِ أَبِي الصَّيف قَالَ: قَالَ كَعْبٌ: إِذَا كَانَ عِنْدَ خُرُوجِ يَأْجُوجَ وَمَأْجُوجَ، حَفَرُوا حَتَّى يَسْمَعَ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ قَرْعَ فُؤُوسِهِمْ، فَإِذَا كَانَ اللَّيْلُ قَالُوا: نَجِيءُ غَدًا فَنَخْرُجُ، فَيُعِيدُهُ اللَّهُ كَمَا كَانَ. فَيَجِيئُونَ مِنَ الْغَدِ فَيَجِدُونَهُ قَدْ أَعَادَهُ اللَّهُ كَمَا كَانَ، فَيَحْفِرُونَهُ حَتَّى يَسْمَعَ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ قَرْعَ فُؤُوسِهِمْ، فَإِذَا كَانَ اللَّيْلُ أَلْقَى اللَّهُ عَلَى لِسَانِ رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ يَقُولُ: نَجِيءُ غَدًا فَنَخْرُجُ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ. فَيَجِيئُونَ مِنَ الْغَدِ فَيَجِدُونَهُ كَمَا تَرَكُوهُ، فَيَحْفِرُونَ حَتَّى يَخْرُجُوا. فَتَمُرُّ الزُّمْرَةُ الْأُولَى بِالْبُحَيْرَةِ، فَيَشْرَبُونَ مَاءَهَا، ثُمَّ تَمُرُّ الزُّمْرَةُ الثَّانِيَةُ فَيَلْحَسُونَ طِينَهَا، ثُمَّ تَمُرُّ الزُّمْرَةُ الثَّالِثَةُ فَيَقُولُونَ : قَدْ كَانَ هَاهُنَا مَرَّةً مَاءٌ، وَيَفِرُّ النَّاسُ مِنْهُمْ، فَلَا يَقُومُ لَهُمْ شَيْءٌ. ثُمَّ يَرْمُونَ بِسِهَامِهِمْ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فَتَرْجِعُ إِلَيْهِمْ مُخَضَّبة بِالدِّمَاءِ فَيَقُولُونَ: غَلَبْنَا أَهْلَ الْأَرْضِ وَأَهْلَ السَّمَاءِ. فَيَدْعُو عَلَيْهِمْ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَيَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ، لَا طَاقَةَ وَلَا يَدَين لَنَا بِهِمْ، فَاكْفِنَاهُمْ بِمَا شِئْتَ"، فَيُسَلِّطُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ دُودًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: النَّغْفُ، فَيَفْرِسُ رِقَابَهُمْ، وَيَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ طَيْرًا تَأْخُذُهُمْ بِمَنَاقِيرِهَا فَتُلْقِيهِمْ فِي الْبَحْرِ، وَيَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ عَيْنًا يُقَالُ لَهَا: "الْحَيَاةُ" يُطَهِّرُ اللَّهُ الْأَرْضَ وَيُنْبِتُهَا، حَتَّى إِنَّ الرُّمَّانَةَ لَيَشْبَعُ مِنْهَا السَّكْن". قِيلَ: وَمَا السَّكن يَا كَعْبُ؟ قَالَ: أَهْلُ الْبَيْتِ -قَالَ: "فَبَيْنَمَا النَّاسُ كَذَلِكَ إِذْ أَتَاهُمُ الصَّريخ أَنَّ ذَا السُّويقَتَين يُرِيدُهُ. قَالَ: فَيَبْعَثُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ طَلِيعَةً سَبْعَمِائَةٍ، أَوْ بَيْنَ السَّبْعِمِائَةِ وَالثَّمَانِمِائَةِ، حَتَّى إِذَا كَانُوا بِبَعْضِ الطَّرِيقِ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ رِيحًا يَمَانِيَّةً طَيِّبَةً، فَيَقْبِضُ فِيهَا رُوحَ كُلِّ مُؤْمِنٍ، ثُمَّ يَبْقَى عَجَاج النَّاسِ، فَيَتَسَافَدُونَ كَمَا تَسَافَدُ الْبَهَائِمُ، فَمَثل السَّاعَةِ كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ يَطِيفُ حَوْلَ فَرَسِهِ يَنْتَظِرُهَا مَتَى تَضَعُ؟ قَالَ كَعْبٌ: فَمَنْ تَكَلَّفَ بَعْدَ قَوْلِي هَذَا شَيْئًا -أَوْ بَعْدَ عِلْمِي هَذَا شَيْئًا-فَهُوَ الْمُتَكَلِّفُ .

هَذَا مِنْ أَحْسَنِ سِيَاقَاتِ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ، لِمَا شَهِدَ لَهُ مِنْ صَحِيحِ الْأَخْبَارِ.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ أَنَّ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ يَحُجُّ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ، وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا عِمْرَانُ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي عُتبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ليُحَجَّنَّ هَذَا الْبَيْتَ، وليُعْتَمَرنّ بَعْدَ خروج يأجوج ومأجوج". انفرد بإخراجه البخاري .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاقْتَرَبَ الْوَعْدُ الْحَقُّ﴾ يَعْنِي: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، إِذَا وُجدت هَذِهِ الْأَهْوَالُ وَالزَّلَازِلُ وَالْبَلَابِلُ، أَزِفَتِ السَّاعَةُ وَاقْتَرَبَتْ، فَإِذَا كَانَتْ وَوَقَعَتْ قَالَ الْكَافِرُونَ: ﴿هَذَا يَوْمٌ عَسِرٌ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ:٨] . وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِذَا هِيَ شَاخِصَةٌ أَبْصَارُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ شِدَّةِ مَا يُشَاهِدُونَهُ مِنَ الْأُمُورِ الْعِظَامِ: ﴿يَا وَيْلَنَا﴾ أَيْ: يَقُولُونَ: ﴿يَا وَيْلَنَا قَدْ كُنَّا فِي غَفْلَةٍ مِنْ هَذَا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا، ﴿بَلْ كُنَّا ظَالِمِينَ﴾ ، يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِظُلْمِهِمْ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ، حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ ذَلِكَ.

---

## 21:98-103 — verses 98-103 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, addressing the people of Mecca among the polytheists of Quraysh and those who followed their religion among the worshippers of idols and images: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood for Hell}. Ibn Abbas said: that is, its fuel, meaning like His saying: {Its fuel is people and stones} [al-Tahrim: 6].

Ibn Abbas also said: {hasab of Hell} means the trees of Hell. And in another report he said: {hasab of Hell} means the firewood of Hell, in the language of the Zanj.

Mujahid, Ikrimah, and Qatadah said: its firewood. And it is so in the reading of Ali and A'ishah, may Allah be pleased with them both.

Al-Dahhak said: {hasab of Hell} means what is thrown into it.

Others said the same. And all these meanings are close to one another.

His saying: {you will enter it} means, you will go into it.

{If these had been gods, they would not have entered it} meaning, if these idols and rivals which you took besides Allah had been true gods, they would not have entered the Fire, nor gone into it. {And all of them will abide therein forever} meaning, the worshippers and their objects of worship, all of them abiding therein forever. {For them therein is groaning}, as He said: {For them therein is groaning and wailing} [Hud: 106]. Al-zafir (groaning) is the going out of their breath, and al-shahiq (wailing) is the drawing in of their breath. {And they therein will not hear}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Mas'ud said: When those who are to abide forever in the Fire remain, they will be placed in coffins of fire, with nails of fire in them, so that none of them will see anyone else being punished in the Fire besides himself. Then Abdullah recited: {For them therein is groaning, and they therein will not hear}.

Ibn Jarir also narrated it, from the hadith of Hajjaj ibn Muhammad, from al-Mas'udi, from Yunus ibn Khabbab, from Ibn Mas'ud, mentioning it.

Concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us}: Ikrimah said: mercy. Others said: happiness (felicity). {Those will be kept far from it}. When the Almighty mentioned the people of the Fire and their punishment because of their associating partners with Allah, He followed this by mentioning the fortunate ones among the believers in Allah and His messengers, those for whom happiness had already been decreed by Allah, and who had done righteous deeds in this world beforehand, as He said: {For those who did good is the best reward, and even more} [Yunus: 26], and He said: {Is the reward of good other than good?} [al-Rahman: 60]. So just as they did good deeds in this world, Allah made their final outcome and their reward good, so He saved them from the punishment, and they obtained abundant reward. So He said: {Those will be kept far from it. They will not hear its hiss} meaning, the sound of its burning in bodies.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Abu Uthman, concerning {They will not hear its hiss}, he said: there are snakes on the bridge (al-sirat) that bite them, and when they bite them, one says: "hiss, hiss."

Concerning His saying: {And they will abide forever in what their souls desired}: He kept them safe from what is feared and dreaded, and they obtained what is sought and beloved.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] al-Nu'man ibn Bashir said, he was sitting up at night with Ali, who recited: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, those will be kept far from it}, and said: I am among them, and Umar is among them, and Uthman is among them, and al-Zubayr is among them, and Talha is among them, and Abd al-Rahman is among them, or he said: Sa'd is among them. He said: and the call to prayer was made, and he stood up, and I think he was dragging his garment, saying: {They will not hear its hiss}.

Shu'bah said, from Abu Bishr, from Yusuf al-Makki, from Muhammad ibn Hatib, who said: I heard Ali say concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us}: he said: Uthman and his companions.

Ibn Abi Hatim also narrated it, and Ibn Jarir narrated it from the hadith of Yusuf ibn Sa'd, not Ibn Mahak, from Muhammad ibn Hatib, from Ali, mentioning it, with the wording: Uthman is among them.

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, those will be kept far from it}: those are the friends of Allah, who will pass over the bridge (al-sirat) faster than lightning, while the disbelievers remain kneeling in it.

This agrees with what we have mentioned. Others said: rather, it was revealed as an exception regarding those who are worshipped, and Uzayr and the Messiah (peace be upon him) were excluded from them, as Hajjaj ibn Muhammad al-A'war said, from Ibn Jurayj and Uthman ibn Ata, from Ata, from Ibn Abbas: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood for Hell}, then He made an exception, saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us}. It is said: they are the angels, and Jesus (peace be upon him), and the like of those who are worshipped besides Allah, Mighty and Majestic is He. Ikrimah, al-Hasan, and Ibn Jurayj said the same.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us}: he said: it was revealed concerning Jesus son of Mary and Uzayr, upon both of them be peace.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from al-Asbagh, from Ali, concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us}: he said: everything that is worshipped besides Allah is in the Fire, except the sun, the moon, and Jesus son of Mary. Its chain of transmission is weak.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: {Those will be kept far from it}, he said: Jesus, Uzayr, and the angels.

Al-Dahhak said: Jesus, Mary, the angels, the sun, and the moon. The same was reported from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Abu Salih, and several others.

Ibn Abi Hatim narrated concerning this a very gharib (singular) hadith, saying: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, concerning His saying: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, those will be kept far from it}, he said: Jesus, Uzayr, and the angels.

Some of them mentioned the story of Ibn al-Zib'ara and the debate of the polytheists. Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh said:

[chain] Ibn Abbas said: Abdullah ibn al-Zib'ara came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: You claim that Allah revealed to you this verse: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood for Hell, you will enter it}. Ibn al-Zib'ara said: The sun, the moon, the angels, Uzayr, and Jesus son of Mary have been worshipped, are all of these in the Fire along with our gods? Then there was revealed: {And when the son of Mary is presented as an example, your people turn away from it in aversion. And they say, "Are our gods better, or is he?" They only present that to you for the sake of argument. Rather, they are a people prone to dispute}, then there was revealed: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, those will be kept far from it}. Al-Hafiz Abu Abdullah narrated it in his book "al-Ahadith al-Mukhtarah".

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: When there was revealed: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood for Hell, you will enter it}, the polytheists said: are the angels, Uzayr, and Jesus then worshipped besides Allah? Then there was revealed: {If these had been gods, they would not have entered it}, that is, the gods that they worship, {and all of them abide therein forever}.

It was narrated from Abu Kudaynah, from Ata ibn al-Sa'ib, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, similarly, and he said: then there was revealed: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, those will be kept far from it}.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar, may Allah have mercy on him, said in the book "al-Sirah": The Messenger of Allah, as I have been informed, sat one day with al-Walid ibn al-Mughirah in the mosque, and al-Nadr ibn al-Harith came and sat with them, and in the mosque were several men of Quraysh. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ spoke, and al-Nadr ibn al-Harith engaged him, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ spoke to him until he silenced him, and recited to him and to them: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood for Hell, you will enter it} up to His saying: {and they therein will not hear}.

Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood up, and Abdullah ibn al-Zibaʿra al-Sahmi came forward and sat down. Al-Walid ibn al-Mughira said to Abdullah ibn al-Zibaʿra: "By God, al-Nadr ibn al-Harith neither stood up nor sat down just now for the son of Abd al-Muttalib, while Muhammad has claimed that we and these gods of ours that we worship are firewood of Hell." Abdullah ibn al-Zibaʿra said: "By God, if I had found him I would have refuted him. Ask Muhammad: everything that is worshipped besides Allah will be in Hell along with whoever worshipped it. We worship the angels, the Jews worship Ezra, and the Christians worship Jesus son of Mary!" Al-Walid and those present in the gathering were amazed at Abdullah ibn al-Zibaʿra's statement, and they thought that he had made a valid argument and won the dispute.

This was mentioned to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and he said: "Everyone who loves to be worshipped besides Allah will be with whoever worshipped him. They only worship the devils and whoever the devils commanded them to worship." And Allah revealed: {Indeed, those for whom the best has preceded from Us, they are the ones removed far from it. They will not hear its hissing sound, and they will abide forever in what their souls desired} meaning Jesus, Ezra, and those among the rabbis and monks who were worshipped, who had lived in obedience to Allah, but whom the people of misguidance who worshipped them took as lords besides Allah. And it was also revealed concerning what they mentioned, that they worship the angels and that the angels are the daughters of Allah: {And they say, "The Most Merciful has taken a son." Exalted is He! Rather, they are honored servants. They do not precede Him in speech, and they act by His command} up to His saying: {And whoever of them should say, "Indeed, I am a god besides Him," that one We would recompense with Hell. Thus do We recompense the wrongdoers} [al-Anbiya: 26-29]. And it was also revealed concerning what was mentioned about the matter of Jesus, that he is worshipped besides Allah, and concerning the amazement of al-Walid and those present at his argument and dispute: {And when the son of Mary is presented as an example, your people turn away from it in aversion. And they say, "Are our gods better, or is he?" They only presented it to you for the sake of argument. Rather, they are a disputatious people. He was not but a servant upon whom We bestowed favor, and We made him an example for the Children of Israel. And if We willed, We could have made from you angels succeeding one another on the earth. And indeed, he is knowledge for the Hour, so do not doubt it} [al-Zukhruf: 57-61], meaning: the signs that I placed at his hands, of raising the dead and healing the sick, are sufficient proof of knowledge of the Hour. He says: {So do not doubt it, and follow Me. This is a straight path} [al-Zukhruf: 61].

What Ibn al-Zibaʿra said is a grave error, because the verse was revealed addressing the people of Mecca concerning their worship of idols, which are inanimate objects without reason, so that it would serve as a rebuke and reproach to those who worshipped them. This is why He said: {Indeed, you and what you worship besides Allah are firewood of Hell}. How then could this be applied to the Messiah, Ezra, and the like, who had righteous deeds and never approved of the worship of those who worshipped them? Ibn Jarir relied in his tafsir, in answering this, on the fact that "ma" (what) among the Arabs is used for that which lacks reason.

Abdullah ibn al-Zibaʿra later accepted Islam, and he was among the well-known poets. He used to satirize the Muslims at first, then he said in apology:

O Messenger of the Sovereign, my tongue has mended what it tore, when I was ruined,

When I ran alongside Satan on the path of misguidance, and whoever inclines toward his inclination is doomed.

Concerning His saying: {The greatest terror will not grieve them}, it is said that death is meant by this. Abd al-Razzaq narrated this from Yahya ibn Rabi'a from Ata.

And it is said that the greatest terror refers to the blowing of the trumpet (al-sur). This was said by al-'Awfi from Ibn Abbas, and by Abu Sinan Sa'id ibn Sinan al-Shaybani, and Ibn Jarir chose this view in his tafsir.

And it is said that it refers to when the servant is ordered to the Fire. This was said by al-Hasan al-Basri.

And it is said that it refers to when the Fire closes over its inhabitants. This was said by Sa'id ibn Jubayr and Ibn Jurayj.

And it is said that it refers to when death is slaughtered between Paradise and Hell. This was said by Abu Bakr al-Hudhali, as narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim from him.

Concerning His saying: {And the angels will receive them, "This is your day which you were promised"}, meaning: the angels say to them, giving them glad tidings on the day of their return when they come out of their graves: {This is your day which you were promised}, that is: meet what pleases you.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخَاطِبًا لِأَهْلِ مَكَّةَ مِنْ مُشْرِكِي قُرَيْشٍ، وَمَنْ دَانَ بِدِينِهِمْ مِنْ عَبَدَةِ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَوْثَانِ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ ، قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَيْ وَقُودُهَا، يَعْنِي كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَقُودُهَا النَّاسُ وَالْحِجَارَةُ﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ:٦] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ أَيْضًا: ﴿حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ بِمَعْنَى: شَجَرِ جَهَنَّمَ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ قَالَ: ﴿حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ يَعْنِي: حَطَبَ جَهَنَّمَ، بِالزِّنْجِيَّةِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَقَتَادَةُ: حَطَبُهَا. وَهِيَ كَذَلِكَ فِي قِرَاءَةِ عَلِيٍّ وَعَائِشَةَ -رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا يُرْمَى بِهِ فِيهَا.

وَكَذَا قَالَ غَيْرُهُ. وَالْجَمِيعُ قَرِيبٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَنْتُمْ لَهَا وَارِدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: دَاخِلُونَ.

﴿لَوْ كَانَ هَؤُلاءِ آلِهَةً مَا وَرَدُوهَا﴾ يَعْنِي: لَوْ كَانَتْ هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامُ وَالْأَنْدَادُ الَّتِي اتَّخَذْتُمُوهَا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ آلِهَةً صَحِيحَةً لَمَا وَرَدُوا النَّارَ، وَلَمَا دَخَلُوهَا، ﴿وَكُلٌّ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾ أَيِ: الْعَابِدُونَ وَمَعْبُودَاتُهُمْ، كُلُّهُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ، ﴿لَهُمْ فِيهَا زَفِيرٌ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَهُمْ فِيهَا زَفِيرٌ وَشَهِيقٌ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٠٦] ، وَالزَّفِيرُ: خُرُوجُ أَنْفَاسِهِمْ، وَالشَّهِيقُ: وُلُوجُ أَنْفَاسِهِمْ، ﴿وَهُمْ فِيهَا لَا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الطَّنَافِسيّ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ فُضَيْل، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ -يَعْنِي: الْمَسْعُودِيَّ-عَنِ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: إِذَا بَقِيَ مَنْ يَخْلُدُ فِي النَّارِ، جُعلوا فِي تَوَابِيتَ مِنْ نَارٍ، فِيهَا مَسَامِيرُ مِنْ نَارٍ، فَلَا يَرَى أَحَدٌ مِنْهُمْ أَنَّهُ يُعَذَّبُ فِي النَّارِ غَيْرُهُ، ثُمَّ تَلَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: ﴿لَهُمْ فِيهَا زَفِيرٌ وَهُمْ فِيهَا لَا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَجَّاجِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنِ الْمَسْعُودِيِّ، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ خَبّاب ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ فَذَكَرَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى﴾ : قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: الرَّحْمَةُ. وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: السَّعَادَةُ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَهْلَ النَّارِ وَعَذَابَهُمْ بِسَبَبِ شِرْكِهِمْ بِاللَّهِ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ السُّعَدَاءِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِاللَّهِ ورسُله ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ السَّعَادَةُ، وَأَسْلَفُوا الْأَعْمَالَ الصَّالِحَةَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةٌ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٢٦] : وَقَالَ ﴿هَلْ جَزَاءُ الإحْسَانِ إِلا الإحْسَانُ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٦٠] ، فَكَمَا أَحْسَنُوا الْعَمَلَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، أَحْسَنَ اللَّهُ مَآلَهُمْ وَثَوَابَهُمْ، فَنَجَّاهُمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ، وحَصَل لَهُمْ جَزِيلُ الثَّوَابِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ. لَا يَسْمَعُونَ حَسِيسَهَا﴾ أَيْ: حَرِيقَهَا فِي الْأَجْسَادِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ الْجُرَيْرِيِّ ، عَنِ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ: ﴿لَا يَسْمَعُونَ حَسِيسَهَا﴾ ، قَالَ: حَيَّاتٌ عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ تَلْسَعُهُمْ، فَإِذَا لَسَعَتْهُمْ قَالَ: حَسَ حَسَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُمْ فِي مَا اشْتَهَتْ أَنْفُسُهُمْ خَالِدُونَ﴾ فَسَلَّمَهُمْ مِنَ الْمَحْذُورِ وَالْمَرْهُوبِ، وَحَصَلَ لَهُمُ الْمَطْلُوبُ وَالْمَحْبُوبُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ أَبِي سُرَيج، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ أَبِي يَزِيدَ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ، عَنْ لَيْثِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَمِّ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ بَشِيرٍ قَالَ -وسَمَرَ مَعَ عَلِيٍّ ذَاتَ لَيْلَةٍ، فَقَرَأَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ قَالَ: أَنَا مِنْهُمْ، وَعُمَرُ مِنْهُمْ، وَعُثْمَانُ مِنْهُمْ، وَالزُّبَيْرُ مِنْهُمْ، وَطَلْحَةُ مِنْهُمْ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ مِنْهُمْ -أَوْ قَالَ: سَعْدٌ مِنْهُمْ-قَالَ: وَأُقِيمَتِ الصَّلَاةُ فَقَامَ، وَأَظُنُّهُ يَجُرُّ ثَوْبَهُ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: ﴿لَا يَسْمَعُونَ حَسِيسَهَا﴾ .

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ يُوسُفَ الْمَكِّيِّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حَاطِبٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَلِيًّا يَقُولُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى﴾ قَالَ: عُثْمَانُ وَأَصْحَابُهُ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا، وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ يُوسُفَ بْنِ سَعْدٍ -وَلَيْسَ بِابْنِ مَاهَكَ-عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حَاطِبٍ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَلَفْظُهُ: عُثْمَانُ مِنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ : فَأُولَئِكَ أَوْلِيَاءُ اللَّهِ يَمُرُّونَ عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ مَرًّا هُوَ أَسْرَعُ مِنَ الْبَرْقِ، وَيَبْقَى الْكُفَّارُ فِيهَا جِثيًا.

فَهَذَا مُطَابِقٌ لِمَا ذَكَرْنَاهُ، وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ نَزَلَتِ اسْتِثْنَاءً مِنَ الْمَعْبُودِينَ، وَخَرَجَ مِنْهُمْ عُزَيْرٌ وَالْمَسِيحُ، كَمَا قَالَ حَجَّاجِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ الْأَعْوَرِ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ وَعُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ ، ثُمَّ اسْتَثْنَى فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى﴾ فَيُقَالُ : هُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ، وَعِيسَى، وَنَحْوُ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا يُعْبَدُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ .

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى﴾ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ وعُزَير، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ عِيسَى بْنِ مَيْسَرَة، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُهَير، حَدَّثَنَا سَعْدُ بْنُ طَرِيف، عَنِ الْأَصْبَغِ، عَنْ عَليّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى﴾ قَالَ: كُلُّ شَيْءٍ يُعْبَدُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ فِي النَّارِ إِلَّا الشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ وَعِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ. إِسْنَادُهُ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ ، قَالَ: عِيسَى، وعُزَيْر، وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: عِيسَى، وَمَرْيَمُ، وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ، وَالشَّمْسُ، وَالْقَمَرُ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، وَأَبِي صَالِحٍ وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي ذَلِكَ حَدِيثًا غَرِيبًا جِدًّا، فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا الْفَضْلُ بْنُ يَعْقُوبَ الرُّخَّاني، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَسْلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ، حَدَّثَنَا اللَّيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُغيث، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ قَالَ: عِيسَى، وعُزَير، وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ .

وَذَكَرَ بَعْضُهُمْ قِصَّةَ ابْنِ الزِّبَعْرَى ومناظرةَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، قَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُويه:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ سَهْلٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ حَسَنٍ الْأَنْمَاطِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَرْعَرَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي حَكِيمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَكَمُ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ أَبَانٍ-عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: تَزْعُمُ أَنَّ اللَّهَ أَنَزَلَ عَلَيْكَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ أَنْتُمْ لَهَا وَارِدُونَ﴾ ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى: قَدْ عُبدت الشَّمْسُ وَالْقَمَرُ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ، وعُزَير وَعِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ، كُلُّ هَؤُلَاءِ فِي النَّارِ مَعَ آلِهَتِنَا؟ فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَلَمَّا ضُرِبَ ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ مَثَلا إِذَا قَوْمُكَ مِنْهُ يَصِدُّونَ. وَقَالُوا أَآلِهَتُنَا خَيْرٌ أَمْ هُوَ مَا ضَرَبُوهُ لَكَ إِلا جَدَلا بَلْ هُمْ قَوْمٌ خَصِمُونَ﴾ ، ثُمَّ نَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ . رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ فِي كِتَابِهِ "الْأَحَادِيثِ الْمُخْتَارَةِ".

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا قَبِيصة بْنُ عُقْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ -يَعْنِي: الثَّوْرِيَّ-عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنِ أَصْحَابِهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ أَنْتُمْ لَهَا وَارِدُونَ﴾ قال المشركون: فالملائكة ،عُزَير، وَعِيسَى يُعْبَدون مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ؟ فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿لَوْ كَانَ هَؤُلاءِ آلِهَةً مَا وَرَدُوهَا﴾ ، الْآلِهَةُ الَّتِي يُعْبَدُونَ، ﴿وَكُلٌّ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾ .

وَرُوِيَ عَنِ أَبِي كُدَيْنَة، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ مِثْلُ ذَلِكَ، وَقَالَ فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَارٍ ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِ "السِّيرَةِ": وَجَلَسَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ -فِيمَا بَلَغَنِي-يَوْمًا مَعَ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَجَاءَ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ حَتَّى جَلَسَ مَعَهُمْ، وَفِي الْمَسْجِدِ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ رِجَالِ قُرَيْشٍ، فَتَكَلَّمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَعَرَضَ لَهُ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، فَكَلَّمَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى أَفْحَمَهُ، وَتَلَا عَلَيْهِ وَعَلَيْهِمْ ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ أَنْتُمْ لَهَا وَارِدُونَ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَهُمْ فِيهَا لَا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ ، ثُمَّ قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَأَقْبَلَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزبَعْرَى السَّهْمِيُّ حَتَّى جَلَسَ، فَقَالَ الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزِّبَعْرَى: وَاللَّهِ مَا قَامَ النَّضْرُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ لِابْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ آنِفًا وَلَا قَعَدَ، وَقَدْ زَعَمَ مُحَمَّدٌ أنَّا وَمَا نَعْبُدُ مِنْ آلِهَتِنَا هَذِهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ. فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى: أَمَا وَاللَّهِ لَوْ وَجَدْتُهُ لَخَصمته، فَسَلُوا مُحَمَّدًا: كُلُّ مَا يُعْبَد مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ فِي جَهَنَّمَ مَعَ مَنْ عَبَده، فَنَحْنُ نَعْبُدُ الْمَلَائِكَةَ، وَالْيَهُودُ تَعْبُدُ عُزَيْرًا، وَالنَّصَارَى تَعْبُدُ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ؟ فَعَجِبَ الْوَلِيدُ وَمَنْ كَانَ مَعَهُ فِي الْمَجْلِسِ، مِنْ قَوْلِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزِّبَعْرَى، وَرَأَوْا أَنَّهُ قَدْ احْتَجَّ وَخَاصَمَ.

فَذُكر ذَلِكَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ: "كُلُّ مَنْ أحَبَّ أَنْ يُعْبَدَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ فَهُوَ مَعَ مَنْ عَبَدَهُ، إِنَّهُمْ إِنَّمَا يَعْبُدُونَ الشَّيَاطِينَ وَمَنْ أمَرَتْهُم بِعِبَادَتِهِ. وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ سَبَقَتْ لَهُمْ مِنَّا الْحُسْنَى أُولَئِكَ عَنْهَا مُبْعَدُونَ. لا يَسْمَعُونَ حَسِيسَهَا وَهُمْ فِي مَا اشْتَهَتْ أَنْفُسُهُمْ خَالِدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عِيسَى وَعُزَيْرٌ وَمَنْ عُبدوا مِنَ الْأَحْبَارِ وَالرُّهْبَانِ، الَّذِينَ مَضَوْا عَلَى طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ، فَاتَّخَذَهُمْ مَنْ يَعْبُدُهُمْ مِنْ أَهْلِ الضَّلَالَةِ أَرْبَابًا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ. وَنَزَلَ فِيمَا يَذْكُرُونَ، أَنَّهُمْ يَعْبُدُونَ الْمَلَائِكَةَ، وَأَنَّهُمْ بَنَاتُ اللَّهِ: ﴿وَقَالُوا اتَّخَذَ الرَّحْمَنُ وَلَدًا سُبْحَانَهُ بَلْ عِبَادٌ مُكْرَمُونَ. لَا يَسْبِقُونَهُ بِالْقَوْلِ وَهُمْ بِأَمْرِهِ يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَنْ يَقُلْ مِنْهُمْ إِنِّي إِلَهٌ مِنْ دُونِهِ فَذَلِكَ نَجْزِيهِ جَهَنَّمَ كَذَلِكَ نَجْزِي الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:٢٦ -٢٩] ، وَنَزَلَ فِيمَا ذُكر مَنْ أَمْرِ عِيسَى، وَأَنَّهُ يُعْبَدُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، وعَجَب الْوَلِيدِ وَمَنْ حَضَره مِنْ حُجَّته وَخُصُومَتِهِ: ﴿وَلَمَّا ضُرِبَ ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ مَثَلا إِذَا قَوْمُكَ مِنْهُ يَصِدُّونَ. وَقَالُوا أَآلِهَتُنَا خَيْرٌ أَمْ هُوَ مَا ضَرَبُوهُ لَكَ إِلا جَدَلا بَلْ هُمْ قَوْمٌ خَصِمُونَ. إِنْ هُوَ إِلا عَبْدٌ أَنْعَمْنَا عَلَيْهِ وَجَعَلْنَاهُ مَثَلا لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. وَلَوْ نَشَاءُ لَجَعَلْنَا مِنْكُمْ مَلائِكَةً فِي الأرْضِ يَخْلُفُونَ. وَإِنَّهُ لَعِلْمٌ لِلسَّاعَةِ فَلا تَمْتَرُنَّ بِهَا﴾ [الزخرف:٥٧ -٦١] أَيْ: مَا وَضَعْتُ عَلَى يَدَيْهِ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ مِنْ إِحْيَاءِ الْمَوْتَى وَإِبْرَاءِ الْأَسْقَامِ، فكَفى بِهِ دَلِيلًا عَلَى عِلْمِ السَّاعَةِ، يَقُولُ: ﴿فَلا تَمْتَرُنَّ بِهَا وَاتَّبِعُونِ هَذَا صِرَاطٌ مُسْتَقِيمٌ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٦١] .

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ ابْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى خَطَأٌ كَبِيرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ الْآيَةَ إِنَّمَا نَزَلَتْ خِطَابًا لِأَهْلِ مَكَّةَ فِي عِبَادَتِهِمُ الْأَصْنَامَ الَّتِي هِيَ جَمَادٌ لَا تَعْقِلُ، لِيَكُونَ ذَلِكَ تَقْرِيعًا وَتَوْبِيخًا لِعَابِدِيهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّكُمْ وَمَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَصَبُ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ فَكَيْفَ يُورِدُ عَلَى هَذَا الْمَسِيحَ وَالْعُزَيْرَ وَنَحْوَهُمَا، مِمَّنْ لَهُ عَمَلٌ صَالِحٌ، وَلَمْ يَرْضَ بِعِبَادَةِ مَنْ عَبَدَهُ. وعَوّل ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ فِي الْجَوَابِ عَلَى أَنَّ "مَا" لِمَا لَا يَعْقِلُ عِنْدَ الْعَرَبِ.

وَقَدْ أَسْلَمَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزِّبَعْرَى بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، وَكَانَ مِنَ الشُّعَرَاءِ الْمَشْهُورِينَ. وَكَانَ يُهَاجِي الْمُسْلِمِينَ أَوَّلًا ثُمَّ قَالَ مُعْتَذِرًا:

يَا رَسُولَ الْمَلِيكِ، إِنَّ لِسَانِي ... رَاتقٌ مَا فتَقْتُ إذْ أنَا بُورُ ...

إذْ أجَاري الشَّيطَانَ فِي سَنَن الغَي ... وَمَنْ مَالَ مَيْلَه مَثْبُور 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا يَحْزُنُهُمُ الْفَزَعُ الأكْبَرُ﴾ قِيلَ الْمُرَادُ بِذَلِكَ الْمَوْتُ. رَوَاهُ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ عَنْ عَطَاءٍ.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِالْفَزَعِ الْأَكْبَرِ: النَّفْخَةُ فِي الصُّورِ. قَالَهُ العَوْفي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبُو سِنَان سَعِيدُ ابن سِنَانٍ الشَّيْبَانِيُّ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ.

وَقِيلَ: حِينَ يُؤْمَر بِالْعَبْدِ إِلَى النَّارِ. قَالَهُ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ.

وَقِيلَ: حِينَ تُطبق النَّارُ عَلَى أَهْلِهَا. قَالَهُ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر، وَابْنُ جُرَيج.

وَقِيلَ: حِينَ يُذبَح الْمَوْتُ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ. قَالَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْهُذَلِيُّ ، فِيمَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَتَلَقَّاهُمُ الْمَلائِكَةُ هَذَا يَوْمُكُمُ الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ تُوعَدُونَ﴾ ، يَعْنِي: تَقُولُ لَهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ، تُبَشِّرُهُمْ يَوْمَ مَعَادِهِمْ إِذَا خَرَجُوا مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ: ﴿هَذَا يَوْمُكُمُ الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ تُوعَدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قابلوا ما يسركم.

---

## 21:104 — verse 104

### Translation

The Almighty says: this will occur on the Day of Resurrection, {The day when We shall roll up the heaven like the rolling up of the sijill for writings}, as He, the Exalted, said: {And they did not accord Allah His due estimation, when the whole earth will be in His grip on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be rolled up in His right hand. Exalted is He and high above what they associate with Him} [al-Zumar: 67]. Al-Bukhari said:

[chain] Ibn Umar, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "Indeed Allah will grasp the earths on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be in His right hand."

Al-Bukhari, may Allah have mercy on him, related this alone from this route.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: Allah will roll up the seven heavens with the creation in them, and the seven earths with the creation in them, rolling all of that up in His right hand, and all of that will be in His hand like the size of a mustard seed.

Concerning His saying: {like the rolling up of the sijill for writings}, it has been said that what is meant by sijill is the written record. And it has also been said that what is meant by sijill here is an angel among the angels.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Umar, regarding the saying of the Almighty: {The day when We shall roll up the heaven like the rolling up of the sijill for writings}, said: the sijill is an angel; when it ascends with the seeking of forgiveness, it is said: "Write it as light."

Ibn Jarir related this likewise, [chain] from Ibn Yaman, with the same wording.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: it has also been related from Abu Ja'far Muhammad ibn Ali ibn al-Husayn that the sijill is an angel.

Al-Suddi said concerning this verse: the sijill is an angel entrusted with the scrolls; when a person dies, his record is raised up to the sijill, who rolls it up and raises it until the Day of Resurrection.

It has also been said that what is meant by it is the name of a Companion who used to write down the revelation for the Prophet ﷺ. Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas, regarding {The day when We shall roll up the heaven like the rolling up of the sijill for writings}, said: the sijill is the man.

Nuh said: Yazid ibn Ka'b, who is al-Awdhi, informed me, [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: the sijill is a scribe of the Prophet ﷺ.

Abu Dawud and al-Nasa'i related this likewise, [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: the sijill is a scribe of the Prophet ﷺ.

Ibn Jarir related it [chain] from Nasr ibn Ali al-Jahdami, as mentioned before. Ibn Adi related it through the route of Yahya ibn Amr ibn Malik al-Nukri, from his father, from Abu al-Jawza, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Prophet ﷺ had a scribe called al-Sijill, and this is the meaning of His saying: {The day when We shall roll up the heaven like the rolling up of the sijill for writings}, meaning: just as the sijill rolls up the writing, so too will We roll up the heaven. Then he said: this is not preserved (not authentically transmitted).

Al-Khatib al-Baghdadi said in his History: [chain] Ibn Umar said: al-sijill is a scribe of the Prophet ﷺ.

This is extremely objectionable (munkar) as a report of Nafi' from Ibn Umar; it is not sound at all. Likewise what was mentioned earlier from Ibn Abbas, through the route of Abu Dawud and others, is also not sound. A group of the hadith masters have explicitly declared it fabricated, even though it appears in the Sunan of Abu Dawud, among them our teacher, the great hadith master Abu al-Hajjaj al-Mizzi, may Allah lengthen his life, extend his term, and seal it with righteous deeds. I have devoted a separate treatise to this hadith alone, and praise be to Allah. The Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir undertook to refute this hadith and rejected it most thoroughly, saying: no one among the Companions is known by the name al-Sijill, and the scribes of the Prophet ﷺ are well known, and none of them bears the name al-Sijill. He, may Allah have mercy on him, spoke truly in this, and it is among the strongest proofs of the objectionable nature of this hadith. As for those who mentioned this name among the names of the Companions, they relied only on this hadith and nothing else. And Allah knows best.

The sound view from Ibn Abbas is that al-sijill is the scroll (record), as reported by Ali ibn Abi Talha and al-Awfi from him. Mujahid, Qatada, and more than one other stated this explicitly. Ibn Jarir preferred it, since it is what is known in the language. On this basis, the meaning of the statement {The day when We shall roll up the heaven like the rolling up of the sijill for writings} would be: over this writing, meaning the thing written, similar to His saying: {And when they had both submitted, and he laid him down upon his forehead (talla-hu lil-jabin)} [al-Saffat: 103], meaning: upon the forehead. This has parallels in the language. And Allah knows best.

Concerning His saying: {As We began the first creation, We will repeat it. A promise binding upon Us. Indeed, We were to do it}, meaning: this will inevitably occur, the day when Allah brings the creation back into being anew, just as He originated them the first time; He who is able to originate them is able to bring them back. That is bound to happen, for it is among the totality of Allah's promise, which is never broken nor altered, and He is able to do that. Hence He said: {Indeed, We were to do it}.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood among us delivering an exhortation and said: "You will be gathered to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, barefoot, naked, and uncircumcised: {As We began the first creation, We will repeat it. A promise binding upon Us. Indeed, We were to do it}." And he mentioned the rest of the hadith. Both of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) related it in their Sahihs from the hadith of Shu'ba, and al-Bukhari related it under this verse in his book.

Layth ibn Abi Sulaym related, from Mujahid, from Aisha, from the Prophet ﷺ, something similar to that.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {As We began the first creation, We will repeat it}, that he said: We will destroy everything, just as it was the first time.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: هَذَا كَائِنٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿يَوْمَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ وَالأرْضُ جَمِيعًا قَبْضَتُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَالسَّماوَاتُ مَطْوِيَّاتٌ بِيَمِينِهِ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٦٧] وَقَدْ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُقَدم بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنِي عَمِّي الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ يَحْيَى، عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبِضُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ الأرضَين، وَتَكُونُ السموات بِيَمِينِهِ" .

انْفَرَدَ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ الْحَجَّاجِ الرَّقِّي، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي الْوَاصِلِ ، عَنِ أَبِي الْمَلِيحِ الْأَزْدِيِّ ، عَنِ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ الْأَزْدِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: يَطْوِي الله السموات السَّبْعَ بِمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْخَلِيقَةِ وَالْأَرْضِينَ السَّبْعَ بِمَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْخَلِيقَةِ، يَطْوِي ذَلِكَ كُلَّهُ بِيَمِينِهِ، يَكُونُ ذَلِكَ كُلُّهُ فِي يَدِهِ بِمَنْزِلَةِ خَرْدَلَةٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ ، قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِالسِّجِلِّ [الْكِتَابُ. وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِالسِّجِلِّ] هَاهُنَا: مَلَك مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْعَلَاءِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ يَمَانٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْوَفَاءِ الْأَشْجَعِيُّ، عَنِ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ ، قَالَ: السِّجِلُّ: مَلَك، فَإِذَا صَعِدَ بِالِاسْتِغْفَارِ قَالَ: اكْتُبْهَا نُورًا.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي كُرَيْب، عَنِ ابْنِ يَمَانٍ، بِهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: وَرُوِيَ عَنْ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ أَنَّ السِّجِلَّ مَلَكٌ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: السِّجِلُّ: مَلَك مُوَكَّلٌ بِالصُّحُفِ، فَإِذَا مَاتَ الْإِنْسَانُ رُفِعَ كتابُه إِلَى السِّجِلِّ فَطَوَاهُ، وَرَفَعَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِهِ اسْمُ رَجُلٍ صِحَابِيٍّ، كَانَ يَكْتُبُ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ الْوَحْيَ: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعة، حَدَّثَنَا نَصْرُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ الجَهْضَميّ، حَدَّثَنَا نُوحُ بْنُ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ، عَنِ ابن عباس: [ ﴿يَوْمَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ ] ، قَالَ: السجل: هو الرجل.

قَالَ نُوحٌ: وَأَخْبَرَنِي يَزِيدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ -هُوَ العَوْذي-عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: السِّجِلُّ كَاتِبٌ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ عَنْ قُتَيْبَةَ بْنِ سَعِيدٍ ، عَنْ نُوحِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ كَعْبٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، قَالَ: السِّجِلُّ كَاتِبٌ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ .

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ نَصْرِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ الْجَهْضَمِيِّ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ عَدِيٍّ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ يَحْيَى بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ مَالِكٍ النُّكْريّ عَنِ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ أَبِي الْجَوْزَاءِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ كَاتِبٌ يُسَمَّى السِّجِلَّ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ ، قَالَ: كَمَا يَطْوِي السِّجِلُّ الْكِتَابَ، كَذَلِكَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: وَهُوَ غَيْرُ مَحْفُوظٍ .

وَقَالَ الْخَطِيبُ الْبَغْدَادِيُّ فِي تَارِيخِهِ: أَنْبَأَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ البَرْقَاني، أَنْبَأَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ يَعْقُوبَ الْحَجَّاجِيُّ، أَنْبَأَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ الْكَرْخِيُّ، أَنَّ حَمْدَانَ بْنَ سَعِيدٍ حَدَّثَهُمْ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ نُمَيْرٍ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، قَالَ: السِّجِلُّ: كَاتِبٌ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ .

وَهَذَا مُنْكَرٌ جِدًّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ نَافِعٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، لَا يَصِحُّ أَصْلًا وَكَذَلِكَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، مِنْ رِوَايَةِ أَبِي دَاوُدَ وَغَيْرِهِ، لَا يَصِحُّ أَيْضًا. وَقَدْ صَرَّحَ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْحُفَّاظِ بِوَضْعِهِ -وَإِنْ كَانَ فِي سُنَنِ أَبِي دَاوُدَ-مِنْهُمْ شَيْخُنَا الْحَافِظُ الْكَبِيرُ أَبُو الْحَجَّاجِ المِزِّي، فَسَح اللَّهُ فِي عُمْرِهِ، ونَسَأ فِي أَجَلِهِ، وَخَتَمَ لَهُ بِصَالِحِ عَمَلِهِ، وَقَدْ أَفْرَدَتُ لِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ جُزْءًا عَلَى حِدَةٍ ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ. وَقَدْ تَصَدَّى الْإِمَامُ أبو جعفر بن جَرِيرٍ لِلْإِنْكَارِ عَلَى هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، وَرَدَّهُ أَتَمَّ رَدٍّ، وَقَالَ: لَا يُعَرف فِي الصَّحَابَةِ أَحَدٌ اسْمُهُ السجِل، وكُتَّاب النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مَعْرُوفُونَ، وَلَيْسَ فِيهِمْ أَحَدٌ اسْمُهُ السِّجِلُّ، وصَدَق رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَهُوَ مِنْ أَقْوَى الْأَدِلَّةِ عَلَى نَكَارة هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ. وَأَمَّا مَنْ ذَكَرَ فِي أَسْمَاءِ الصَّحَابَةِ هَذَا، فَإِنَّمَا اعْتَمَدَ عَلَى هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، لَا عَلَى غَيْرِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَالصَّحِيحُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّ السِّجِلَّ هِيَ الصَّحِيفَةُ، قَالَهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ وَالْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنْهُ. وَنَصَّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ؛ لِأَنَّهُ الْمَعْرُوفُ فِي اللُّغَةِ، فَعَلَى هَذَا يَكُونُ مَعْنَى الْكَلَامِ: ﴿يَوْمَ نَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ كَطَيِّ السِّجِلِّ لِلْكُتُبِ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى [هَذَا] الْكِتَابِ، بِمَعْنَى الْمَكْتُوبِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَلَمَّا أَسْلَمَا وَتَلَّهُ لِلْجَبِينِ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:١٠٣] ، أَيْ: عَلَى الْجَبِينِ، وَلَهُ نَظَائِرُ فِي اللُّغَةِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَمَا بَدَأْنَا أَوَّلَ خَلْقٍ نُعِيدُهُ وَعْدًا عَلَيْنَا إِنَّا كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ﴾ يَعْنِي: هَذَا كَائِنٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ، يَوْمَ يُعِيدُ اللَّهُ الْخَلَائِقَ خَلْقًا جَدِيدًا، كَمَا بَدَأَهُمْ هُوَ الْقَادِرُ عَلَى إِعَادَتِهِمْ ، وذلك واجب الوقوع، لأنه من جُمْلَةِ وَعْدِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي لَا يُخْلَفُ وَلَا يُبَدَّلُ، وَهُوَ الْقَادِرُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّا كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع وَابْنُ جَعْفَرٍ الْمَعْنَى ، قَالَا : حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ بْنِ النُّعْمَانِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَامَ فِينَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِمَوْعِظَةٍ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّكُمْ مَحْشُورُونَ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ حُفَاةً عُرَاةً غُرْلا كَمَا بَدَأْنَا أَوَّلَ خَلْقٍ نُعِيدُهُ، وَعْدًا عَلَيْنَا إِنَّا كُنَّا فَاعِلِينَ"؛ وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ، أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ. وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عِنْدَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ فِي كِتَابِهِ .

وَقَدْ رَوَى لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، نَحْوَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿كَمَا بَدَأْنَا أَوَّلَ خَلْقٍ نُعِيدُهُ﴾ قَالَ: نُهْلِكُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، كَمَا كَانَ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ.

---

## 21:105-107 — verses 105-107 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about what He has decreed and ordained for His righteous servants of happiness in this world and the next, and inheritance of the earth in this world and the next, as in His saying, the Exalted: {Indeed the earth belongs to Allah; He gives it as an inheritance to whom He wills among His servants, and the final outcome is for the righteous} [al-A'raf: 128]. And He said: {Indeed We shall surely help Our messengers and those who believe in the life of this world and on the Day when the witnesses will stand} [Ghafir: 51]. And He said: {Allah has promised those among you who believe and do righteous deeds that He will surely make them successors in the earth, just as He made those before them successors, and He will surely establish for them their religion which He has approved for them, [and He will surely change their state, after their fear, to security]}, the verse [al-Nur: 55]. And He, the Exalted, informed that this is written and inscribed in the scriptural books of law and in the books of decree, and that it is bound to occur without fail. Therefore the Exalted said: {And We have already written in the Zabur, after the Reminder}. Al-A'mash said: I asked Sa'id ibn Jubayr about His saying, the Exalted, {And We have already written in the Zabur, after the Reminder}, and he said: the Zabur is the Torah, the Gospel, and the Qur'an.

Mujahid said: the Zabur is "the Book."

Ibn Abbas, al-Sha'bi, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and others said: the Zabur is that which was sent down upon David (peace be upon him), and the Reminder is the Torah. And from Ibn Abbas: the Zabur is the Qur'an.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: the Reminder is that which is in heaven.

Mujahid said: the Zabur is the books that came after the Reminder, and the Reminder is the Mother of the Book with Allah.

Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, preferred this view. Likewise Zayd ibn Aslam said: it is the first Book. Al-Thawri said: it is the Preserved Tablet. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: the Zabur is the books that were sent down upon the prophets, and the Reminder is the Mother of the Book in which things were written before that.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: Allah, glorified is He, informed in the Torah, the Zabur, and in His prior knowledge, before the heavens and the earth existed, that He would make the nation of Muhammad ﷺ inherit the earth and admit them into Paradise, and they are the righteous.

Mujahid reported from Ibn Abbas concerning {that the earth is inherited by My righteous servants}: he said, it means the land of Paradise. Likewise said Abu al-Aliyah, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Sha'bi, Qatadah, al-Suddi, Abu Salih, al-Rabi' ibn Anas, and al-Thawri, may Allah the Exalted have mercy on them all.

His saying: {Indeed in this is a sufficient message for a people who worship}, meaning: indeed in this Qur'an which We sent down upon Our servant Muhammad ﷺ is a sufficient message, a benefit and sufficiency, for a worshipping people, and they are those who worshipped Allah by means of what He legislated, loved, and was pleased with, and who preferred obedience to Allah over obedience to Satan and the desires of their own souls.

His saying, the Exalted: {And We have not sent you except as a mercy to the worlds}: the Exalted informs that Allah made Muhammad ﷺ a mercy to the worlds, meaning He sent him as a mercy to all of them. Whoever accepts this mercy and is grateful for this blessing attains happiness in this world and the next, and whoever rejects it and denies it suffers loss in this world and the next, as the Exalted said: {Have you not seen those who exchanged the favor of Allah for disbelief and led their people down to the house of ruin, Hell, wherein they will burn, and what a wretched settlement it is} [Ibrahim: 28-29]. And Allah, the Exalted, said describing the Qur'an: {Say, it is for those who believe a guidance and a healing, but as for those who do not believe, there is deafness in their ears, and it is blindness upon them. Those are being called from a distant place} [Fussilat: 44].

Muslim said in his Sahih: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: it was said, "O Messenger of Allah, invoke a curse upon the polytheists," and he said, "I have not been sent as one who curses; rather I have been sent as a mercy." Muslim alone reported this.

And in another hadith: "I am but a mercy that is given as a gift." Narrated by Abd Allah ibn Abi Arabah and others, [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, raised to the Prophet ﷺ. Ibrahim al-Harbi said: others narrated it from Waki' without mentioning Abu Hurayrah. Al-Bukhari said likewise; he was asked about this hadith and said: it was found with Hafs ibn Ghiyath as a mursal (report with the Companion link omitted).

The Hafiz Ibn Asakir said: Malik ibn Su'ayr ibn al-Khims narrated it [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, raised to the Prophet. Then he traced it through the route of Abu Bakr ibn al-Muqri' and Abu Ahmad al-Hakim, both from Bakr ibn Muhammad ibn Ibrahim al-Sufi: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I am but a mercy that is given as a gift."

Then he brought it by the route of al-Salt ibn Mas'ud, [chain] from Ibn Umar, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Indeed Allah sent me as a mercy given as a gift; I was sent to raise up some people and bring down others."

Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] Ahmad ibn Salih said: I found a book in Madinah from Abd al-Aziz al-Darawardi and Ibrahim ibn Muhammad ibn Abd al-Aziz ibn Umar ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Awf, [chain] from Muhammad ibn Jubayr ibn Mut'im, from his father, who said: Abu Jahl said, when he returned to Mecca from his encounter concerning Hamzah: "O assembly of Quraysh, indeed Muhammad has settled in Yathrib and sent out his scouts, and he only wants to strike at some of you, so beware of passing along his path or drawing near him, for he is like a ravening lion. He is furious with you because you drove him out the way ticks are driven off the pads of camels' feet. By Allah, he indeed has sorcery; I have never seen him nor any of his companions without seeing Satan with them. And you well know the enmity of the two sons of Qaylah," meaning al-Aws and al-Khazraj, "he is an enemy who has sought help from an enemy." Mut'im ibn Adiy said to him: "O Abu al-Hakam, by Allah, I have never seen anyone more truthful in speech nor more faithful to his promise than your brother whom you have driven out. Since you have done what you have done, be the most restrained of people toward him." Abu Sufyan ibn al-Harith said: "Be as harsh as you have been toward him. Indeed, if the two sons of Qaylah overpower you, they will observe neither kinship nor covenant with you. If you obey me, you will drive them into the worst of straits, or you will expel Muhammad from among them, so that he becomes solitary and outcast. As for the two sons of Qaylah, by Allah, they and the people of Dahlak are equal in abasement, and I will handle their sharpness for you." And he said [poetry]:

I shall grant a portion of myself, harsh,
regardless of what has been of nearness or distance,
The men of Khazraj are people of abasement,
whenever seriousness turns to jest.

This reached the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and he said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, I shall surely kill them and crucify them and guide them, even though they are averse to it. Indeed I am a mercy that Allah has sent me as, and He will not take my soul until Allah makes His religion manifest. I have five names: I am Muhammad, and Ahmad, and I am al-Mahi (the Effacer) by whom Allah effaces disbelief, and I am al-Hashir (the Gatherer), by whose footsteps people will be gathered, and I am al-Aqib (the Last)."

Ahmad ibn Salih said: I hope that this hadith is sound.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Amr ibn Abi Qurrah al-Kindi said: Hudhayfah was in al-Mada'in, and he used to relate things that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ had said.
